

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/CarModGUI.lua ---

--[[
    CarModGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Car PaintGUI
-- Khizzer
-- August 31, 2021

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local CarPaintGUI = {}

local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm);
local clientComm = Comm.ClientComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, false, 'BusinessLogos');
local businessLogoProperty = clientComm:GetProperty('CarBusinessLogos');

type BusinessLogoData = {
    GroupID: number,
    MinimumRank: number,
    LogoID: number
}

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local PlayerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui;
local carPaintGUI = PlayerGUI:WaitForChild('CarPaintGUI');
local mainFrame = carPaintGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local colourFrame = bodyFrame.ColourFrame;
local plateFrame = bodyFrame.PlateFrame;
local businessLogoFrame = bodyFrame.BusinessLogoFrame;

local tipsLabel = bodyFrame.TipsLabel;

local buyBtn = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local sidebarImage = bodyFrame.SidebarImage;
local sidebarBtnList = sidebarImage.SidebarScrollingFrame;
local licensePlateBtn = sidebarBtnList.PlateBtn;
local paintBtn =  sidebarBtnList.PaintBtn;
local businessLogoBtn = sidebarBtnList.BusinessLogoBtn;

local colourWheel = colourFrame.ColourWheel;
local colourPreview = colourFrame.ColourPreview;
local darknessSlider = colourFrame.DarknessSlider;
local slider = darknessSlider.Slider;

local plateBoxImage = plateFrame.PlateBoxImage;
local plateBox = plateBoxImage.PlateBox;
local newPlateLabel = plateFrame.NewPlateLabel;
local carModelLabel = plateFrame.CarModelLabel;
local oldPlateLabel = plateFrame.OldPlateLabel;

local businessLogoScrollingFrame = businessLogoFrame.LogoScrollingFrame;
local removeLogoBtn = btnsFrame.RemoveBtn;

local prefabs = carPaintGUI.Prefabs;
local logoPrefab = prefabs.LogoPrefab;



local MAX_PLATE_LENGTH = 6;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local selectedBusinessLogo;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local PAINT_TIP = 'Use the colour wheel to select a desired colour, then press \'Buy\'.'
local PLATE_TIP = "Enter your desired license plate in the box, then press submit!"

local mathMin = math.min;
local stringLen = string.len;

local function toPolar(v: Vector2): (number, number)
	return math.atan2(v.Y, v.X), v.Magnitude;
end

local function radToDeg(x)
	return ((x + math.pi) / (2 * math.pi)) * 360;
end

local hue, saturation, value = 0, 0, 1;

local NetworkController;
local MainListeners;
local SidebarListeners;
local ListenerList;

local selectedBtn;
local selectedBusinessLogo;

local function UpdateSelector(mouseX, mouseY)
    local radius = colourWheel.AbsoluteSize.x/2;
    local d = Vector2.new(mouseX, mouseY) - colourWheel.AbsolutePosition - colourWheel.AbsoluteSize/2;

    if (d:Dot(d) > radius*radius) then
		d = d.unit * radius;
	end

	colourWheel.Selector.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, d.x, 0.5, d.y);

	local phi, len = toPolar(d * Vector2.new(1, -1));
	hue, saturation = radToDeg(phi)/360, len / radius;
	darknessSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, 1);

	colourPreview.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, value);
end;

local function UpdateSlider(mouseX, mouseY)
    local rY = mouseY - darknessSlider.AbsolutePosition.y;
	local cY = math.clamp(rY, 0, darknessSlider.AbsoluteSize.y - slider.AbsoluteSize.y);
	slider.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, cY);

	value = 1 - (cY / (darknessSlider.AbsoluteSize.y - slider.AbsoluteSize.y));

    colourPreview.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, value);
end

function CarPaintGUI.IsEnabled()
    return carPaintGUI.Enabled;
end;

function CarPaintGUI.Enable()
    carPaintGUI.Enabled = true
    openTween:Play();
    openTween.Completed:Wait();

    SidebarListeners = ListenerList.new();
    MainListeners = ListenerList.new();

    local paintHoverTween = TweenService:Create(paintBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local paintHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(paintBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local paintSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(paintBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

    local plateHoverTween = TweenService:Create(licensePlateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local plateHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(licensePlateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local plateSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(licensePlateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

    local businessLogoHoverTween = TweenService:Create(businessLogoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local businessLogoHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(businessLogoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local businessLogoSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(businessLogoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});


    SidebarListeners:Connect(paintBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= paintBtn then
            paintHoverTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(paintBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= paintBtn then
            paintHoverEndTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(paintBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if MainListeners then MainListeners:DisconnectAll(); end;

        businessLogoFrame.Visible = false;
        removeLogoBtn.Visible = false;

        if selectedBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        colourFrame.Visible = true;
        plateFrame.Visible = false;


        selectedBtn = paintBtn;
        paintSelectedTween:Play();

        local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService");
        local Mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse();

        local WheelDown = false;
        local SliderDown = false;

        MainListeners:Connect(UserInputService.InputEnded, function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                WheelDown = false;
                SliderDown = false;
            end;
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(colourWheel.MouseButton1Down, function()
            WheelDown = true;
            UpdateSelector(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(colourWheel.MouseMoved, function()
            if WheelDown then
                UpdateSelector(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
            end;
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(darknessSlider.MouseButton1Down, function()
            SliderDown = true;
            UpdateSlider(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(darknessSlider.MouseMoved, function()
            if SliderDown then
                UpdateSlider(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
            end;
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(buyBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            NetworkController.Send('PaintCar', colourPreview.ImageColor3);
        end);
    end);

    SidebarListeners:Connect(licensePlateBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= licensePlateBtn then
            plateHoverTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(licensePlateBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= licensePlateBtn then
            plateHoverEndTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(licensePlateBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if MainListeners then MainListeners:DisconnectAll(); end;

        businessLogoFrame.Visible = false;
        removeLogoBtn.Visible = false;

        local car = Players.LocalPlayer.Car.Value;
        if not car then return; end;

        if selectedBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        selectedBtn = licensePlateBtn;
        plateSelectedTween:Play();

        colourFrame.Visible = false;
        plateFrame.Visible = true;

        carModelLabel.Text = 'Car Model: '..car.Name;
        oldPlateLabel.Text = 'License Plate: '..car.Body.LicensePlate.LicensePlateGUI.LicensePlateLabel.Text;

        MainListeners:Connect(plateBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'), function()
            local text = plateBox.Text;
            plateBox.Text = string.upper(text:sub(1, MAX_PLATE_LENGTH):gsub('%p+', ''):gsub('%s+', '')); --Restrict to letters only!
            newPlateLabel.Text = string.upper(text .. ('-'):rep(mathMin(MAX_PLATE_LENGTH - #text, MAX_PLATE_LENGTH)));
        end)

        MainListeners:Connect(buyBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            if stringLen(plateBox.Text) ~= 6 then return; end;
            NetworkController.Send('EditLicensePlate', plateBox.Text);
        end);
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(businessLogoBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= businessLogoBtn then
            businessLogoHoverTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(businessLogoBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedBtn ~= businessLogoBtn then
            businessLogoHoverEndTween:Play();
        end;
    end)

    SidebarListeners:Connect(businessLogoBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if MainListeners then MainListeners:DisconnectAll(); end;

        local car = localPlayer.Car.Value;

        if not car.Config:GetAttribute('CanHaveBusinessLogo') then return _G.AeroError('This car cannot have a business logo.'); end;

        businessLogoFrame.Visible = true;
        removeLogoBtn.Visible = true;
        colourFrame.Visible = false;
        plateFrame.Visible = false;

        if selectedBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        selectedBtn = businessLogoBtn;
        businessLogoSelectedTween:Play();

        MainListeners:Connect(removeLogoBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            NetworkController.Send('AddBusinessLogo', 'None');
        end)

        for _,v in next, businessLogoScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        local logos = businessLogoProperty:Get();

        for i: string, v: BusinessLogoData in next, logos do
            -- skip logos if we're not authorised to see them
            if localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(v.GroupID) < v.MinimumRank and localPlayer:GetAttribute("Developer") ~= true then
                continue
            end

            local logoBtn = logoPrefab:Clone();
            logoBtn.Logo.Image = `https://www.roblox.com/Thumbs/Asset.ashx?width=420&height=420&assetId={v.LogoID}`;
            logoBtn:FindFirstChild('Name').Text = i;
            logoBtn.Parent = businessLogoScrollingFrame;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(logoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(logoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(logoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            MainListeners:Connect(logoBtn.MouseEnter, function()
                if selectedBusinessLogo == logoBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            MainListeners:Connect(logoBtn.MouseLeave, function()
                if selectedBusinessLogo == logoBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            MainListeners:Connect(logoBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
                if selectedBusinessLogo then
                    TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                end

                selectedBusinessLogo = logoBtn;
                selectedTween:Play();

                NetworkController.Send('AddBusinessLogo', i);
            end);
        end;
    end)
end;

function CarPaintGUI.Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    carPaintGUI.Enabled = false;

    MainListeners:DisconnectAll();
    SidebarListeners:DisconnectAll();
end

function CarPaintGUI:Start()
    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(self.Disable)
end;

function CarPaintGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
end;


return CarPaintGUI

--[[

-- Car RadioGUI
-- Khizzer
-- February 24, 2022

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local carRadioGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('CarRadioGUI');
local mainFrame = carRadioGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local soundIdFrame = bodyFrame.SoundIdFrame;
local soundIdBox = soundIdFrame.SoundIdBox;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local playBtn = btnsFrame.PlayBtn;
local stopBtn = btnsFrame.StopBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local GuiListeners;
local Error;
local NetworkController;
local ListenerList;
local CarGUI;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local CarRadioGUI = {}

function CarRadioGUI.Toggle()
    if carRadioGUI.Enabled then
        GuiListeners:DisconnectAll();
        closeTween:Play();
        closeTween.Completed:Wait();
        carRadioGUI.Enabled = false;
    else
        carRadioGUI.Enabled = true;
        openTween:Play();
        GuiListeners:Connect(playBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            if #soundIdBox.Text < 5 then
                Error('Valid ID not found');
            end;
            NetworkController.Send('CAR_RADIO', 'PLAY' , soundIdBox.Text);
            CarRadioGUI.Toggle();
        end)

        GuiListeners:Connect(stopBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            CarRadioGUI.Toggle();
            NetworkController.Send('CAR_RADIO', 'STOP')
        end);

        GuiListeners:Connect(exitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            CarRadioGUI.Toggle();
        end)
    end;
end;

function CarRadioGUI:Start()
    GuiListeners = ListenerList.new();
end;
function CarRadioGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    CarGUI = self.Controllers.Car.CarGUI;
end


return CarRadioGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/CellControlGUI.lua ---

--[[
    CellControlGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Cell ControlGUI
-- Khizzer
-- February 2, 2022



local CellControlGUI = {}
local NetworkController;
local ListenerList;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local cellControlGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('CellControlGUI');
local mainFrame = cellControlGUI.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;

local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local cellsImage = bodyFrame.CellsImage;
local cellsListScrollingFrame = cellsImage.CellsListScrollingFrame;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local components = cellControlGUI.Components;
local CellBtnPreFab = components.CellBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local cellsListenerList;

function CellControlGUI:Enable()
    local cellModels = workspace.PrisonCells;

    cellsListenerList:DisconnectAll();

    cellControlGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    for _,v in next, cellsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    local cellModelChildren = cellModels:GetChildren();
    
    table.sort(cellModelChildren, function(a, b)
        local cellNumberA = a.Name:sub(2, -1);
        local cellNumberB = b.Name:sub(2, -1);

        return cellNumberA < cellNumberB;
    end);


    for _,v in next, cellModelChildren do
        local cellName = v.Name;
        local cellBtn = CellBtnPreFab:Clone();
        cellBtn.CellLabel.Text = cellName;
        cellBtn.Parent = cellsListScrollingFrame;
        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(cellBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(cellBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(cellBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        if v.Main:GetAttribute('Opened') == true then
            cellBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
        
        cellsListenerList:Connect(cellBtn.MouseEnter, function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Opened') == true and cellBtn.ImageColor3 ~= SELECTED_BTN_COLOR then
                cellBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
            end;

            if v:GetAttribute('Opened') == true then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);
        
        cellsListenerList:Connect(cellBtn.MouseLeave, function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Opened') == true then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);
        
        cellsListenerList:Connect(cellBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            NetworkController.Send('PrisonCell', cellName);
            if v:GetAttribute('Opened') == false then --hacky and unreliable
                selectedTween:Play();
            else
                TweenService:Create(cellBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            end;
        end);
    end
end

function CellControlGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    cellsListenerList:DisconnectAll();
    for _,v in next, cellsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    cellControlGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function CellControlGUI.IsEnabled()
    return cellControlGUI.Enabled;
end

function CellControlGUI:Start()
    cellsListenerList = ListenerList.new();
    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(CellControlGUI.Disable)

    self.Modules.UI.Draggable.new(cellControlGUI, topBarFrame, mainFrame)
end;

function CellControlGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
end


return CellControlGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/CitationGUI.lua ---

--[[
    CitationGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- CitationGUI
-- oSudden
-- November 26, 2021

local CitationGUI = {};
local NetworkController;
local PlayerGui;
local TweenService;
local CanTween;
local ClosedPosition;
local OpenPosition;
local Maid;
local CurrentMaid;
local CitationsModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CitationsModule'));

local focusConnection;
local focusLostConnection;
local searchConnection;


function GetSelectionText(CitationsTable)
	local Formatted = ""
	for i,v in pairs(CitationsTable) do
		if v then
			if #Formatted < 1 then
				Formatted = i
			else
				Formatted = Formatted..", "..i
			end
		end
	end
	return "Selected Offences: "..Formatted
end

function GetSelectionPrice(CitationsTable)
	local Price = 0
	for i,v in pairs(CitationsTable) do
		if v then
			for citation, amount in pairs(CitationsModule) do
				if citation == i then
					Price += amount;
				end
			end
		end
	end
	return "Total Citation Amount: $"..tostring(Price or 0)
end

function CitationGUI:Enable(Target : Player)
	if Target then
		local citationGUI = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("CitationGUI")
		local mainFrame = citationGUI:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
		local bodyFrame = mainFrame:WaitForChild("BodyFrame")
		local btnsFrame = bodyFrame:WaitForChild("BtnsFrame")

		local crimesBtnImage = bodyFrame.CitationFrame.CrimesBtnImage;
		local crimesBtnBox = crimesBtnImage.CrimesBox;
		local crimesList = crimesBtnImage.crimesImage.crimesScrollingFrame

		local SelectedCitations = {}

		local components = citationGUI:WaitForChild("Components")


		CurrentMaid = Maid.new();
		
		bodyFrame.CitationFrame.UsernameLabel.Text = "Username: "..Target.Name
		
		mainFrame.Visible = true
		local Tween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0), {Position = OpenPosition})
		Tween:Play()
		
		for _, UI in pairs(bodyFrame.CitationFrame.CrimesBtnImage.crimesImage.crimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
			if UI:IsA("ImageButton") then
				UI:Destroy()
			end
		end

		if not focusConnection then 
			focusConnection = crimesBtnBox.Focused:Connect(function()
				if not crimesBtnImage.crimesImage.Visible then
					crimesBtnImage.crimesImage.Visible = true;
				else
					crimesBtnImage.crimesImage.Visible = false;
				end;
	
				if not searchConnection then
					searchConnection = crimesBtnBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'):Connect(function()
						for _,v in next, crimesList:GetChildren() do
							if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
								v.Visible = false;
								if string.find((v.Name):lower(), (crimesBtnBox.Text):lower()) then
									v.Visible = true;
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end);
				end;
			end);
		end;

		if not focusLostConnection then
			focusLostConnection = crimesBtnBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
				task.wait(0.5);
				crimesBtnImage.crimesImage.Visible = false;
	
				if searchConnection then
					searchConnection:Disconnect();
					searchConnection = nil;
				end
			end)
		end

		for citation, amount in CitationsModule do
			local Item = components.CrimeBtn:Clone()
			if citation ~= nil then
				Item.CrimeLabel.Text = citation;
				Item.Name = citation;
				Item.Parent = bodyFrame.CitationFrame.CrimesBtnImage.crimesImage.crimesScrollingFrame;

				CurrentMaid:GiveTask(Item.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
					if not SelectedCitations[citation] then
						local Tween = TweenService:Create(Item, TweenInfo.new(0.07, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)})
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
				end))

				CurrentMaid:GiveTask(Item.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
					if not SelectedCitations[citation] then
						local Tween = TweenService:Create(Item, TweenInfo.new(0.07, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)})
						Tween:Play()
						Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
							Tween:Destroy()
						end)
					end
				end))
				
				CurrentMaid:GiveTask(Item.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
					if #SelectedCitations < 3 then
						if not SelectedCitations[citation] then
							SelectedCitations[citation] = true
							local Tween = TweenService:Create(Item, TweenInfo.new(0.07, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159)})
							Tween:Play()
							Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
								Tween:Destroy()
							end)
							bodyFrame.CitationFrame.SelectedOffencesLabel.Text = GetSelectionText(SelectedCitations)
							bodyFrame.CitationFrame.TotalCitationLabel.Text = GetSelectionPrice(SelectedCitations)
							print(SelectedCitations)
						else
							SelectedCitations[citation] = nil
							local Tween = TweenService:Create(Item, TweenInfo.new(0.07, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)})
							Tween:Play()
							Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
								Tween:Destroy()
							end)
							bodyFrame.CitationFrame.SelectedOffencesLabel.Text = GetSelectionText(SelectedCitations)
							bodyFrame.CitationFrame.TotalCitationLabel.Text = GetSelectionPrice(SelectedCitations)
						end
					end
				end))
			end
		end
		
		CurrentMaid:GiveTask(btnsFrame.BuyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			print(SelectedCitations)
			NetworkController.Send('SendCitation', Target, SelectedCitations, bodyFrame.CitationFrame.DetailsBoxImage.PlateBox.Text)
			task.wait()
			CitationGUI:Disable()
		end))
		
		CurrentMaid:GiveTask(btnsFrame.ExitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			CitationGUI:Disable()
		end))
	end
end;

function CitationGUI:Disable()
	local UI = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("CitationGUI")
	local Main = UI:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
	local Components = UI:WaitForChild("Components")
	local Body = Main:WaitForChild("BodyFrame")
	for _, UI in pairs(Body.CitationFrame.CrimesBtnImage.crimesImage.crimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
		if UI:IsA("ImageButton") then
			UI:Destroy()
		end
	end
	Body.CitationFrame.SelectedOffencesLabel.Text = "Selected Offences:"
	Body.CitationFrame.UsernameLabel.Text = "Username: "
	Body.CitationFrame.TotalCitationLabel.Text = "Total Citation Amount: $0"
	local Tween = TweenService:Create(Main, TweenInfo.new(0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quad,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{Position = ClosedPosition})
	Tween:Play()
	Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
		Main.Visible = false
		Tween:Destroy()
	end)
	if CurrentMaid then
		CurrentMaid:Destroy()
	end

	if searchConnection then
        searchConnection:Disconnect();
        searchConnection = nil;
    end

    if focusConnection then
        focusConnection:Disconnect();
        focusConnection = nil;
    end

    if focusLostConnection then
        focusLostConnection:Disconnect();
        focusLostConnection = nil;
    end
end;

function CitationGUI:Start()

end

function CitationGUI:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
	NetworkController.Connect('OpenCitation', function(open, target)
		if type(open) == "boolean" then
			if open == true then
				CitationGUI:Enable(target)
			else
				CitationGUI:Disable()
			end
		end
	end)
	PlayerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui");
	TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	CanTween = true
	OpenPosition = UDim2.new(0.5,0,0.5,0)
	ClosedPosition = UDim2.new(0.5,0,1.5,0)
	Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
end

return CitationGUI

--[[
    CourtFilingGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Court FilingGUI
-- Khizzer
-- February 25, 2022



local CourtFilingGUI = {}

local MultipleChoice;
local ShortAnswer;
local LongAnswer;
local NetworkController;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local questions = {};

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local courtFilingGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('CourtFilingGUI');
local mainFrame = courtFilingGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local formImage = bodyFrame.FormImage;
local formScrollingFrame = formImage.FormScrollingFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local submitBtn = btnsFrame.SubmitBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local formSelectionImage = bodyFrame.FormSelectionImage;
local formsListScrollingFrame = formSelectionImage.FormsListScrollingFrame;
local civilActionBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.CivilActionBtn;
local criminalActionBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.CriminalActionBtn;
local leaveToAppealBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.LeaveToAppealBtn;
local noticeOfAppealBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.NoticeOfAppealBtn;
local prerogrativeWritBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.PrerogrativeWritBtn;
local judicialReviewBtn = formsListScrollingFrame.JudicialReviewBtn;

local components = courtFilingGUI.Components;
local multipleChoicePrefab = components.MultipleChoice;
local shortAnswerPrefab = components.ShortAnswer;
local longAnswerPrefab = components.LongAnswer;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local caseType = '';

local function CreateMultipleChoice(question: string, choices: table)
    local answerClass = MultipleChoice.new(multipleChoicePrefab, question, choices);
    answerClass.Component.Parent = formScrollingFrame;
    return answerClass;
end;

local function CreateShortAnswer(question: string)
    local answerClass = ShortAnswer.new(shortAnswerPrefab, question)
    answerClass.Component.Parent = formScrollingFrame;
    return answerClass;
end;

local function CreateLongAnswer(question: string)
    local answerClass = LongAnswer.new(longAnswerPrefab, question)
    answerClass.Component.Parent = formScrollingFrame;
    return answerClass;
end;

local TORTS = {'Negligence', 'Battery', 'Violation of rights', 'False citation', 'Violation of public law', 'Trespassing', 'False imprisonment', 'Breach of privacy', 'Breach of contract', 'Defamation', 'Harassment', 'Right to challenge disciplinary action'}

local CIVIL_ACTION_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Petitioner'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Defendant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications Contact of Petitioner'}};
    {CreateMultipleChoice, {'Torts', TORTS}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}

local CRIMINAL_ACTION_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Represenative for the Crown'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications Contact of Representative'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Defendant'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Charges'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}

local PREROGATIVE_WRIT_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications Contact of Applicant'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Grounds for Petition for Prerogative Writ'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}

local JUDICIAL_REVIEW_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications contact of Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Respondent '}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Government action for which judicial review is sought'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}

local LEAVE_TO_APPEAL_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications contact of Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Respondent '}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Case citation'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}

local NOTICE_OF_APPEAL_QUESTIONS = {
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Communications contact of Applicant'}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Respondent '}};
    {CreateShortAnswer, {'Case citation'}};
    {CreateLongAnswer, {'Statement of Facts'}};
}


local function ProcessFormTable(form)
    formImage.Visible = true;
    formSelectionImage.Visible = false;
    submitBtn.Visible = true;
    for _,v in next, questions do
        v:Destroy();
    end;
    for _,v in ipairs(form) do
        local questionFunction = v[1];
        local class = questionFunction(unpack(v[2]));
        table.insert(questions, class);
    end;
end;

function CourtFilingGUI.Enable()
    for _,v in next, questions do
        v:Destroy();
    end;
    questions = {};
    formSelectionImage.Visible = true;
    formImage.Visible = false;
    courtFilingGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();
end;

function CourtFilingGUI.Disable()
    for _,v in next, questions do
        v:Destroy();
    end;
    questions = {};
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    courtFilingGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function CourtFilingGUI:Start()
    civilActionBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(CIVIL_ACTION_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Civil Action'..'\n\n';
    end)
    criminalActionBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(CRIMINAL_ACTION_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Criminal Action'..'\n\n';
    end)
    leaveToAppealBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(LEAVE_TO_APPEAL_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Leave To Appeal'..'\n\n';
    end)
    noticeOfAppealBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(NOTICE_OF_APPEAL_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Notice of Appeal'..'\n\n';
    end)
    prerogrativeWritBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(PREROGATIVE_WRIT_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Prerogrative Writ'..'\n\n';
    end)
    judicialReviewBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        ProcessFormTable(JUDICIAL_REVIEW_QUESTIONS);
        caseType = 'Judicial Review'..'\n\n';
    end)
    
    submitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        local responses = '**Case Type**: \n'..caseType;
        for _,v in next, questions do
            local question = v.Component.Question.Text;
            local answer;
            if v['AnswerBox'] then
                answer = v.AnswerBox.Text;
            else
                answer = table.concat(v['Answers'], ', ');
            end;
            responses = responses..'**'..question..'**\n'..answer..'\n\n';
        end;
        NetworkController.Send('CourtFile', responses);
    end)

    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        CourtFilingGUI.Disable();
    end)
end;

function CourtFilingGUI:Init()
    ShortAnswer = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('ShortAnswer')));
    LongAnswer = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('LongAnswer')));
    MultipleChoice = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('MultipleChoice')));
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return CourtFilingGUI

--[[
    MultipleChoice (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI → CourtFilingGUI
    Parent: CourtFilingGUI
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Multiple Choice
-- Khizzer
-- February 25, 2022

local MultipleChoice = {}
MultipleChoice.__index = MultipleChoice
local Maid; 
local FastRemoveFirstValue;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

function MultipleChoice.new(component: ImageLabel, question: string, choices: table)
    local self = setmetatable({}, MultipleChoice)
    self.Component = component:Clone();
    self.ChoiceBtnPrefab = component.Parent.ChoiceBtn;
    self.Answers = {}

    local maid = Maid.new();
    self.Maid = maid;
    maid:GiveTask(self.Component)

    local questionLabel = self.Component.Question;
    questionLabel.Text = question;

    self:SetupChoices(choices);

    return self
end;

function MultipleChoice:SetupChoices(choices)
    local choicesImageLabel = self.Component.Choices;
    local choiceBtnPrefab = self.ChoiceBtnPrefab;
    for _,v in next, choices do
        local choiceBtn = choiceBtnPrefab:Clone();
        choiceBtn.Parent = choicesImageLabel;
        choiceBtn.ChoiceLabel.Text = v;

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(choiceBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(choiceBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(choiceBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
        
        self.Maid.GiveTask(self.Maid, choiceBtn.MouseEnter.Connect(choiceBtn.MouseEnter, function()
            local choiceText = choiceBtn.ChoiceLabel.Text;
            if table.find(self.Answers, choiceText) then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end));
        
        self.Maid.GiveTask(self.Maid, choiceBtn.MouseLeave.Connect(choiceBtn.MouseLeave, function()
            local choiceText = choiceBtn.ChoiceLabel.Text;
            if table.find(self.Answers, choiceText) then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end));
        
        self.Maid.GiveTask(self.Maid, choiceBtn.MouseButton1Click.Connect(choiceBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
            local choiceText = choiceBtn.ChoiceLabel.Text;
            if table.find(self.Answers, choiceText) then
                TweenService:Create(choiceBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                FastRemoveFirstValue(self.Answers, choiceText);
            else
                selectedTween:Play();
                table.insert(self.Answers, choiceText);
            end;
        end));
    end;

    local uiListLayout = choicesImageLabel.UIListLayout;
    local absoluteContentSize = uiListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize;

    choicesImageLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, absoluteContentSize.Y);
    self.Component.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, absoluteContentSize.Y + 40);
end;

function MultipleChoice:GetAnswer(): table
    return self.Answers;
end;

function MultipleChoice:Destroy()
    self.Maid:DoCleaning();
end

function MultipleChoice:Init()
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
    FastRemoveFirstValue = self.Shared.TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
end;


return MultipleChoice

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/DispatchGUI.lua ---

--[[
    DispatchGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- DispatchGUI
-- Khizzer
-- October 6, 2021



local DispatchGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local dispatchGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('DispatchGUI');
local callsFrame = dispatchGUI.CallsFrame;
local callsTopBarFrame = callsFrame.TopBarFrame;
local callsListScrollingFrame = callsFrame.BodyFrame.CallsListImage.CallsListScrollingFrame;
local callBtnPrefab = dispatchGUI.Components.CallBtnPrefab;

local detailsFrame = callsFrame.DetailsFrame;
local detailsBodyFrame = detailsFrame.BodyFrame;
local callLocationFrame = detailsBodyFrame.CallLocationFrame;
local callDetailsFrame = detailsBodyFrame.CallDetailsFrame;
local locationLabel = callLocationFrame.LocationLabel;
local detailsLabel = callDetailsFrame.DetailsLabel;
local unitsLabel = detailsBodyFrame.UnitsLabel;

local btnsFrame = detailsBodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local joinCallBtn = btnsFrame.JoinBtn;
local joinCallLabel = joinCallBtn.JoinLabel;
local c4CallBtn = btnsFrame.C4Btn;

local dispatchSound = localPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild('Sounds'):WaitForChild('Dispatch');

local joinCallConnection;
local c4CallConnection;

local selectedBtn;
local joinedCall;

local Notification;

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    callsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#callsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
end;

local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

function CreateCall(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER: string, caller: string, location: string, details: string)
    local callBtn = callBtnPrefab:Clone();
    callBtn.Parent = callsListScrollingFrame;
    callBtn.Name = UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER;
    callBtn.CallLabel.Text = caller;
    UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize();

    local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(callBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(callBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(callBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});


    callBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn == callBtn then return; end;
        hoverTween:Play();
    end)

    callBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn == callBtn then return; end;
        hoverEndTween:Play();
    end)

    callBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        locationLabel.Text = '';
        detailsLabel.Text = '';

        if joinedCall == UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER then
            joinCallLabel.Text = 'Leave'
        else
            joinCallLabel.Text = 'Join'
		end;

		if c4CallConnection then
			c4CallConnection:Disconnect();
			c4CallConnection = nil;
		end

        if selectedBtn and selectedBtn == callBtn then
            selectedBtn = nil;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
            detailsFrame.Visible = false;
            if joinCallConnection then
                joinCallConnection:Disconnect();
                joinCallConnection = nil;
            end;
            return
        elseif selectedBtn and selectedBtn ~= callBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            selectedBtn = callBtn;
            if joinCallConnection then
                joinCallConnection:Disconnect();
                joinCallConnection = nil;
            end;
        else
            selectedBtn = callBtn;
        end

        selectedTween:Play();

        detailsFrame.Visible = true;

        locationLabel.Text = location;
        detailsLabel.Text = details;

        local units = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetCallUnits', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
        repeat task.wait() until units;
        unitsLabel.Text = 'UNITS:\n' .. table.concat(units, '\n');

        joinCallConnection = joinCallBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            NetworkController.Send((joinCallLabel.Text == 'Join' and 'JOIN_CALL') or (joinCallLabel.Text == 'Leave' and 'LEAVE_CALL'), UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
            if not joinedCall then
                joinedCall = UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER;
            else
                joinedCall = nil;
            end;
            joinCallLabel.Text = ((joinedCall == UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER and 'Leave') or ('Join'));
        end)

        c4CallConnection = c4CallBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			NetworkController.Send('CODE4', UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
			c4CallConnection:Disconnect();
			c4CallConnection = nil;
        end)
    end)
end;

function DispatchGUI:Enable()
    local calls = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetDispatchCalls');
	for _,v in next, callsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
			v:Destroy();
		end
	end

	for UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER,v in next, calls or {} do
		CreateCall(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, v['caller'], v['location'], v['details']);
	end

    joinCallBtn.Visible = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS'
    c4CallBtn.Visible = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS'

    dispatchGUI.Enabled = true;
end;

function DispatchGUI:Disable()
	dispatchGUI.Enabled = false;
	for _,v in next, callsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
			v:Destroy();
		end
	end
end;

function DispatchGUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('NewDispatchCall', function(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, caller, location, details)
        dispatchSound:Play();
        CreateCall(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, caller, location, details)
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('UPDATE_UNITS', function(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, tableOfUnits)
        if selectedBtn then
            if selectedBtn.Name == UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER then
                unitsLabel.Text = 'UNITS:\n' .. table.concat(tableOfUnits, '\n');
            end;
        end;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('REMOVE_CALL', function(UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER, plr)
        if selectedBtn then
            if selectedBtn.Name == UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER then
                locationLabel.Text = '';
                detailsLabel.Text = '';
                unitsLabel.Text = 'UNITS: ';
                detailsFrame.Visible = false;
                callsListScrollingFrame[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]:Destroy();
                if joinCallConnection then
                    joinCallConnection:Disconnect();
                    joinCallConnection = nil;
                end;
                if c4CallConnection then
                    c4CallConnection:Disconnect();
                    c4CallConnection = nil;
                end;
            end;
            selectedBtn = nil;
        else
            callsListScrollingFrame[UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER]:Destroy();
        end;
        if joinedCall == UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER then
            joinCallLabel.Text = 'Join'
            joinedCall = nil;
		end;
		Notification.new('Code 4', 'A call was code 4ed by '..plr)

    end)

    self.Modules.UI.Draggable.new(dispatchGUI, callsTopBarFrame, callsFrame)
end;

function DispatchGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
	Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification;
end;

return DispatchGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/DownedGUI.lua ---

--[[
    DownedGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- DownedGUI
-- Khizzer
-- March 24, 2022



local DownedGUI = {}

local guiListeners;
local ListenerList;
local NetworkController;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.1);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local downedGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('DownedGUI');
local mainFrame = downedGUI.MainFrame;
local btnsFrame = mainFrame.BtnsFrame;
local respawnBtn = btnsFrame.RespawnBtn;
local timerLabel = respawnBtn.TimerLabel;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function DownedGUI:Enable()
    if not guiListeners then
        guiListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;
    downedGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    task.defer(function()
        for i = 7, 0, -1 do
            if i == 0 then
                timerLabel.Text = 'Respawn';
                guiListeners:Connect(respawnBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
                    print('button clicked')
                    NetworkController.Send('RAGDOLL_RESPAWN')
                    guiListeners:DisconnectAll();
                    closeTween:Play();
                    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
                    downedGUI.Enabled = false;
                end)
                break;
            end
            timerLabel.Text = 'Respawn ['..tostring(i)..']';
            task.wait(1);
        end;
    end);
end;

function DownedGUI:Disable()
    if guiListeners then
        guiListeners:DisconnectAll();
    end;
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    downedGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function DownedGUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('SetDownedGUI', function(state)
        if state == true then
            self:Enable();
        else
            self:Disable();
        end;
    end)
end

function DownedGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
end;


return DownedGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/ElectionGUI.lua ---

--[[
    ElectionGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- ElectionGUI
-- Khizzer
-- October 19, 2021

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5)
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23)
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159)

local ElectionGUI = {}
local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;
local TableUtil;
local ListenerList;
local FrameListenerList;
local Error;
local FastRemoveFirstValue;
local DeveloperCheck;

local localPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
local electionGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("ElectionGUI")
local mainFrame = electionGUI.MainFrame
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local submitBtn = btnsFrame.SubmitBtn;
local voteBtn = btnsFrame.VoteBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local backBtn = btnsFrame.BackBtn;

local tipsLabel = bodyFrame.TipsLabel
local startFrame = bodyFrame.StartFrame
local viewCandidatesBtn = startFrame.ViewCandidatesBtn;
local adminBtn = startFrame.AdminBtn;
local currentElectionLabel = startFrame.CurrentElectionLabel;

local candidatesFrame = bodyFrame.CandidatesFrame;
local voteCandidatesList = candidatesFrame.CandidatesListImage.CandidatesListScrollingFrame;

local adminFrame = bodyFrame.AdminFrame
local addCandidateBtn = adminFrame.AddCandidateBtn
local candidateBox = adminFrame.CandidateBoxImage.CandidateBox
local candidatesList = adminFrame.CandidatesList
local candidatesListScrollingFrame = candidatesList.CandidatesListScrollingFrame
local electionNameBoxImage = adminFrame.ElectionNameBoxImage
local electionNameBox = electionNameBoxImage.ElectionNameBox
local electionLengthBox = adminFrame.ElectionLengthBox;
local winnersBoxImage = adminFrame.WinnersBoxImage;
local winnersBox: TextBox = winnersBoxImage.WinnersBox;

local Components = electionGUI.Components
local candidateBtnPrefab = Components.CandidateBtn

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local ELECTION_COMMISSION = {885226366};

local electionDetails = game.ReplicatedStorage.ElectionDetails;
local winners = 0;

local candidateList = {}
local selectedLengthBtn;
local selectedVoteBtns = {};

local function ShowAdminPanel(enabled)
	FrameListenerList:DisconnectAll()
	if enabled then
		startFrame.Visible = false;
		candidatesFrame.Visible = false;
		adminFrame.Visible = true;
		tipsLabel.Text = "Elections Administration"
		submitBtn.Visible = true;
		backBtn.Visible = true;
		voteBtn.Visible = false;
		FrameListenerList:Connect(addCandidateBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
			local username = candidateBox.Text
			if string.len(username) <= 2 then
				Error("Username must be 3 or more characters.")
				return
			end
			local candidateBtn = candidateBtnPrefab:Clone()
			candidateBtn.CandidateLabel.Text = username
			candidateBtn.Parent = candidatesListScrollingFrame
			candidateList[#candidateList + 1] = username;
			FrameListenerList:Connect(candidateBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
				FastRemoveFirstValue(candidateList, candidateBtn.CandidateLabel.Text);
				candidateBtn:Destroy();
			end)
		end)

		FrameListenerList:Connect(submitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
			if string.len(electionNameBox.Text) <= 3 then
				Error('Election name must be longer than 3 characters.')
				return
			end
			if #candidateList <= 1 then
				Error('Add more candidates to create an election.')
				return
			end;

			local duration = tonumber(electionLengthBox.Text);

			if #electionLengthBox.Text == 0 then
				Error('Election duration must be a number.');
				return;
			end;

			if not duration then
				Error('Election duration must be a number.');
				return;
			end;

			if duration <= 0 then
				Error('Election duration must be greater than 0.')
				return;
			end;

			local winnersInput;

			if #winnersBox.Text == 0 then
				winnersInput = 1;
			else
				if not tonumber(winnersBox.Text) then
					Error('Winners must be a number.');
					return;
				end;
				if tonumber(winnersBox.Text) <= 0 then
					Error('Number of winners must be greater than 0.')
					return;
				end;
			end;
			winnersInput = tonumber(winnersBox.Text);

			NetworkController.Send('CREATE_ELECTION', electionNameBox.Text , candidateList, duration , winnersInput);
		end)
	else
		tipsLabel.Text = "Click 'View candidates' to begin the voting process!"
		startFrame.Visible = true;
		adminFrame.Visible = false;
		candidatesFrame.Visible = false;
		for _,v in next, candidatesListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
				v:Destroy();
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

local function ShowCandidatesFrame(enabled: boolean)
	FrameListenerList:DisconnectAll();
	if enabled then
		startFrame.Visible = false;
		backBtn.Visible = true;
		adminFrame.Visible = false;
		submitBtn.Visible = false;
		voteBtn.Visible = false;
		tipsLabel.Text = `Loading`

		local candidateDetails = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('ElectionGetCandidateDetails');
		if not candidateDetails then return end;

		candidatesFrame.Visible = true;
		tipsLabel.Text = `You can vote for up to {winners} candidates by clicking on them; modify your vote by clicking again. Votes are in blue.`
		voteBtn.Visible = true;
		selectedVoteBtns = {};

		for _,name in next, candidateDetails do
			local voteCandidateBtn = candidateBtnPrefab:Clone();
			voteCandidateBtn.Parent = voteCandidatesList;
			voteCandidateBtn.CandidateLabel.Text = name;

			local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(voteCandidateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, { ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR })
			local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(voteCandidateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, { ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR })
			local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(voteCandidateBtn, TWEEN_INFO, { ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR })
			local deselectedTween = hoverEndTween

			FrameListenerList:Connect(voteCandidateBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
				local selectedI = table.find(selectedVoteBtns, voteCandidateBtn)
				if selectedI then
					table.remove(selectedVoteBtns, selectedI)
					deselectedTween:Play()
				else
					if name == "Spoil my ballot" then
						for _, btn in selectedVoteBtns do
							TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, { ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR }):Play()
						end
						selectedVoteBtns = {}
					end

					if #selectedVoteBtns == winners then
						Error(`You can only vote for up to {winners} candidates.`)
						return
					end

					for i, btn in selectedVoteBtns do
						if btn.CandidateLabel.Text == "Spoil my ballot" then
							TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, { ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR }):Play()
							table.remove(selectedVoteBtns, i)
						end
					end

					table.insert(selectedVoteBtns, voteCandidateBtn)
					selectedTween:Play()
				end
			end)

			FrameListenerList:Connect(voteCandidateBtn.MouseEnter, function()
				if not table.find(selectedVoteBtns, voteCandidateBtn) then
					hoverTween:Play()
				end
			end)

			FrameListenerList:Connect(voteCandidateBtn.MouseLeave, function()
				if not table.find(selectedVoteBtns, voteCandidateBtn) then
					hoverEndTween:Play()
				end
			end)
		end;

		FrameListenerList:Connect(voteBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
			if #selectedVoteBtns == 0 then Error('Select a candidate!') end;
			NetworkController.Send('ADD_VOTE', TableUtil.Map(selectedVoteBtns, function(btn)
				return btn.CandidateLabel.Text
			end))
			ElectionGUI:Disable();
		end)
	else
		tipsLabel.Text = "Click 'View candidates' to begin the voting process!"
		startFrame.Visible = true;
		adminFrame.Visible = false;
		candidatesFrame.Visible = false;
		for _,v in next, voteCandidatesList:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
				v:Destroy();
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

function ElectionGUI.IsEnabled()
	return electionGUI.Enabled;
end;

function ElectionGUI:Enable()
	electionGUI.Enabled = true;
	if electionDetails:GetAttribute('GUID') then
		currentElectionLabel.Text = `CURRENT ELECTION: {electionDetails:GetAttribute('Title')}`;
		winners = electionDetails:GetAttribute('Winners')
	else
		currentElectionLabel.Text = 'CURRENT ELECTION: N/A'
		winners = 0
	end;

	candidatesFrame.Visible = false
	adminFrame.Visible = false
	startFrame.Visible = true
	tipsLabel.Text = "Click 'View candidates' to begin the voting process!"
	openTween:Play();
end;

function ElectionGUI:Disable()
	if FrameListenerList then
		FrameListenerList:DisconnectAll();
	end;
	closeTween:Play();
	closeTween.Completed:Wait();
	electionGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function ElectionGUI:Start()
	FrameListenerList = ListenerList.new()
	--self.ShowAdminPanel(true)
	--ShowCandidatesFrame(true);
	viewCandidatesBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		ShowCandidatesFrame(true)
	end);

	if DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or table.find(ELECTION_COMMISSION, localPlayer.UserId) then
		adminBtn.Visible = true;
		adminBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
			ShowAdminPanel(true);
		end);
	end


	backBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		FrameListenerList:DisconnectAll();
		ShowCandidatesFrame(false);
		ShowAdminPanel(false);
	end)

	exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		self:Disable();
	end)
	--UpdateElectionPart();
end

function ElectionGUI:Init()
	NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
	Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController
	ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList
	TableUtil = self.Shared.TableUtil;
	FastRemoveFirstValue = TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
	DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end

return ElectionGUI

--[[
    ErrorGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local TextService = game:GetService('TextService');

local NetworkController;

local DEFAULT_SIZE = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0);
local MIN_SIZE = 45;
local PADDING = 15;
--local ABSOLUTE_SIZE_X = 145;
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local Error;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local errorGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('ErrorGUI');
local mainFrame = errorGUI.MainFrame;
local UIScale = errorGUI.UIScale;

local components = errorGUI.Components;
-- local errorFramePrefab = components.ErrorFrame;

local function CreateErrorFrame(err: string)
--[[     local errorFrame = errorFramePrefab:Clone();
    local errorLabel = errorFrame.ErrorLabel;
    errorFrame.Size = DEFAULT_SIZE;
    errorLabel.Text = err;
    errorFrame.Parent = mainFrame; ]]

    local errorFrame = Error {
        Text = err;
        Parent = mainFrame;
    };

    errorGUI.Enabled = true;

--[[     local ySize = TextService:GetTextSize(err, errorLabel.TextSize, errorLabel.Font, Vector2.new(ABSOLUTE_SIZE_X, 200)).Y;
    do
        local errorLabelSizeX = errorLabel.Size.X;
        errorLabel.Size = UDim2.new(errorLabelSizeX.Scale, errorLabelSizeX.Offset, 0, ySize);
    end; ]]

    

    task.defer(function()
        local ySize = errorFrame.ErrorLabel.TextBounds.Y / UIScale.Scale;

        local openTween = TweenService:Create(errorFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, math.max(ySize + PADDING, MIN_SIZE))});
        openTween:Play();

        task.spawn(function()
            openTween.Completed:Wait();
            local waitTime = (#err*0.1)+1
            task.wait(waitTime);
            local closeTween = TweenService:Create(errorFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = DEFAULT_SIZE});
            closeTween:Play();
            closeTween.Completed:Wait();
            errorFrame:Destroy();
            if #mainFrame:GetChildren() == 1 then
                errorGUI.Enabled = false;
            end;
        end)
    end);
end;

local ErrorGUI = {};

function ErrorGUI.Error(err)
    CreateErrorFrame(err);
end;

function ErrorGUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('Error', CreateErrorFrame);
end;

function ErrorGUI:Init()
    Error = self.Fusion.Components.Error;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return ErrorGUI;

--[[

    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Fire GearGUI
-- Khizzer
-- March 30, 2023



local FireGearGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local NetworkController;
local Draggable;
local Trove;

local GuiTrove;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local fireGearGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('FireGearGUI');
local mainFrame = fireGearGUI.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local controlsImage = bodyFrame.ControlsImage;
local controlsScrollingFrame = controlsImage.ControlsScrollingFrame;
local helmetBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.HelmetBtn;
local visorBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.VisorBtn;
local maskBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.MaskBtn;
local gasMaskBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.GasMaskBtn;
local oxygenTankBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.OxygenTankBtn;
local originalHatsBtn = controlsScrollingFrame.OriginalHatsBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function FireGearGUI:Enable()
    if not GuiTrove then GuiTrove = Trove.new(); end;

    fireGearGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    for _,v in {helmetBtn, visorBtn, maskBtn, gasMaskBtn, oxygenTankBtn} do
        v:SetAttribute('Enabled', true);

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local defaultTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then return; end;

            hoverTween:Play();
        end));

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then return; end;

            defaultTween:Play();
        end));

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            v:SetAttribute('Enabled', not v:GetAttribute('Enabled'));

            task.defer(function()
                if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then
                    selectedTween:Play();
                else
                    defaultTween:Play();
                end;
            end)

            NetworkController.Send('FireGear', v.Name:gsub('Btn', ''));
        end));
    end;

    GuiTrove:Add(originalHatsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('VFRS_ToggleOriginalHats');
    end));
end;

function FireGearGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        fireGearGUI.Enabled = false;
        if GuiTrove then
            GuiTrove:Clean();
            GuiTrove = nil;
        end;
    end)
end;

function FireGearGUI:CharacterAdded(char)
    self:Disable();
end;

function FireGearGUI:Start()
    Draggable.new(fireGearGUI, topBarFrame, mainFrame);
    NetworkController.Connect('FireGearGUI', function()
        self:Enable();
    end);
end

function FireGearGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Draggable = self.Modules.UI.Draggable;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end;


return FireGearGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/FishingGUI.lua ---

--[[
    FishingGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- FishingGUI
-- Khizzer
-- November 7, 2022

local NetworkController;

local FishingGUI = {}

local ListenerList;
local GuiListeners;
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService");

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local fishingGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('FishingGUI');
local mainFrame = fishingGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local fishingFrame = bodyFrame.FishingFrame;
local fishImage = fishingFrame.FishImage;
local userBarImage = fishingFrame.UserBarImage;
local progressFrame = bodyFrame.ProgressFrame;
local progressImage = progressFrame.Progress;

-- clamp between 0, 336

local mouseDown = false;

local thread;

local playing = false;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.627, 0)});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5), {Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1.5, 0)});

local rightTween: Tween;
local leftTween: Tween;

local function collidesWith(gui1, gui2)
    local gui1_topLeft = gui1.AbsolutePosition;
    local gui1_bottomRight = gui1_topLeft + gui1.AbsoluteSize;

    local gui2_topLeft = gui2.AbsolutePosition;
    local gui2_bottomRight = gui2_topLeft + gui2.AbsoluteSize;

    return ((gui1_topLeft.x < gui2_bottomRight.x and gui1_bottomRight.x > gui2_topLeft.x) and (gui1_topLeft.y < gui2_bottomRight.y and gui1_bottomRight.y > gui2_topLeft.y)) 
end;

local progress = 0;

function FishingGUI:Enable()
    if not GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;

    fishingGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    GuiListeners:Connect(UserInputService.InputBegan, function(input: InputObject, gameProcessed)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            mouseDown = true;
            local timeNeeded = (367 - userBarImage.Position.X.Offset) / 100;
            if leftTween then
                leftTween:Cancel();
                leftTween = nil;
            end;
            rightTween = TweenService:Create(userBarImage, TweenInfo.new(timeNeeded, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {Position = UDim2.fromOffset(367, 0)});
            rightTween:Play();
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(UserInputService.InputEnded, function(input: InputObject, gameProcessed)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            mouseDown = false;
            local timeNeeded = math.abs(0 - userBarImage.Position.X.Offset) / 100;
            if rightTween then
                rightTween:Cancel();
                rightTween = nil;
            end;
            leftTween = TweenService:Create(userBarImage, TweenInfo.new(timeNeeded, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {Position = UDim2.fromOffset(0, 0)});
            leftTween:Play();
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:BindToRenderStep('FishingGUI', 1, function()
        --Check if userBarImage and fishImage are overlapping
        if collidesWith(userBarImage, fishImage) then
            progress += 0.4;
        else
            progress -= 0.4;
        end;
        progress = math.clamp(progress, 0, 100);

        if progress == 100 then
            NetworkController.Send('Fishing', 'CatchFish');
            if thread then
                task.cancel(thread);
                thread = nil;
            end;
            FishingGUI:Disable();
        end;

        progressImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(math.clamp(progress / 100, 0 , 100), 1);
    end);

    thread = task.defer(function()
        while true do
            --Move the fish randomly
            local left = math.clamp(fishImage.Position.X.Offset - 100 , 0, 336);
            local right = math.clamp(fishImage.Position.X.Offset + 100, 0, 336);
            local x = {left, right};
            local newX = x[math.random(1, 2)];

            fishImage:TweenPosition(UDim2.fromOffset(newX, 0), Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, 1, true);
            task.wait(3)
        end;
    end);
end;

function FishingGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        fishingGUI.Enabled = false;
    end)

    if GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners:DisconnectAll();
        GuiListeners = nil;
    end;
    if thread then
        task.cancel(thread);
        thread = nil;
    end;
    if rightTween then
        rightTween:Cancel();
        rightTween = nil;
    end;
    if leftTween then
        leftTween:Cancel();
        leftTween = nil;
    end;
end;

function FishingGUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('FishingMinigame', function()
        FishingGUI:Enable();
    end);
end;

function FishingGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
end;


return FishingGUI


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/FriskGUI.lua ---

--[[
    FriskGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- FriskGUI
-- Khizzer
-- June 23, 2022



local FriskGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
--local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local PlayerGui = Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local friskGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('FriskGUI');
local mainFrame = friskGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local toolsFrame = bodyFrame.ToolsFrame;

local btnsFrame = mainFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local components = friskGUI.Components;
local toolBtnPrefab = components.ToolBtn;

local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local function LoadTool(victim, tool)
    local toolBtn = toolBtnPrefab:Clone();
    local takeImage = toolBtn.TakeImage;
    local toolName = tool.Name;
    local toolLabel = toolBtn.ToolLabel;

    toolLabel.Text = toolName;

    toolBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        toolBtn:Destroy();
        NetworkController.Send('RemoveTool', victim, toolName);
    end);

    toolBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        takeImage.Visible = true;
    end);

    toolBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        takeImage.Visible = false;
    end);

    toolBtn.Parent = toolsFrame;
end;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION,});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION,});

function FriskGUI:Enable(victim)
    friskGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    for _,v in toolsFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for _,v in NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('Frisk', victim) do
        if v:IsA('Tool') then
            LoadTool(victim, v);
        end;
    end;
end;

function FriskGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    friskGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function FriskGUI:Start()
    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end)
end;

function FriskGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return FriskGUI
