--[[
    GamepassGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- GamepassGUI
-- Khizzer
-- February 8, 2024

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService')
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local Gamepasses;
local Trove;
local NetworkController;

local GuiTrove;

type Gamepass = {
    Gamepass: number,
    Product: number
}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local gamepassGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('GamepassGUI');
local mainFrame = gamepassGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local gamepassListImage = bodyFrame.GamepassListImage;
local gamepassListScrollingFrame = gamepassListImage.GamepassListScrollingFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn: ImageButton = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local buyBtn: ImageButton = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local giftBtn: ImageButton = btnsFrame.GiftBtn;
local usernameBox: TextBox = btnsFrame.UsernameBox;

local selectedBtn: TextButton?;

local components = gamepassGUI.Components;
local gamepassPrefab: TextButton & {Thumbnail: ImageLabel, NameLabel: TextLabel} = components.Gamepass;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local GamepassGUI = {}


function GamepassGUI:Enable()
    if GuiTrove then GuiTrove:Destroy(); end;

    gamepassGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    GuiTrove = Trove.new();

    for attribute, gamepassTable: Gamepass in next, Gamepasses.RegularGamepasses do
        local gamepassId = gamepassTable.Gamepass;
        local productId = gamepassTable.Product;

        local gamepassBtn = gamepassPrefab:Clone();
        gamepassBtn.Parent = gamepassListScrollingFrame;

        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn);

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
        
        GuiTrove:Add(hoverTween);
        GuiTrove:Add(hoverEndTween);
        GuiTrove:Add(selectedTween);

        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == gamepassBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end));
        
        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == gamepassBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end));
        
        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end
            
            selectedBtn = gamepassBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
        end));

        local productInfo = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(gamepassId, Enum.InfoType.GamePass);
        gamepassBtn.Thumbnail.Image = `rbxassetid://{productInfo.IconImageAssetId}`;
        gamepassBtn.NameLabel.Text = productInfo.Name;
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('GamepassID', gamepassId);
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('ProductID', productId);
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('Attribute', attribute);
    end

    for attribute, gamepassTable: Gamepass in next, Gamepasses.GearGamepasses do
        local gamepassId = gamepassTable.Gamepass;
        local productId = gamepassTable.Product;

        local gamepassBtn = gamepassPrefab:Clone();
        gamepassBtn.Parent = gamepassListScrollingFrame;

        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn);

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(gamepassBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
        
        GuiTrove:Add(hoverTween);
        GuiTrove:Add(hoverEndTween);
        GuiTrove:Add(selectedTween);

        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == gamepassBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end));
        
        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == gamepassBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end));
        
        GuiTrove:Add(gamepassBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end
            
            selectedBtn = gamepassBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
        end));

        local productInfo = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(gamepassId, Enum.InfoType.GamePass);
        gamepassBtn.Thumbnail.Image = `rbxassetid://{productInfo.IconImageAssetId}`;
        gamepassBtn.NameLabel.Text = productInfo.Name;
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('GamepassID', gamepassId);
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('ProductID', productId);
        gamepassBtn:SetAttribute('Attribute', attribute);
    end

    GuiTrove:Add(exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end));

    GuiTrove:Add(buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if not selectedBtn then return; end;
        local gamepassId = selectedBtn:GetAttribute('GamepassID');
        MarketplaceService:PromptGamePassPurchase(localPlayer, gamepassId); --since the server can detect it we dont really need to ask it
    end));

    GuiTrove:Add(giftBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if not selectedBtn then return; end;

        if #usernameBox.Text < 3 then return _G.AeroError('Please enter a valid username.'); end;
        local userId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(usernameBox.Text);

        if not userId then return _G.AeroError('User does not exist.'); end;

        NetworkController.Send('GamepassGift', userId, selectedBtn:GetAttribute('Attribute'));
        --Until roblox makes a way to attach data to a purchase i have to do this
    end));
end

function GamepassGUI:Disable()
    if GuiTrove then GuiTrove:Destroy(); end;

    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        gamepassGUI.Enabled = false;
    end)
end

function GamepassGUI:Toggle()
    if gamepassGUI.Enabled then
        self:Disable();
    else
        self:Enable();
    end;
end;

function GamepassGUI:Start()
end

function GamepassGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Gamepasses = self.Shared.Constants.Gamepasses;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end


return GamepassGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/GangGUI.lua ---

--[[
    GangGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- GangGUI
-- Khizzer
-- May 14, 2022

local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

type TextType = 'Primary' | 'Secondary' | 'Tertiary';

type GangRank = 'Member' | 'Enforcer' | 'Leader';

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local MEMBER_LIMIT = 8;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local gangGUI: ScreenGui = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('GangGUI');
local mainFrame: Frame = gangGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame: Frame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local categoryFrame: ImageLabel = bodyFrame.CategoryFrame;
local leaderboardBtn: ImageButton = categoryFrame.LeaderboardBtn;
local myGangBtn: ImageButton = categoryFrame.MyGangBtn;
local gangListImage: ImageLabel = bodyFrame.GangListImage;
local gangListScrollingFrame: ScrollingFrame = gangListImage.GangListScrollingFrame;
local gangMembersImage: ImageLabel = bodyFrame.GangMembersImage;
local memberListScrollingFrame: ScrollingFrame = gangMembersImage.MemberListScrollingFrame;
local detailsFrame: ImageLabel = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local kickBtn = btnsFrame.KickBtn;
local createBtn = btnsFrame.CreateBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local gangNameBoxImage = detailsFrame.GangNameBoxImage;
local gangNameBox = gangNameBoxImage.GangNameBox;
local inviteBtn = memberListScrollingFrame.InviteBtn;

local components: Configuration = gangGUI.Components;
local templateBtn: ImageButton = components.TemplateBtn;

local selectedBtn = leaderboardBtn;
local selectedGangBtn;
local selectedMemberBtn;

local kickBtnConnection;

local invitePlayersOn = false;

local GangGUI = {}

GangGUI.CreateBtn = createBtn;

local function SetText(textType: TextType, text: string)
    local textLabel = detailsFrame:FindFirstChild(textType .. 'Label');
    assert(textLabel, '[GangGUI]: ' ..textType.. ' label not found.');
    if textLabel then
        textLabel.Text = text;
    end;
end;

type gangData = {
    Name: string;
    Members: number;
    Leader: string;
    Notoriety: number;
};

type gangMemberData = {
    Name: string;
    Rank: GangRank;
    Notoriety: number;
};

type myGangData = {
    GangData: gangData;
    IsLeader: boolean;
    Members: {gangMemberData}
};

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {
    Position = ACTIVE_POSITION
});

local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {
    Position = DEFAULT_POSITION
});

function GangGUI.ShowCategory(category: 'MyGang' | 'Leaderboard')
    gangMembersImage.Visible = false;
    gangListImage.Visible = false;
    for _,v in next, {gangListScrollingFrame, memberListScrollingFrame} do
        for _, v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
            if v2:IsA('ImageButton') and v2.Name ~= 'InviteBtn' then
                v2:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
    end;

    if category == 'Leaderboard' then
        gangListImage.Visible = true;
        gangNameBoxImage.Visible = false;
        createBtn.Visible = false;

        local otherGangData: {gangData} = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetOtherGangData');
        if not otherGangData then return; end;

        for _,gangData in next, otherGangData do
            local gangBtn = templateBtn:Clone();
            gangBtn.Parent = gangListScrollingFrame;
            gangBtn.TextLabel.Text = gangData.Name;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(gangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(gangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(gangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
            
            gangBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedGangBtn == gangBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);
            
            gangBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedGangBtn == gangBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);
            
            gangBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if selectedGangBtn then
                    TweenService:Create(selectedGangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                end;
                
                selectedGangBtn = gangBtn;
                selectedTween:Play();

                SetText('Primary', gangData.Name);
                SetText('Secondary', gangData.Members .. ' members');
                SetText('Tertiary', 'Leader: '..gangData.Leader);
                SetText('Quaternary', 'Notoriety: '..gangData.Notoriety);
            end);
        end;
    elseif category == 'MyGang' then
        gangMembersImage.Visible = true;

        if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Gang') ~= nil then
            gangNameBoxImage.Visible = false;
            createBtn.Visible = false;
            local myGangData: myGangData = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetMyGangData');
            
            if not myGangData then _G.AeroError('[GangGUI] Failed to load your gang data'); return; end;
    
            createBtn.Visible = false;
            SetText('Primary', myGangData.GangData.Name);
            SetText('Secondary', myGangData.GangData.Members .. ' members');
            SetText('Tertiary', 'Leader: '..myGangData.GangData.Leader);
            SetText('Quaternary', 'Notoriety: '..myGangData.GangData.Notoriety);
    
            for _,v in next, myGangData.Members do
                local rank = v.Rank;
                local name = v.Name;
                local notoriety = v.Notoriety;

                local memberBtn = templateBtn:Clone();
                memberBtn.Parent = memberListScrollingFrame;
                memberBtn.TextLabel.Text = name;
                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(memberBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(memberBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(memberBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
                
                memberBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if selectedMemberBtn == memberBtn then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);
                
                memberBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if selectedMemberBtn == memberBtn then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);
                
                memberBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if selectedMemberBtn then
                        TweenService:Create(selectedMemberBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                    end
    
                    selectedMemberBtn = memberBtn;
                    selectedTween:Play();
    
                    SetText('Primary', name);
                    SetText('Secondary', 'Rank: '.. rank);
                    SetText('Tertiary', 'Notoriety: '.. notoriety);
                    SetText('Quaternary', '');
    
                    kickBtn.Visible = (rank ~= 'Leader');
                    if kickBtnConnection then
                        kickBtnConnection:Disconnect();
                        kickBtnConnection = nil;
                    end;
                    kickBtnConnection = kickBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                        local success = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('KickFromGang', name);
                        if success then
                            kickBtnConnection:Disconnect();
                            memberBtn:Destroy();
                            kickBtnConnection = nil;
                        end
                    end)
                end);
            end;
            inviteBtn.Visible = true;
        else
            SetText('Primary', 'You are not in a gang');
            SetText('Secondary', '');
            SetText('Tertiary', '');
            SetText('Quaternary', '');
            gangNameBoxImage.Visible = true;
            createBtn.Visible = true;
            inviteBtn.Visible = false;
        end
    end;
end;

function GangGUI:Enable()
    return _G.AeroError("This feature is temporarily disabled whilst it is being worked on. It will be back soon!");
--[[     if not gangGUI.Enabled then
        gangGUI.Enabled = true;
        openTween:Play();
        openTween.Completed:Wait();
    end; ]]
end;

function GangGUI:Disable()
    if gangGUI.Enabled then
        closeTween:Play();
        closeTween.Completed:Wait();
        gangGUI.Enabled = false;
    end;
end;

function GangGUI:Toggle()
    if gangGUI.Enabled then
        self:Disable();
    else
        self:Enable();
    end;
end;

function GangGUI:Start()
    local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(inviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(inviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end)

    inviteBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if invitePlayersOn then return; end;
        hoverTween:Play();
    end);
    
    inviteBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if invitePlayersOn then return; end;
        hoverEndTween:Play();
    end);
    
    inviteBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        for _,v in memberListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v.Name == 'InvitePlayer' then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        if invitePlayersOn then
            invitePlayersOn = false;
            TweenService:Create(inviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            inviteBtn.InviteLabel.Text = 'Invite Players';
            for _,v in memberListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') and v ~= inviteBtn then
                    v.Visible = true;
                end;
            end;
            return;
        else
            invitePlayersOn = true;
            TweenService:Create(inviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            inviteBtn.InviteLabel.Text = 'Back';
            for _,v in memberListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') and v ~= inviteBtn then
                    v.Visible = false;
                end;
            end;
        end

        for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
            if v ~= localPlayer and v.Team == game.Teams.Civilian then
                local playerInviteBtn = templateBtn:Clone();
                playerInviteBtn.Parent = memberListScrollingFrame;
                playerInviteBtn.TextLabel.Text = v.Name;
                playerInviteBtn.Name = 'InvitePlayer';

                local _hoverTween = TweenService:Create(playerInviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local _hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(playerInviteBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                
                playerInviteBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    _hoverTween:Play();
                end);
                
                playerInviteBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    _hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);
                
                playerInviteBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    NetworkController.Send('InviteToGang', v.Name);
                end);
            end
        end
    end);

    local leaderboardHoverTween = TweenService:Create(leaderboardBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local leaderHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(leaderboardBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local leaderboardSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(leaderboardBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
    
    leaderboardBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn == leaderboardBtn then return; end;
        leaderboardHoverTween:Play();
    end);
    
    leaderboardBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn == leaderboardBtn then return; end;
        leaderHoverEndTween:Play();
    end);
    
    leaderboardBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end
        
        selectedBtn = leaderboardBtn;
        leaderboardSelectedTween:Play();
    
        self.ShowCategory('Leaderboard');
    end);

    local myGangHoverTween = TweenService:Create(myGangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local myGangHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(myGangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local myGangSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(myGangBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
    
    myGangBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
    if selectedBtn == myGangBtn then return; end;
        myGangHoverTween:Play();
    end);
    
    myGangBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
    if selectedBtn == myGangBtn then return; end;
        myGangHoverEndTween:Play();
    end);
    
    myGangBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if selectedBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end
        
        selectedBtn = myGangBtn;
        myGangSelectedTween:Play();
        
        self.ShowCategory('MyGang');
    end);

    createBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        local gangName = gangNameBox.Text;
        if #gangName <= 3 then _G.AeroError('Gang name too short.') return; end;

        local success = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('CreateGang', gangName);
        if success then
            createBtn.Visible = false;
            gangNameBoxImage.Visible = false;
            SetText('Primary', gangName);
            SetText('Secondary', '1 member');
            SetText('Tertiary', 'Leader: '..localPlayer.Name);
            SetText('Quaternary', 'Notoriety: 0');
            inviteBtn.Visible = true;
        end;
    end);
end;

function GangGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return GangGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/GasPumpGUI.lua ---

--[[
    GasPumpGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Gas PumpGUI
-- Khizzer
-- July 26, 2021



local GasPumpGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local PlayerGUI = localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerGui');
local gasPumpGUI = PlayerGUI:WaitForChild('GasPumpGUI');
local mainFrame = gasPumpGUI.MainFrame;
local gasFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame.GasFrame;

local exitBtn = mainFrame.BodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local gasBar = gasFrame.GasBar;
local gasBarImage = gasBar.GasBarImage;

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local OpenTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION})
local CloseTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION})

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");

local gasChangeConnection;
local pumpConnections = {};

local TwoDPFormat;

local pumping = false;
local enabled = false

local humanoidRootPart;

local NetworkController;

function GasPumpGUI:Enable(interactionPart)
    self:Disable();
    OpenTween:Play();
    enabled = true

    gasFrame.GasPriceLabel.Text = "Today's Gas Price: "..TwoDPFormat(ReplicatedStorage.GasPrice.Value);

    if localPlayer.Car.Value == nil then self:Disable() return; end;

    local car = localPlayer.Car.Value

    local gas: IntValue = car.Config.State.Gas;
    local maxGas = gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100;

    gasBarImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(gas.Value / maxGas, 1);

    gasChangeConnection = gas.Changed:Connect(function(newValue)
        gasBarImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(newValue / maxGas, 1)
    end);

    pumpConnections[1] = gasFrame.PumpBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        pumping = true;
    end)
    pumpConnections[2] = gasFrame.PumpBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
        pumping = false;
	end);

	pumpConnections[3] = exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		self:Disable();
	end)

    while enabled do
        if pumping and car and gas then
            local gasValue = gas.Value;
            local newCapacity = gasValue + 1;
            if newCapacity >= (gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100) then break end
            NetworkController.Send('GasPump');
        end

        task.wait(.3);
    end;

    while (interactionPart.Position - humanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 7 do task.wait(); end;
    self:Disable();
end;

function GasPumpGUI:Disable()
    if gasChangeConnection then
        gasChangeConnection:Disconnect()
        gasChangeConnection = nil;
    end;
    if pumpConnections[1] then
        pumpConnections[1]:Disconnect();
        pumpConnections[2] = nil;
    end;
    if pumpConnections[2] then
        pumpConnections[2]:Disconnect();
        pumpConnections[2] = nil;
    end;
    pumping = false;
    enabled = false
    CloseTween:Play();
end;

function GasPumpGUI:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;

    humanoidRootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end

function GasPumpGUI:Start()
end;

function GasPumpGUI:Init()
    TwoDPFormat = self.Shared.NumberUtil.TwoDPFormat;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return GasPumpGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/GasRobberyUI.lua ---

--[[
    GasRobberyUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Gas HeistUI
-- Khizzer
-- June 12, 2023

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local gasRobberyGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('GasRobberyGUI');
local mainFrame = gasRobberyGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local gameFrame = bodyFrame.GameFrame;
local tipsLabel = bodyFrame.TipsLabel;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local Trove;
local UserInput;
local NetworkController;

local LETTER_PREFAB = gasRobberyGUI.Components.LetterPrefab;

local GasRobberyUI = {}

local CHARACTER_SETS = {
    "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ",
    "0123456789"
}

local LETTER_COUNT = 72;

local selectedIndex = 1;

local currentCode;

local PlayerControl = require(localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerScripts'):WaitForChild('PlayerModule'):WaitForChild('ControlModule'));

local function GetRandomCharacter()
    local characterSet = CHARACTER_SETS[math.random(1, #CHARACTER_SETS)]
    local randomString = math.random(#characterSet)
    return string.sub(characterSet, randomString, randomString)
end;

local function GeneratePattern()

    local characterLength = 4
    local characterSet = CHARACTER_SETS[math.random(1, #CHARACTER_SETS)]
    local randomSet = ""

    for i = 1, characterLength do
        local randomString = math.random(#characterSet)
        randomSet = randomSet .. string.sub(characterSet, randomString, randomString)
    end

    return randomSet
end;

local function GetTextFromIndex(layoutOrder: number)
    for _,v in next, gameFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('TextLabel') then
            if v.LayoutOrder == layoutOrder then
                return v.Text;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

local function evaluate(): boolean
    local code = "";
    for i = 0, 3 do
        code = code .. GetTextFromIndex(selectedIndex + i);
    end;

    if code == currentCode then return true; end;

    return false;
end;

function GasRobberyUI:_createPuzzle()
    local code = GeneratePattern();

    currentCode = code;

    local randomIndex = math.random(1, LETTER_COUNT - 4); --Cant start at LETTER_COUNT - 4 to LETTER_COUNT because it will go out of bounds

    for i = 1, LETTER_COUNT do
        if i > randomIndex and i <= randomIndex + 3 then continue; end;
        if i == randomIndex then
            for i2 = 1, 4 do
                local letter = LETTER_PREFAB:Clone();
                letter.Parent = gameFrame;
                letter.Text = code:sub(i2, i2);
                letter.LayoutOrder = i + i2 - 1;
                self._trove:Add(letter);
            end;
        else
            local letter = LETTER_PREFAB:Clone();
            letter.Parent = gameFrame;
            letter.Text = GetRandomCharacter();
            letter.LayoutOrder = i;
            self._trove:Add(letter);
        end;
    end;

    tipsLabel.Text = `Use A and D to naviagate and press Enter to submit. Look for the code: {code}`;
end;

function GasRobberyUI:_selectIndex(layoutOrder: number)
    local indexesToHighlight = {};
    for i = 0, 3 do
        local nextIndex = layoutOrder + i;
        local isOverflowing = nextIndex > LETTER_COUNT;
        if isOverflowing then
            local overflowAmount = nextIndex - LETTER_COUNT;
            table.insert(indexesToHighlight, overflowAmount);
        else
            table.insert(indexesToHighlight, layoutOrder + i);
        end;
    end;

    for _,v in next, gameFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('TextLabel') then
            if table.find(indexesToHighlight, v.LayoutOrder) then
                v.TextColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
            else
                v.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

function GasRobberyUI:_startMinigame(interactionPart: Part)
    self._isMinigameActive = true;

    if not self._trove then
        self._trove = Trove.new();
    end;

    gasRobberyGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    self:_createPuzzle();

    self._trove:Add(function()
        closeTween:Play();
        closeTween.Completed:Wait();
        gasRobberyGUI.Enabled = false;
        self._isMinigameActive = false;
        PlayerControl:Enable();
    end)

    PlayerControl:Disable();

    local Keyboard = UserInput:Get('Keyboard');

    self._trove:Add(Keyboard.KeyDown:Connect(function(keyCode)
        local nextIndex = selectedIndex;

        if keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then
            nextIndex = selectedIndex - 1;
            if nextIndex <= 0 then
                nextIndex = LETTER_COUNT;
            end;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then
            nextIndex = selectedIndex + 1;
            if nextIndex > LETTER_COUNT then
                nextIndex = 1;
            end;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Return then
            local isCorrect = evaluate();
            if isCorrect then
                NetworkController.Send('GasRobberySuccess', interactionPart)
            else
                NetworkController.Send('GasRobberyFail', interactionPart);
            end;
            self._trove:Destroy();
            self._trove = nil;
        end;

        selectedIndex = nextIndex;

        self:_selectIndex(selectedIndex);
    end));

    while true do
        task.wait(1.25);
        if self._isMinigameActive == false then break; end;
        for _, letter in gameFrame:GetChildren() do
            if letter:IsA('TextLabel') then
                local nextLayoutOrder = letter.LayoutOrder + 1;
                if nextLayoutOrder > LETTER_COUNT then nextLayoutOrder = 1; end;
                letter.LayoutOrder = nextLayoutOrder;
            end;
        end;
        self:_selectIndex(selectedIndex);
    end;
end;

function GasRobberyUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('GasStationRobbery', function(interactionPart: Part)
        if not CollectionService:HasTag(interactionPart, 'GasStationRobbery') then
            warn('[GasRobberyUI] Interaction part is invalid?')
        end;
        self:_startMinigame(interactionPart);
    end);
end;

function GasRobberyUI:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    UserInput = self.Controllers.UserInput;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return GasRobberyUI

]]
-- Hotbar LayoutGUI
-- Khizzer
-- March 6, 2022

local NetworkController;
local InventoryGUI;
local Error;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local selectedBtn;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local hotbarLayoutGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('HotbarLayoutGUI');
local mainFrame = hotbarLayoutGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local layoutsListImage = bodyFrame.LayoutsListImage;
local layoutsScrollingFrame = layoutsListImage.LayoutsScrollingFrame;
local layout1Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout1;
local layout2Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout2;
local layout3Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout3;
local layout4Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout4;
local layout5Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout5;
local layout6Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout6;
local layout7Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout7;
local layout8Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout8;
local layout9Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout9;
local layout10Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout10;
local layout11Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout11;
local layout12Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout12;
local layout13Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout13;
local layout14Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout14;
local layout15Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout15;
local layout16Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout16;
local layout17Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout17;
local layout18Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout18;
local layout19Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout19;
local layout20Btn = layoutsScrollingFrame.Layout20;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local saveBtn = btnsFrame.SaveBtn;
local loadBtn = btnsFrame.LoadBtn;
local layoutNameBoxImage = btnsFrame.LayoutNameBoxImage;
local layoutNameBox = layoutNameBoxImage.LayoutNameBox;

local connections = {}

local HotbarLayoutGUI = {}

function HotbarLayoutGUI.IsEnabled()
    return hotbarLayoutGUI.Enabled;
end

local function DisconnectAll()
	for i,conn in pairs(connections) do
		if type(conn) == 'userdata' and conn then
			conn:Disconnect()
		end
	end
end

local DEFAULT_NAMES = {
    [layout1Btn] = 'Layout 1';
    [layout2Btn] = 'Layout 2';
    [layout3Btn] = 'Layout 3';
    [layout4Btn] = 'Layout 4';
    [layout5Btn] = 'Layout 5';
    [layout6Btn] = 'Layout 6';
    [layout7Btn] = 'Layout 7';
    [layout8Btn] = 'Layout 8';
    [layout9Btn] = 'Layout 9';
    [layout10Btn] = 'Layout 10';
    [layout11Btn] = 'Layout 11';
    [layout12Btn] = 'Layout 12';
    [layout13Btn] = 'Layout 13';
    [layout14Btn] = 'Layout 14';
    [layout15Btn] = 'Layout 15';
    [layout16Btn] = 'Layout 16';
    [layout17Btn] = 'Layout 17';
    [layout18Btn] = 'Layout 18';
    [layout19Btn] = 'Layout 19';
    [layout20Btn] = 'Layout 20';
};

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function HotbarLayoutGUI:Enable()
    if self.IsEnabled() then return; end;
    DisconnectAll();
    hotbarLayoutGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    local btns = {layout1Btn, layout2Btn, layout3Btn, layout4Btn, layout5Btn, layout6Btn, layout7Btn, layout8Btn, layout9Btn, layout10Btn, layout11Btn, layout12Btn, layout13Btn, layout14Btn, layout15Btn, layout16Btn, layout17Btn, layout18Btn, layout19Btn, layout20Btn};

    for i,btn in ipairs(btns) do
        local name = localPlayer.BackpackLayouts:FindFirstChild(`{i}`):GetAttribute('Name');
        btn.LayoutNameLabel.Text = name;

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        table.insert(connections, (#connections + 1), btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == btn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end));

        table.insert(connections, (#connections + 1),btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == btn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end));

        table.insert(connections, (#connections + 1),btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedBtn = btn;
            selectedTween:Play();
        end));
    end

    table.insert(connections, (#connections + 1), saveBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        local hotbarOrder = InventoryGUI.GetHotbarTools();
        if not selectedBtn then Error('No layout selected to overwrite') return; end;
        local layoutName = DEFAULT_NAMES[selectedBtn];

        local layoutNickname = layoutNameBox.Text;
        if #layoutNickname < 1 then
            Error('Name too short. Saved as default name.');
            layoutNickname = layoutName;
        end;

        NetworkController.Send('UPDATE_BACKPACK_LAYOUT', layoutName, hotbarOrder, layoutNickname);
    end))

    table.insert(connections, (#connections + 1), loadBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        if not selectedBtn then Error('No layout selected to load.') return; end;

        local layoutName = DEFAULT_NAMES[selectedBtn];
        layoutName = (layoutName):sub(8);
        local backpackLayout = localPlayer.BackpackLayouts:FindFirstChild(layoutName);
        if not backpackLayout then Error('No layout found. Try rejoining. If this persists, contact a developer.'); return; end;

        local savedLayoutData = {};

        for i = 1, 10 do
            local toolName = backpackLayout:GetAttribute('Slot'..tostring(i));
            if toolName == 'Tool Name' then break; end;

            savedLayoutData[#savedLayoutData+1] = toolName;
        end;

        InventoryGUI:SortHotbar(savedLayoutData)
    end))
end;

function HotbarLayoutGUI:Disable()
    DisconnectAll();
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    hotbarLayoutGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function HotbarLayoutGUI.Toggle()
    if HotbarLayoutGUI.IsEnabled() then
        HotbarLayoutGUI:Disable();
    else
        HotbarLayoutGUI:Enable();
    end;
end;

function HotbarLayoutGUI:Start()
end;

function HotbarLayoutGUI:Init()
    Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    InventoryGUI = self.Controllers.UI.InventoryGUI;
end;


return HotbarLayoutGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/InventoryGUI.lua ---

--[[
    InventoryGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService');

local Error;
local Trove;

local UNEQUIPPED_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local EQUIPPED_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local UNEQUIPPED_HOVER_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(60, 60, 60);
local EQUIPPED_HOVER_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(89, 131, 169);
local FULL_MAIN_FRAME_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 655, 0, 70);
local OPENED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 655, 0, 225);
local CLOSED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 655, 0, 0);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local GUI_INSET_Y = game:GetService('GuiService'):GetGuiInset().Y;
local MAX_TOOLS = 10;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local playerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui;

local postSimulation = RunService.Heartbeat;

local backpack;

local char;
local humanoid;

local inventoryTrove;

local inventoryGUI = playerGUI:WaitForChild('InventoryGUI');
local UIScaleInstance = inventoryGUI.UIScale;
local mainFrame = inventoryGUI.MainFrame;
local extraFrame = inventoryGUI.ExtraFrame;
local extraScrollingFrame = extraFrame.ScrollingFrame;

local components = inventoryGUI.Components;
local toolBtnPrefab = components.ToolBtn;

local mainFrameFullTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = FULL_MAIN_FRAME_SIZE});

local extraFrameOpenTween = TweenService:Create(extraFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = OPENED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE});
local extraFrameCloseTween = TweenService:Create(extraFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = CLOSED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE});

local enabled = true;

local uiScale = 1;

local isExtraFrameOpen = false;

local tools = {};
local extraTools = {};

local equippedTool;

local numberKeys = {
    One = 1,
    Two = 2,
    Three = 3,
    Four = 4,
    Five = 5,
    Six = 6,
    Seven = 7,
    Eight = 8,
    Nine = 9,
    Zero = 10
};

local function IsToolEquipped(tool)
    return tool.Parent == char;
end;

local function GetToolDataFromInstance(instance)
    local searchIndex = instance:IsA('Tool') and 'tool' or 'button';
    local searchedArray = tools;
    local toolArrayIndex: number;

    local searchComplete = false;

    for i, v in next, searchedArray do
        if v[searchIndex] == instance then
            toolArrayIndex = i;
            searchComplete = true;
            break;
        end;
    end;
    if not toolArrayIndex then
        searchedArray = extraTools;
        for i, v in next, searchedArray do
            if v[searchIndex] == instance then
                toolArrayIndex = i;
                searchComplete = true;
                break;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    if not searchComplete then return; end;

    return searchedArray, toolArrayIndex;
end;

local function GetPositionForPositionLabel(position)
    return (position == 10) and 0 or position;
end;

local function UpdateMainAndExtraFrame()
    if isExtraFrameOpen then
        if mainFrame.Size ~= FULL_MAIN_FRAME_SIZE then
            mainFrame.Visible = true;
            mainFrameFullTween:Play();
        end;
        if extraFrame.Size ~= OPENED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE then
            extraFrame.Visible = true;
            extraFrameOpenTween:Play();
        end;
    else
        local amountOfTools = #tools;
        if amountOfTools == 0 then
            coroutine.wrap(function()
                local targetProps = {Size = UDim2.fromOffset(0, 70)};
                local tween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, targetProps);
                tween:Play();
                tween.Completed:Wait();
                if mainFrame.Size == targetProps.Size then
                    mainFrame.Visible = false;
                end;
            end)();
        else
            mainFrame.Visible = true;
            TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = UDim2.fromOffset((amountOfTools * 65) + 5, 70)}):Play();
        end;
        if extraFrame.Size ~= CLOSED_EXTRA_FRAME_SIZE then
            extraFrameCloseTween:Play();
            extraFrameCloseTween.Completed:Wait();
            extraFrame.Visible = false;
        end;
    end;
end;

local function OnInput(input, gameProcessedEvent)
    if gameProcessedEvent then return; end;
    if not enabled then return; end;

    local toolArrayIndex = numberKeys[input.KeyCode.Name];

    if toolArrayIndex then
        local toolData = tools[toolArrayIndex];
        if not toolData then return; end;
        local tool = toolData.tool;
        if not IsToolEquipped(tool) then
            humanoid:EquipTool(tool);
        else
            humanoid:UnequipTools();
        end;
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Backquote then
--[[         isExtraFrameOpen = not extraFrame.Visible;
        UpdateMainAndExtraFrame(); ]]
    end;
end;

local function IsMouseInBounds(mousePosition, target)
    for i, v in next, playerGUI:GetGuiObjectsAtPosition(mousePosition.X, mousePosition.Y) do
        if v == target then
            return true;
        end;
    end;
end;

local function GetObjectUnderMouse(mousePosition)
    for i, v in next, mainFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            if IsMouseInBounds(mousePosition, v) then
                return v;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    for i, v in next, extraScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            if IsMouseInBounds(mousePosition, v) then
                return v;
            end;
        end;
    end;

    if IsMouseInBounds(mousePosition, mainFrame) then
        return mainFrame;
    end;

    if (extraFrame.Visible) and (IsMouseInBounds(mousePosition, extraFrame)) then
        return extraScrollingFrame;
    end;
end;

local function UpdateToolBtns(startIndex)
    for i = startIndex, #tools do
        local btn = tools[i].button;
        local positionLabel = btn.PositionLabel;
        local newPosition = i;
        btn.LayoutOrder = newPosition;
        positionLabel.Text = GetPositionForPositionLabel(newPosition);
    end;
end;

local function UpdateExtraToolBtns(startIndex)
    for i = startIndex, #extraTools do
        local btn = extraTools[i].button;
        local newPosition = i;
        btn.LayoutOrder = newPosition;
    end;
end;

local function UpdateExtraScrollingFrame()
    extraScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (math.floor(#extraTools / 10) + 1) * 65);
end;

local function UpdateScale()
    uiScale = UIScaleInstance.Scale;
end;

local function MoveToolBtn(toolBtn, objectUnderMouse)
    local searchedArray, toolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(toolBtn);
    if not toolArrayIndex then return end;
    local toolData = searchedArray[toolArrayIndex];

    if objectUnderMouse:IsA('ImageButton') then
        local targetSearchedArray, targetToolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(objectUnderMouse);
        if not targetToolArrayIndex then return; end;
        local targetToolData = targetSearchedArray[targetToolArrayIndex];

        searchedArray[toolArrayIndex] = targetToolData;
        targetSearchedArray[targetToolArrayIndex] = toolData;

        local toolBtnLayoutOrder = toolBtn.LayoutOrder;
        toolBtn.LayoutOrder = objectUnderMouse.LayoutOrder;
        objectUnderMouse.LayoutOrder = toolBtnLayoutOrder;

        local toolBtnParent = toolBtn.Parent;
        toolBtn.Parent = objectUnderMouse.Parent;
        objectUnderMouse.Parent = toolBtnParent;

        if toolBtn.Parent == extraScrollingFrame then
            toolBtn.PositionLabel.Text = '';
        end;
        if objectUnderMouse.Parent == extraScrollingFrame then
            objectUnderMouse.PositionLabel.Text = '';
        end;

        if ((searchedArray == tools) or (targetSearchedArray == tools)) then
            UpdateToolBtns(math.min(toolArrayIndex, targetToolArrayIndex));
        end;
        if (searchedArray == extraTools) or (targetSearchedArray == extraTools) then
            UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
            UpdateExtraToolBtns(math.min(toolArrayIndex, targetToolArrayIndex));
        end;
    elseif objectUnderMouse == mainFrame then
        if #tools == MAX_TOOLS then return; end;

        table.remove(searchedArray, toolArrayIndex);
        local newArrayIndex = #tools + 1;
        tools[newArrayIndex] = toolData;

        toolBtn.LayoutOrder = newArrayIndex;
        toolBtn.Parent = objectUnderMouse;

        if searchedArray == tools then
            UpdateToolBtns(toolArrayIndex);
        else
            toolBtn.PositionLabel.Text = GetPositionForPositionLabel(newArrayIndex);
            UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
            UpdateExtraToolBtns(math.min(toolArrayIndex));
        end;
    elseif objectUnderMouse == extraScrollingFrame then
        table.remove(searchedArray, toolArrayIndex);
        local newArrayIndex = #extraTools + 1;
        extraTools[newArrayIndex] = toolData;

        toolBtn.PositionLabel.Text = '';

        toolBtn.LayoutOrder = newArrayIndex;
        toolBtn.Parent = objectUnderMouse;

        UpdateToolBtns(toolArrayIndex);
        UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
    end;
end;

local function StartBtnDragging(toolBtn)
    local finalPosition = Vector2.new();
    local toolBtnClone = toolBtn:Clone();
    toolBtnClone.Parent = inventoryGUI;

    while UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1) do
        local mouseLocation = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation();
        mouseLocation = Vector2.new(mouseLocation.X, mouseLocation.Y - GUI_INSET_Y);
        finalPosition = mouseLocation;
        toolBtnClone.Position = UDim2.fromOffset(mouseLocation.X / uiScale, mouseLocation.Y / uiScale);
        postSimulation:Wait();
    end;

    toolBtnClone:Destroy();

    local objectUnderMouse = GetObjectUnderMouse(finalPosition);
    if (not objectUnderMouse) or (objectUnderMouse == toolBtn) then return; end;

    MoveToolBtn(toolBtn, objectUnderMouse);
end;

local function ToolAdded(tool)
    local isInventoryFull = (#tools == MAX_TOOLS);
    local toolArrayIndex = #tools + 1;

    local lastClickedTime = os.time();
    local heldTag = os.time();

    local toolBtn = toolBtnPrefab:Clone();
    local positionLabel = toolBtn.PositionLabel;
    local nameLabel = toolBtn.NameLabel;
    toolBtn.LayoutOrder = isInventoryFull and (#extraTools + 1) or toolArrayIndex;
    positionLabel.Text = isInventoryFull and '' or GetPositionForPositionLabel(toolArrayIndex);
    nameLabel.Text = tool.Name;
    toolBtn.Parent = isInventoryFull and extraScrollingFrame or mainFrame;

    if isInventoryFull then
        UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
    end;

    toolBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if toolBtn:GetAttribute('Flash') then return; end;
        if equippedTool == tool then
            TweenService:Create(toolBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = EQUIPPED_HOVER_COLOR}):Play();
        else
            TweenService:Create(toolBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = UNEQUIPPED_HOVER_COLOR}):Play();
        end;
    end);

    toolBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if toolBtn:GetAttribute('Flash') then return; end;
        if equippedTool == tool then
            TweenService:Create(toolBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = EQUIPPED_COLOR}):Play();
        else
            TweenService:Create(toolBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = UNEQUIPPED_COLOR}):Play();
        end;
    end);

    toolBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        local thisTag = os.time();
        heldTag = thisTag;
        if not IsToolEquipped(tool) then
            humanoid:EquipTool(tool);
        else
            humanoid:UnequipTools();
        end;
        if thisTag - lastClickedTime < 0.2 then
            if toolBtn.Parent == extraScrollingFrame then
                MoveToolBtn(toolBtn, mainFrame);
                return;
            end;
        end;
        lastClickedTime = thisTag;
        wait(0.06);
        if heldTag == thisTag then
            StartBtnDragging(toolBtn);
        end;
    end);

    toolBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
        heldTag = 0;
    end);

    local targetToolsTbl = isInventoryFull and extraTools or tools;
    targetToolsTbl[#targetToolsTbl + 1] = {
        tool = tool,
        button = toolBtn
    };

    UpdateMainAndExtraFrame();
end;

local function ToolEquipped(tool)
    local searchedArray, toolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(tool);
    if not toolArrayIndex then return; end;
    local toolData = searchedArray[toolArrayIndex];
    equippedTool = toolData.tool;
    TweenService:Create(toolData.button, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = EQUIPPED_COLOR}):Play();
end;

local function ToolUnequipped(tool)
    local searchedArray, toolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(tool);
    if not toolArrayIndex then return; end;
    local toolData = searchedArray[toolArrayIndex];
    equippedTool = nil;
    if toolData.button:GetAttribute('Flash') then return; end;
    TweenService:Create(toolData.button, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = UNEQUIPPED_COLOR}):Play();
end;

local function ToolRemoved(tool)
    local searchedArray, toolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(tool);
    if not toolArrayIndex then return; end;
    local toolData = searchedArray[toolArrayIndex];

    if equippedTool == tool then
        ToolUnequipped(tool);
    end;

    table.remove(searchedArray, toolArrayIndex);
    toolData.button:Destroy();

    if searchedArray == tools then
        UpdateToolBtns(toolArrayIndex);
    elseif searchedArray == extraTools then
        UpdateExtraToolBtns(toolArrayIndex);
    end;

    UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
    UpdateMainAndExtraFrame();
end;

local InventoryGUI = {};

local phoneThread;

function InventoryGUI:CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;

    if phoneThread then
        task.cancel(phoneThread);
        phoneThread = nil;
    end

    tools = {};
    extraTools = {};

    for i, v in next, mainFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for i, v in next, extraScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    char = char_;
    backpack = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Backpack');
    humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');

    inventoryTrove = Trove.new();
    inventoryTrove:AttachToInstance(backpack);

    for i, v in next, backpack:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Tool') then
            ToolAdded(v);
        end;
    end;

    inventoryTrove:Add(char.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            local _, toolArrayIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(child);
            if not toolArrayIndex then
                ToolAdded(child);
            end;
            ToolEquipped(child);
        end;
    end));

    inventoryTrove:Add(char.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            if child.Parent == backpack then return; end;
            ToolRemoved(child);
        end;
    end));

    inventoryTrove:Add(backpack.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            if equippedTool == child then
                ToolUnequipped(child);
            else
                ToolAdded(child);
            end;
        end;
    end));

    inventoryTrove:Add(backpack.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA('Tool') then
            if not IsToolEquipped(child) then
                ToolRemoved(child);
            end;
        end;
    end));

    if (#tools == 0) and (#extraTools == 0) then
        UpdateExtraScrollingFrame();
        UpdateMainAndExtraFrame();
    end;
end;

function InventoryGUI.SetEnabled(isEnabled)
    enabled = isEnabled;
    inventoryGUI.Enabled = isEnabled;
    localPlayer.Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools();
end;

function InventoryGUI.GetHotbarTools()
    local a = {};
    for _,v in next, tools do
        table.insert(a, #a + 1, v.tool.Name);
    end;
    return a;
end;

function InventoryGUI:SortHotbar(layout)
    humanoid:UnequipTools();
    for _,v in next, mainFrame:GetChildren() do
        MoveToolBtn(v, extraScrollingFrame);
    end;
    for _,toolName in next, layout do
        humanoid:UnequipTools();
        if not backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName) then
            Error('Could not find '..toolName..' in your backpack.');
            continue;
        else
            local searchedArray, toolIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(backpack[toolName])
            if not searchedArray then
                Error('Could not find '..toolName..' in your backpack.');
                continue;
            else
                local toolArray = searchedArray[toolIndex];
                MoveToolBtn(toolArray.button, mainFrame);
            end;
        end;
    end
    UpdateMainAndExtraFrame()
end;

function InventoryGUI.ExtraFrameToggle()
    isExtraFrameOpen = not extraFrame.Visible;
    UpdateMainAndExtraFrame();
end

--I wanted to make this generic but i cant see a use case for it outside of the phone
function InventoryGUI.FlashPhone(state: boolean)
    local tool = backpack:FindFirstChild('Phone') or char:FindFirstChild('Phone');
    if not tool then return; end;

    local searchedArray, toolIndex = GetToolDataFromInstance(tool);
    if not searchedArray then return; end;

    local toolArray = searchedArray[toolIndex];
    local button = toolArray.button;

    if state == false then
        print('Stopping flash');
        if phoneThread then
            task.cancel(phoneThread);
            phoneThread = nil;
        end

        button:SetAttribute('Flash', false);
        button.ImageColor3 = char:FindFirstChild('Phone') and EQUIPPED_COLOR or UNEQUIPPED_COLOR;
    else
        phoneThread = task.defer(function()
            button:SetAttribute('Flash', true);
            while true do
                button.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(170, 137, 53);
                task.wait(0.3);
                button.ImageColor3 = UNEQUIPPED_COLOR;
                task.wait(0.3);
            end
        end)
    end
end

function InventoryGUI:Start()

    UpdateScale();
    UIScaleInstance:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Scale'):Connect(UpdateScale);

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(OnInput);

    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('SetInventoryEnabled', self.SetEnabled);

    while true do
        local suc = pcall(function()
            game.StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Backpack, false);
        end);
        if suc then break; end;
        task.wait();
    end;
end;

function InventoryGUI:Init()
    Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end;

return InventoryGUI;

--[[
    JailGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TextChatService = game:GetService('TextChatService');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

-- JailGUI
-- Khizzer
-- December 25, 2021


local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local jailGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('JailGUI');
local mainFrame = jailGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local timeLabel = bodyFrame.TimeLabel;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local bailBTn = btnsFrame.BailBtn;
local releaseBtn = btnsFrame.ReleaseBtn;


local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.2);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local SecondsToMinutes;

local prisonTime = localPlayer:WaitForChild('PrisonTime');

local emoteCommands = TextChatService:WaitForChild('TextChatCommands');
local emoteCommand: TextChatCommand = emoteCommands:WaitForChild('RBXEmoteCommand');

local timeListener: RBXScriptConnection?;
local bailConnection: RBXScriptConnection?;
local releaseConnection: RBXScriptConnection?;

local NetworkController;


local JailGUI = {}

function JailGUI:Enable()
    jailGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();
    timeListener = prisonTime.Changed:Connect(function(newTime)
        local formattedTime = SecondsToMinutes(newTime)
        timeLabel.Text = 'Remaining Prison Sentence: '..formattedTime
        bailBTn.Visible = newTime > 0 and newTime < 1500
        releaseBtn.Visible = newTime <= 0
    end)

    bailConnection = bailBTn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('Bail')
    end)

    releaseConnection = releaseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('PrisonRelease')
    end)
end;

function JailGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait()
    jailGUI.Enabled = false;
    bailBTn.Visible = false
    releaseBtn.Visible = false
    if timeListener then
        timeListener:Disconnect();
        timeListener = nil;
    end

    if bailConnection then
        bailConnection:Disconnect();
        bailConnection = nil;
    end;
end;

function JailGUI:Start()
    localPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(function()
        if localPlayer.Team == game.Teams.Prisoner then
            self:Enable()
            emoteCommand.Parent = nil;
        else
            self:Disable();
            emoteCommand.Parent = emoteCommands;
        end
    end)

    if localPlayer.Team == game.Teams.Prisoner then
        self:Enable()
    else
        self:Disable();
    end

    NetworkController.Connect('JailGUI', function(status)
        self[status](self)
    end)
end;

function JailGUI:Init()
    SecondsToMinutes = self.Shared.SecondsToMinutes;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end


return JailGUI

local function HideOtherUIs(val)
	if val == true then
		for i,v in pairs(localPlayer.PlayerGui:GetChildren()) do
			if v:IsA("ScreenGui") then
				if v ~= judgeGUI and v.Name ~= 'BottomLeftGUI' then
					if v.Enabled == true then
						table.insert(hid, (#hid + 1), v)
						v.Enabled = false
					end
				end
			end
		end
	else
		for i,v in pairs(hid) do
			if v:IsA("ScreenGui") then
				v.Enabled = true
				hid[i] = nil
			end
		end
	end
end
