function JudgeGUI:ShowSubMenu(menu)
    mainMenuUIListeners:DisconnectAll();
    toggledBtn = {};
    if not UIListeners then
        UIListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;

    if menu == 'warrant' then
        local activeWarrants = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetActiveWarrants');

        for _,v in next, warrantsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantExitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable()
        end)

        for identifier,warrantTable in next, activeWarrants do
            local warrantBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone();
            warrantBtn.Parent = warrantsScrollingFrame;

            warrantBtn.Name = identifier;
            warrantBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = warrantTable[1];

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(warrantBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(warrantBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(warrantBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            UIListeners:Connect(warrantBtn.MouseEnter, function()
            if selectedWarrantBtn == warrantBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            UIListeners:Connect(warrantBtn.MouseLeave, function()
            if selectedWarrantBtn == warrantBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            UIListeners:Connect(warrantBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
            if selectedWarrantBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedWarrantBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedWarrantBtn = warrantBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
            end);

            local wdb = false
            UIListeners:Connect(removeWarrantBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
                if wdb then return end
                if selectedWarrantBtn then
                    wdb = true
                    NetworkController.Send('REMOVE_WARRANT', selectedWarrantBtn.Name);
                    task.wait(2)
                    wdb = false
                else
                    Error('No warrant selected to remove.');
                end;
            end);
        end

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantCrimesBox.Focused, function()
            if not warrantListImage.Visible then
                warrantListImage.Visible = true;
            else
                warrantListImage.Visible = false;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantCrimesBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'), function()
            for _,v in next, warrantCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v.Visible = false;
                    if string.find((v.Name):lower(), (warrantCrimesBox.Text):lower()) then
                        v.Visible = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantCrimesBox.FocusLost, function()
            task.wait(0.5);
            warrantListImage.Visible = false;
        end)

        if #warrantCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() == 1 then
            for crime, prisonTime in CrimesModule do
                local crimeBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone();
                crimeBtn.Name = crime;
                crimeBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = crime;
                crimeBtn.ZIndex = 4;
                crimeBtn.Parent = warrantCrimesScrollingFrame;

                local defaultTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                crimeBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then
                        --disables if toggled
                        defaultTween:Play()
                        FastRemoveFirstValue(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    elseif #toggledBtn == 3 and (not table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn)) then
                        --3 crimes activated, remove first one
                        TweenService:Create(toggledBtn[1], TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                        table.remove(toggledBtn, 1);
                        table.insert(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                        selectedTween:Play()
                    elseif #toggledBtn < 3 and (not table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn)) then
                        --2 or less crimes activated
                        selectedTween:Play();
                        table.insert(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    end;
                end);
            end;
        end;

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantBackBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable();
            JudgeGUI:Enable();
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(warrantSubmitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            if #warrantReasonBox.Text < 10 then Error('Warrant reasoning too short'); return; end;
            if #toggledBtn == 0 then Error('No crimes selected for warrant'); return; end;
            if #toggledBtn > 3 then Error('Cannot issue more than three charges for warrant'); return; end;
            if #warrantUsernameBox.Text < 3 then Error('Username too short'); return; end;

            local crimesTable = {}
            for i,v in next, toggledBtn do
                table.insert(crimesTable, v.TemplateLabel.Text);
            end;

            JudgeGUI:Disable();

            local description = ('You are about to issue a warrant for the arrest of %s for the crimes: %s. The reasoning for this warrant is: %s. Are you sure this is correct?'):format(warrantUsernameBox.Text, table.concat(crimesTable, ', '), warrantReasonBox.Text);
            YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt('Judicial System', description,
            function()
                JudgeGUI:Disable()
                NetworkController.Send('SUBMIT_WARRANT', warrantUsernameBox.Text , crimesTable, warrantReasonBox.Text);
            end,
            function()
                JudgeGUI:Enable();
            end)
        end)
    elseif menu == 'fines' then
        if #fineCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() == 1 then
            for crime, amount in CitationsModule do

                local crimeBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone();
                crimeBtn.Name = crime;
                crimeBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = crime;
                crimeBtn.ZIndex = 4;
                crimeBtn.Parent = fineCrimesScrollingFrame;

                local defaultTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                crimeBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then
                        defaultTween:Play()
                        FastRemoveFirstValue(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    else
                        selectedTween:Play();
                        table.insert(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    end;
                end);
            end;
        end;

        UIListeners:Connect(fineCrimesBox.Focused, function()
            if not fineListImage.Visible then
                fineListImage.Visible = true;
            else
                fineListImage.Visible = false;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(fineCrimesBox.FocusLost, function()
            task.wait(.5);
            fineListImage.Visible = false;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(fineCrimesBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'), function()
            for _,v in next, fineCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v.Visible = false;
                    if string.find((v.Name):lower(), (fineCrimesBox.Text):lower()) then
                        v.Visible = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(fineSubmitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            local username = fineUsernameBox.Text;
            if #username < 3 then
                Error('Username too short');
                return;
            end;
            if #toggledBtn == 0 then
                Error('No selected fine offences');
                return;
            end;
            local crimesTable = {}
            for i,v in next, toggledBtn do
                table.insert(crimesTable, v.TemplateLabel.Text);
            end;

            JudgeGUI:Disable();

            local description = ('You are about to issue a fine to %s for the crimes: %s. The reasoning for this fine is: %s. Are you sure this is correct?'):format(fineUsernameBox.Text, table.concat(crimesTable, ', '), fineReasonBox.Text);
            YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt('Judicial System', description,
                function()
                    UIListeners:DisconnectAll();
                    NetworkController.Send('SUBMIT_FINE', fineUsernameBox.Text , crimesTable, fineReasonBox.Text, tonumber(fineCustomBox.Text));
                end,
                function()
                    JudgeGUI:Enable();
                end)
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(fineBackBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable();
            JudgeGUI:Enable();
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(fineExitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable()
        end)
    elseif menu == 'arrest' then
        if #arrestCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() == 1 then
            for crime, prisonTime in CrimesModule do
                local crimeBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone();
                crimeBtn.Name = crime;
                crimeBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = crime;
                crimeBtn.ZIndex = 4;
                crimeBtn.Parent = arrestCrimesScrollingFrame;

                local defaultTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(crimeBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                crimeBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                crimeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if table.find(toggledBtn, crimeBtn) then
                        defaultTween:Play()
                        FastRemoveFirstValue(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    else
                        selectedTween:Play();
                        table.insert(toggledBtn, crimeBtn);
                    end;
                end);
            end;
        end;

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestCrimesBox.Focused, function()
            if not arrestListImage.Visible then
                arrestListImage.Visible = true;
            else
                arrestListImage.Visible = false;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestCrimesBox.FocusLost, function()
            task.wait(.5);
            arrestListImage.Visible = false;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestCrimesBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'), function()
            for _,v in next, arrestCrimesScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v.Visible = false;
                    if string.find((v.Name):lower(), (arrestCrimesBox.Text):lower()) then
                        v.Visible = true;
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestSubmitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            local username = arrestUsernameBox.Text;
            if #username < 3 then
                Error('Username too short');
                return;
            end;
            if #toggledBtn == 0 then
                Error('No selected arrest offences');
                return;
            end;
            local crimesTable = {}
            for i,v in next, toggledBtn do
                table.insert(crimesTable, v.TemplateLabel.Text);
            end;

            JudgeGUI:Disable();

            local description = ('You are about to issue a arrest to %s for the crimes: %s. The reasoning for this arrest is: %s. Are you sure this is correct?'):format(arrestUsernameBox.Text, table.concat(crimesTable, ', '), arrestReasonBox.Text);
            YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt('Judicial System', description,
                function()
                    NetworkController.Send('JUDGE_ARREST', arrestUsernameBox.Text , crimesTable, arrestReasonBox.Text, tonumber(arrestCustomBox.Text));
                end,
                function()
                    JudgeGUI:Enable();
                end)
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestBackBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable();
            JudgeGUI:Enable();
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(arrestExitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable()
        end)
    elseif menu == 'expungement' then
        local function updateChargesLabel(charges)
            if #charges == 0 then
                expungementChargesLabel.Text = 'No charges inputted'
            else
                expungementChargesLabel.Text = `Charges ({#charges}): `..table.concat(charges, '; ')
            end
        end

        for _,v in next, expungementArrestsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
        for _,v in next, expungementCitationsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
        UIListeners:Connect(expungementSearchBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            if expungementUsernameBox.Text == '' then return; end;
            local data = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('DatabaseLookup', expungementUsernameBox.Text);
            if data == 'Not found' then print('No data') return; end;

            for _,v in next, expungementArrestsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v:Destroy();
                end;
            end;
            for _,v in next, expungementCitationsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v:Destroy();
                end;
            end;

            lastSearchedUser = expungementUsernameBox.Text;

            for uniqueIdentifier,record in next, data['ArrestRecord'] do
                local recordBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone()
                recordBtn.Parent = expungementArrestsScrollingFrame;
                recordBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = `{record['Length']}s - {record['Date']}`;
                recordBtn.Name = uniqueIdentifier;

                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                recordBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                recordBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                recordBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn then
                        TweenService:Create(selectedExpungementRecordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                    end

                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then
                        TweenService:Create(selectedExpungementRecordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play()
                        selectedExpungementRecordBtn = nil;
                    end

                    selectedExpungementRecordBtn = recordBtn;
                    selectedTween:Play();

                    expungementOfficerLabel.Text = 'Officer: '..record['Officer'];
                    updateChargesLabel(record['Offences']);
                    expungementLengthLabel.Text = 'Sentence Length (s): '..tostring(record['Length']);
                    expungementDescriptionLabel.Text = 'Desc. of Incident: \n'..record['Details']
                end)
            end;

            for uniqueIdentifier,record in next, data['CitationRecord'] do
                local recordBtn = templateBtnPrefab:Clone()
                recordBtn.Parent = expungementCitationsScrollingFrame;
                recordBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = `${record['Price']} - {record['Date']}`;
                recordBtn.Name = uniqueIdentifier;

                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                recordBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                recordBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                recordBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn then
                        TweenService:Create(selectedExpungementRecordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                    end

                    if selectedExpungementRecordBtn == recordBtn then
                        TweenService:Create(selectedExpungementRecordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play()
                        selectedExpungementRecordBtn = nil;
                    end

                    selectedExpungementRecordBtn = recordBtn;
                    selectedTween:Play();

                    expungementOfficerLabel.Text = 'Officer: '..record['Officer'];
                    updateChargesLabel(record['Offences']);
                    expungementLengthLabel.Text = 'Cited amount (CA$): '..tostring(record['Price']);
                    expungementDescriptionLabel.Text = 'Desc. of Incident: \n'..record['Details']
                end)
            end;
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(expungementRemoveBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            if not selectedExpungementRecordBtn then return; end;

            local UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER = selectedExpungementRecordBtn.Name;
            local recordType = (selectedExpungementRecordBtn.Parent == expungementCitationsScrollingFrame and 'Citation') or 'Arrest';

            NetworkController.Send('JUDGE_REMOVE_RECORD', lastSearchedUser, recordType, UNIQUE_IDENTIFIER);
        end);

        UIListeners:Connect(expungementClearAllBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable();
            YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt('Judicial System', 'You are about to clear this user\'s record. You may only do this once every 20 minutes. Are you sure?',
            function()
                NetworkController.Send('JUDGE_CLEAR_RECORDS', lastSearchedUser);
            end,
            function()
                JudgeGUI:Enable();
            end)
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(expungementExitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable()
        end)

        UIListeners:Connect(expungementBackBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            JudgeGUI:Disable();
            JudgeGUI:Enable();
        end)
    end;
end;

function JudgeGUI:Disable()
    if UIListeners then
        UIListeners:Destroy();
    end;
    if mainMenuUIListeners then
        mainMenuUIListeners:DisconnectAll();
    end;
    expungementCloseTween:Play();
    fineMenuCloseTween:Play();
    arrestMenuCloseTween:Play();
    warrantMenuCloseTween:Play();
    mainMenuCloseTween:Play();
    mainFrame.Visible = false;
    warrantFrame.Visible = false;
    arrestFrame.Visible = false;
    fineFrame.Visible = false;
    expungementFrame.Visible = false;
    judgeGUI.Enabled = false;
    HideOtherUIs(false);
end

function JudgeGUI:Start()
    UIListeners = ListenerList.new();
    mainMenuUIListeners = ListenerList.new();
end

function JudgeGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error;
    CrimesModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CrimesModule'));
    FastRemoveFirstValue = self.Shared.TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
    YesNoPromptGUI = self.Controllers.UI.YesNoPromptGUI;
    CitationsModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CitationsModule'));
    CrimesModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CrimesModule'));
end


return JudgeGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/LadderGUI.lua ---

--[[
    LadderGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- LadderGUI
-- oSudden
-- November 13, 2021

local LadderGUI = {};

local PlayerGui;

local TweenService;

local CanTween;

local OpenPosition;

local ClosedPosition;

local NetworkController;

local ContextActionService;

local Connections;

local function DisconnectAll()
	for i,conn in pairs(Connections) do
		if type(conn) == 'userdata' and conn then
			conn:Disconnect()
		end
	end
end

local function HandleContext(Action, Input, Object)
	print(Object.Name)
end

function LadderGUI:Enable()
	DisconnectAll()
	local UI = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("LadderControlGUI")
	local MainFrame = UI:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
	local BodyFrame = MainFrame:WaitForChild("BodyFrame")
	local BtnsFrame = BodyFrame:WaitForChild("BtnsFrame")
	local ControlsFrame = BodyFrame:WaitForChild("ControlsFrame")
	MainFrame.Visible = true
	local Tween = TweenService:Create(MainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {Position = OpenPosition})
	Tween:Play()
	Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
		Tween:Destroy()
	end)
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), BtnsFrame:WaitForChild("ExitBtn").MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		LadderGUI:Disable()
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("LeftBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Left", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("RightBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Right", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("UpBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Up", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("DownBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Down", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("ResetBtn").MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Reset");
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("OutBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Out", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("InBtn").MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "In", true);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("LeftBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Left", false);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("RightBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Right", false);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("UpBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Up", false);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("DownBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Down", false);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("OutBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "Out", false);
	end))
	table.insert(Connections, (#Connections + 1), ControlsFrame:WaitForChild("InBtn").MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', "In", false);
	end))
end;

function LadderGUI:Disable()
	DisconnectAll()
	local UI = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("LadderControlGUI")
	local MainFrame = UI:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
	local BodyFrame = MainFrame:WaitForChild("BodyFrame")
	local BtnsFrame = BodyFrame:WaitForChild("BtnsFrame")
	local ControlsFrame = BodyFrame:WaitForChild("ControlsFrame")
	local Tween = TweenService:Create(MainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, false, 0), {Position = ClosedPosition})
	Tween:Play()
	Tween.Completed:Connect(function()
		MainFrame.Visible = false
		Tween:Destroy()
	end)
end;

function LadderGUI:Start()

end

function LadderGUI:Init()
	
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
	
	NetworkController.Connect('OpenLadder', function(open)
		if type(open) == "boolean" then
			if open == true then
				LadderGUI:Enable()
			else
				LadderGUI:Disable()
			end
		end
	end)
	
	PlayerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui");

	TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
	
	ContextActionService = game:GetService("ContextActionService")

	CanTween = true

	OpenPosition = UDim2.new(0.5,0,0.5,0)
	ClosedPosition = UDim2.new(0.5,0,1.5,0)
	
	Connections = {};
end

return LadderGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/LicenseLookupGUI.lua ---

--[[
    LicenseLookupGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- License Lookup Controller
-- Khizzer
-- June 18, 2021



local LicenseLookupGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local LicenseDataGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui.licenseDatabaseGUI;
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.7);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local mainFrame = LicenseDataGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local WhitelistedTeams;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local username = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame.NameLabel
local carModel = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame.ModelLabel
local carColour = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame.ColourFrame

function LicenseLookupGUI:Toggle()
	if LicenseDataGUI.Enabled == false then
		LicenseDataGUI.Enabled = true
        mainFrame.Visible = true;
        openTween:Play();
    else
		closeTween:Play();
		LicenseDataGUI.Enabled = false
        closeTween.Completed:Wait();
        mainFrame.Visible = false;
        username.Text = 'Username: ';
        carModel.Text = 'Car Model: ';
        carColour.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
    end
end


function LicenseLookupGUI:Start()

    if not WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(localPlayer) then
        LicenseDataGUI.Enabled = false;
    end

    localPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(function()
        if not WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(localPlayer) then
            LicenseDataGUI.Enabled = false;
        end
    end)

    bodyFrame.SearchBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local response = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('LicenseDataLookup', bodyFrame.PlateBoxImage.PlateBox.Text)
        if response == nil then
            _G.AeroError('That plate wasn\'t found in the database!');
            return;
        end;

        username.Text = 'Username: '..response.Owner;
        carModel.Text = 'Car Model: '..response.CarType;
        carColour.BackgroundColor3 = response.Color
    end)

    mainFrame.BodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(self.Toggle)

end

function LicenseLookupGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification
end


return LicenseLookupGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/LogsGUI.lua ---

--[[
    LogsGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- LogsGUI
-- Khizzer
-- August 25, 2023

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService')

local NetworkFunctionController;
local Trove;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local logsGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('LogsGUI');
local mainFrame = logsGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local logsFrame = bodyFrame.LogsFrame;
local logLabel = bodyFrame.LogLabel;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local nextBtn = btnsFrame.NextBtn;
local prevBtn = btnsFrame.PrevBtn;
local refreshBtn = btnsFrame.RefreshBtn;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;


local components = logsGUI.Components;
local logPrefab = components.Log;

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local logsTrove;

local currentPage = 1;

local LogsGUI = {}

local logPages = {}

function LogsGUI:_shiftToPage(logType, pageNumber: number)
    local page = logPages[pageNumber];

    if not page then return; end;

    for _,v in logsFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('TextLabel') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for _,v in page do
        local log = logPrefab:Clone();
        log.Text = v:gsub('\n', ' ');
        log.Parent = logsFrame;
    end;

    logLabel.Text = `{logType:upper()} - PAGE {pageNumber}`;
    currentPage = pageNumber;

    nextBtn.Visible = not (pageNumber == #logPages)
    prevBtn.Visible = pageNumber > 1;
end

function LogsGUI:_requestLogs(logType: string, refresh: boolean)
    local logs = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('RequestLogs', logType);

    if not logs then logs = {}; end;

    -- Split logs into pages of 200 elements each (leaving 25 pages)
    local page = 1;
    local pageTbl = {};

    for _,v in logs do
        table.insert(pageTbl, v);
        if #pageTbl >= 200 then
            logPages[page] = pageTbl;
            page += 1;
            pageTbl = {};
        end;
    end;
    if #pageTbl < 200 then
        logPages[page] = pageTbl;
    end;

    if refresh then
        self:_shiftToPage(logType, 1);
    end;
end

function LogsGUI:Enable(logType)
    logsGUI.Enabled = true;

    if logsTrove then
        logsTrove:Destroy();
    else
        logsTrove = Trove.new();
    end;

    openTween:Play();

    self:_requestLogs(logType);

    self:_shiftToPage(logType, 1);

    logsTrove:Add(nextBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:_shiftToPage(logType, currentPage + 1);
    end));

    logsTrove:Add(prevBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:_shiftToPage(logType, currentPage - 1);
    end));

    logsTrove:Add(refreshBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:_requestLogs(logType, true);
    end));

    logsTrove:Add(exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end))
end

function LogsGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    logsGUI.Enabled = false;

    logsTrove:Destroy();
    logsTrove = nil;
end

function LogsGUI:Start()

end

function LogsGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end


return LogsGUI

--[[

]]
-- Medic GearGUI
-- Khizzer
-- March 04, 2024



local MedicGearGUI = {}

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local NetworkController;
local Trove;

local GuiTrove;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local medicGearGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('MedicGearGUI');
local mainFrame = medicGearGUI.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local controlsImage = bodyFrame.ControlsImage;
local controlsScrollingFrame = controlsImage.ControlsScrollingFrame;
local crouchBtn: ImageButton = controlsScrollingFrame.CrouchBtn;
local glovesBtn: ImageButton = controlsScrollingFrame.GlovesBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local MEDICAL_TEAMS = {'Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service', 'Vancouver Coastal Health', 'British Columbia Ambulance Service'};

local crouchTrack: AnimationTrack;
local isCrouched = false;

local btnHandlers = {
    CrouchBtn = function()
        if isCrouched then
            crouchTrack:Stop();
            isCrouched = false;
        else
            crouchTrack:Play();
            isCrouched = true;
        end;
    end;
    GlovesBtn = function()
        NetworkController.Send('MedicGear', 'Gloves');
    end;
}

function MedicGearGUI:Enable()
    if not GuiTrove then GuiTrove = Trove.new(); end;

    medicGearGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    crouchBtn:SetAttribute('Enabled', isCrouched);
    glovesBtn:SetAttribute('Enabled', localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('MedicGloves') and true or false);

    for _,v in {crouchBtn, glovesBtn} do
        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local defaultTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(v, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then return; end;

            hoverTween:Play();
        end));

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then return; end;

            defaultTween:Play();
        end));

        GuiTrove:Add(v.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            v:SetAttribute('Enabled', not v:GetAttribute('Enabled'));

            task.defer(function()
                if v:GetAttribute('Enabled') then
                    selectedTween:Play();
                else
                    defaultTween:Play();
                end;
            end)

            local func = btnHandlers[v.Name];
            func();
        end));
    end;

    GuiTrove:Add(exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end))
end;

function MedicGearGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        medicGearGUI.Enabled = false;
        if GuiTrove then
            GuiTrove:Clean();
            GuiTrove = nil;
        end;
    end)
end;

function MedicGearGUI:CharacterAdded(char)
    self:Disable();

    if table.find(MEDICAL_TEAMS, localPlayer.Team.Name) or localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") == "12VFA" then
        local humanoid: Humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
        if crouchTrack then crouchTrack:Destroy(); end;
        crouchTrack = humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(crouchBtn.CrouchAnimation);
        isCrouched = false;
    end;
end;

function MedicGearGUI:Toggle()
    if medicGearGUI.Enabled then
        self:Disable();
    else
        self:Enable();
    end;
end

function MedicGearGUI:Start()

end

function MedicGearGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end;


return MedicGearGUI

if game.GameId == 2662277337 then return {}; end;

local StarterPlayer = game:GetService('StarterPlayer');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

function NameHideGUI:CharacterAdded(_char: Model)
    humanoid = _char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');

    toggleBtnLabel.Text = 'Hide';
    statusLabel.Text = 'NAME IS SHOWING';
end

function NameHideGUI:Enable()
    nameHideGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    if not GuiTrove then
        GuiTrove = Trove.new();
    end;

    if humanoid.DisplayName == " " then
        toggleBtnLabel.Text = 'Show';
        statusLabel.Text = 'NAME IS HIDDEN';
    else
        toggleBtnLabel.Text = 'Hide';
        statusLabel.Text = 'NAME IS SHOWING';
    end;

    GuiTrove:Add(humanoid:GetPropertyChangedSignal('DisplayName'):Connect(function()
        if humanoid.DisplayName == " " then
            toggleBtnLabel.Text = 'Show';
            statusLabel.Text = 'NAME IS HIDDEN';
        else
            toggleBtnLabel.Text = 'Hide';
            statusLabel.Text = 'NAME IS SHOWING';
        end;
    end));

    GuiTrove:Add(toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('ToggleNameHide');
    end));

    GuiTrove:Add(exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end));
end;

function NameHideGUI:Disable()
    if GuiTrove then
        GuiTrove:Destroy();
        GuiTrove = nil;
    end;

    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        nameHideGUI.Enabled = false;
    end);
end;

function NameHideGUI:Toggle()
    if nameHideGUI.Enabled then
        self:Disable();
    else
        self:Enable();
    end;
end;

function NameHideGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/Notification.lua ---

--[[
    Notification (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TextService = game:GetService('TextService');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local DEFAULT_SIZE = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0);
local TWEEN_TIME = 0.33;

local COLOURS = {
    Blue = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
    Red = Color3.fromRGB(245, 54, 54);
    Green = Color3.fromRGB(81, 181, 100);
    Black = Color3.fromRGB(21, 21, 21);
    Yellow = Color3.fromRGB(245, 178, 61);
    Purple = Color3.fromRGB(133, 71, 158);
    PhoneOrange = Color3.fromRGB(170, 137, 53);
}

local bottomLeftGUI = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('BottomLeftGUI');
local UIScale = bottomLeftGUI.UIScale;
local mainFrame = bottomLeftGUI.MainFrame.NotificationFrame;

local components = bottomLeftGUI.Components;
local notificationFramePrefab = components.NotificationFrame;
local TITLE_SIZE = notificationFramePrefab.TitleLabel.TextSize;
local MIDDLE_PADDING = notificationFramePrefab.DescLabel.AbsolutePosition.Y - (notificationFramePrefab.TitleLabel.AbsolutePosition.Y + TITLE_SIZE);

local Notification = {};

function Notification.new(title, desc, image, colour)
    local notificationFrame = notificationFramePrefab:Clone();
    local descLabel = notificationFrame.DescLabel;
    notificationFrame.Size = DEFAULT_SIZE;
    notificationFrame.TitleLabel.Text = title;
    descLabel.Text = desc;
    if image then
        notificationFrame.ImageLabel.Image = image;
    end;

    if colour then
        colour = COLOURS[colour];
    else
        colour = COLOURS['Blue'];
    end;

    notificationFrame.TopBarFrame.ImageColor3 = colour
    notificationFrame.Parent = mainFrame;

    task.defer(function()
        local ySize = descLabel.TextBounds.Y / UIScale.Scale;
    
        local openTween = TweenService:Create(notificationFrame, TweenInfo.new(TWEEN_TIME), {Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, ySize + 35)});
        openTween:Play();

        task.spawn(function()
            openTween.Completed:Wait();

            local waitTime = (#desc * 0.1) + 1;
            task.wait(waitTime);

            local closeTween = TweenService:Create(notificationFrame, TweenInfo.new(TWEEN_TIME), {Size = DEFAULT_SIZE});
            closeTween:Play();
            closeTween.Completed:Wait();
            notificationFrame:Destroy();
        end);
    end)
end;

function Notification:Start()
    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('Notification', function(...)
        self.new(...);
    end);
end;

function Notification:Init()
end;

return Notification;

--[[
    PatrolLogGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Patrol LogGUI
-- Khizzer
-- December 9, 2022



local PatrolLogGUI = {}

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local patrolLogGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('PatrolLogGUI');
local mainFrame = patrolLogGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local informationFrame = bodyFrame.InformationFrame;
local startLabel = informationFrame.StartLabel;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local logBtn = btnsFrame.LogBtn;
local logLabel = logBtn.LogLabel;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;
local ListenerList;
local GuiListeners;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function PatrolLogGUI:_startShiftLog()
    --Makes sure vServices is actually up
    local serverAlive: boolean = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('PatrolLogHandshake');
    if not serverAlive then
        _G.AeroError('vServices is down. Please try again later.');
        return;
    end;

    local suc = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('StartPatrolLog');
    if suc then
        local startTime = DateTime.now():FormatLocalTime('LT', 'en-us');
        startLabel.Text = 'START TIME ' .. startTime;
        logLabel.Text = '10-7';
    else
        _G.AeroError('Error while starting patrol log. Please try again later.');
    end;
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:_endShiftLog()
    local suc = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('EndPatrolLog');
    if suc then
        local endTime = DateTime.now():FormatLocalTime('LT', 'en-us');
        startLabel.Text = 'END TIME ' .. endTime;
        logLabel.Text = '10-8';
        task.delay(5, function()
            startLabel.Text = 'START TIME: N/A';
        end)
    else
        _G.AeroError('Error while ending patrol log. Please try again later or take a picture of this error as proof of end time.');
    end;
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:Enable()
    if self._enabled then return end;

    patrolLogGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();
    openTween.Completed:Wait();
    self._enabled = true;

    if not GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;

    GuiListeners:Connect(logBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if logLabel.Text == '10-8' then
            self:_startShiftLog();
        else
            self:_endShiftLog();
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(exitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        self:Disable();
    end)
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:Disable()
    if not self._enabled then return end;

    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    self._enabled = false;
    patrolLogGUI.Enabled = false;

    if GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners:DisconnectAll();
    end;
    GuiListeners = nil;
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('ResetPatrolLogGUI', function()
        logLabel.Text = '10-8'
        startLabel.Text = 'START TIME: N/A';
    end)
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:Toggle()
    if self._enabled then
        self:Disable();
    else
        self:Enable();
    end;
end;

function PatrolLogGUI:Init()
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    self._enabled = patrolLogGUI.Enabled;
end;


return PatrolLogGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/PhoneGUI.lua ---

--[[
    PhoneGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TextChatService = game:GetService('TextChatService');
local TextService = game:GetService('TextService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

-- PhoneGui
-- Automationeer


local PhoneGUI = {}

local NetworkController
local Error
local Notification
local Trove
local InventoryGUI;

local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm)
local ClientComm = Comm.ClientComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, false, "PhoneNetwork")
local BusinessProperty = ClientComm:GetProperty("CallableBusinesses")

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23)
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159)

local SERVICES = {
    { "911", "Emergency" },
    -- { "Automobile Association", "BCAA" },
    -- { "TransLink Taxi", "Taxi" },
}

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
local phoneGUI: ScreenGui = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('PhoneGUI')

local PhoneTrove

local MainFrame = phoneGUI:FindFirstChild("MainFrame") :: Frame
local Components = phoneGUI:FindFirstChild("Components") :: Configuration

-- TODO: Listen for chat events

local BodyFrame = MainFrame.BodyFrame :: Frame
local BtnsFrame = BodyFrame.BtnsFrame :: Frame
local TipLabel = BodyFrame.TipLabel :: TextLabel

local NumberTemplate = Components.NumberBtn :: ImageButton
local MessageTemplate = Components.MessageLabel :: TextLabel

local frames = {
    NumbersList = BodyFrame.NumbersListFrame :: Frame,
    MessageList = BodyFrame.MessageListFrame :: Frame,
    Emergency = BodyFrame.EmergencyFrame :: Frame,
    CallerSplash = BodyFrame.CallerSplashFrame :: Frame & {
        AvatarImage: ImageLabel,
        CallerName: TextLabel,
    },
}

local tips = {
    [frames.NumbersList] = "CONTACTS",
    [frames.MessageList] = "CALL MESSAGES",
    [frames.Emergency] = "911 EMERGENCY",
    [frames.CallerSplash] = "INCOMING CALL",
}

local useButtons = {
    [frames.NumbersList] = { BtnsFrame.CloseBtn, BtnsFrame.CallBtn },
    [frames.MessageList] = { BtnsFrame.HangUpBtn },
    [frames.Emergency] = { BtnsFrame.HangUpBtn, BtnsFrame.CallBtn },
    [frames.CallerSplash] = { BtnsFrame.AcceptBtn, BtnsFrame.DeclineBtn },
}

type CallData = {
    id: string,
    caller: Player,
    target: Player | string,
    staff: Player?, -- business member handling the call
    targetIsPlayer: boolean,
    connected: boolean,
}

local selectedNumber: ImageButton?
local token = "default"
local messageOrder = 0
local activeCall: {
    id: string,
    caller: Player,
    target: Player | string,
    targetIsPlayer: boolean,
}? = nil

local callDebounce = false

local function setFrame(useFrame: Frame)
    for _, frame in frames do
        frame.Visible = useFrame == frame
    end

    for _, btn in BtnsFrame:GetChildren() do
        if btn:IsA("GuiButton") then
            btn.Visible = if table.find(useButtons[useFrame], btn) then true else false
        end
    end

    TipLabel.Text = tips[useFrame]
end

local function pruneFrame(frame: Frame)
    for _, obj in frame:GetChildren() do
        if obj:IsA("GuiButton") or obj:IsA("GuiLabel") then
            obj:Destroy()
        end
    end
end

local function insertNumber(text: string, order: number, class: string, target: string)
    local btn = NumberTemplate:Clone()
    btn.Name = `{class}_{target}`
    btn.LayoutOrder = order
    btn.NumberLabel.Text = text
    btn:SetAttribute("Class", class)
    btn:SetAttribute("Target", target)

    local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR})
	local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR})
	local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(btn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR})

    btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if selectedNumber ~= btn then
            hoverTween:Play()
        end
    end)
    btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if selectedNumber ~= btn then
            hoverEndTween:Play()
        end
    end)
    btn.Activated:Connect(function()
        if selectedNumber == btn then
            selectedNumber = nil
            hoverEndTween:Play()
            return
        end

        local tween: Tween?
        if selectedNumber then
            tween = TweenService:Create(selectedNumber, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            (tween :: Tween).Completed:Connect(function()
                (tween :: Tween):Destroy()
            end)
        end

        selectedNumber = btn
        selectedTween:Play()
        if tween then
            tween:Play()
        end
    end)

    -- possibly redundant? can't remember if tweens destroy when the instance does since their parents are nil (iirc)
    btn.Destroying:Connect(function()
        hoverTween:Destroy()
        hoverEndTween:Destroy()
        selectedTween:Destroy()
    end)

    btn.Parent = frames.NumbersList.NumbersListScrollingFrame
end

local function goToMessageList()
    messageOrder = 0
    pruneFrame(frames.MessageList.MessageListScrollingFrame)
    setFrame(frames.MessageList)
end

local function insertMessage(text: string, isLocalPlayer: boolean)
    local messageListScrollingFrame: ScrollingFrame = frames.MessageList.MessageListScrollingFrame;

    local clone = MessageTemplate:Clone()
    clone.Visible = false
    clone.Parent = messageListScrollingFrame;
    local textSize = TextService:GetTextSize(text, clone.TextSize, clone.Font, Vector2.new(clone.AbsoluteSize.X, math.huge))
    clone.Size = UDim2.new(clone.Size.X.Scale, clone.Size.X.Offset, 0, textSize.Y + 8)
    clone.Text = text

    clone.BackgroundColor3 = isLocalPlayer and Color3.fromRGB(63, 126, 194) or Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)

    messageOrder += 1
    clone.LayoutOrder = messageOrder
    clone.Visible = true

    messageListScrollingFrame.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, messageListScrollingFrame.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y - messageListScrollingFrame.AbsoluteSize.Y);
end

local function populateNumbers()
    pruneFrame(frames.NumbersList.NumbersListScrollingFrame)
    selectedNumber = nil
    local i = 0

    for _, v in SERVICES do
        insertNumber(v[1], i, "Service", v[2])
        i += 1
    end

    for _, business in (BusinessProperty:Get() or {}) do
        insertNumber(business, i, "Business", business)
        i += 1
    end

    for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
        if player == localPlayer then
            continue
        end
        insertNumber(player.Name, i, "Player", player.Name)
        i += 1
    end
end

local function startCall()
    if not selectedNumber then
        return
    end

    if selectedNumber.Name == "Service_Emergency" then
        setFrame(frames.Emergency)
    else
        local callClass = selectedNumber:GetAttribute("Class")
        local callTarget = selectedNumber:GetAttribute("Target")

        if callClass == "Player" then
            callTarget = Players:FindFirstChild(callTarget)
        elseif callClass ~= "Business" then
            error(`Invalid call class {callClass} for target {callTarget}`)
        end

        token = `ct{HttpService:GenerateGUID()}`
        callDebounce = true
        NetworkController.Send("CALL_REQUEST", callTarget, token)
        goToMessageList()
        insertMessage(`Calling {callTarget}...`)
    end
end

function PhoneGUI:Close()
    local humanoid = localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        humanoid:UnequipTools()
    end
end

function PhoneGUI:Enable()
    if not PhoneTrove then PhoneTrove = Trove.new() end

    if frames.NumbersList.Visible == true then
        populateNumbers()
    end

    PhoneTrove:Add(BtnsFrame.CallBtn.Activated:Connect(function()
        if frames.NumbersList.Visible == true then
            startCall()
        else
            local details = frames.Emergency.DetailsImage.DetailsBox.Text
            local location = frames.Emergency.LocationImage.LocationBox.Text

            if #details < 5 then
                Error("Details are too short")
                return
            end
            if #location < 5 then
                Error("Location is too short")
                return
            end

            NetworkController.Send("911_CALL", location, details)
            PhoneGUI:Close()
            setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
        end
    end))

    PhoneTrove:Add(BtnsFrame.HangUpBtn.Activated:Connect(function()
        if frames.Emergency.Visible == true then
            setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
            populateNumbers()
        elseif not callDebounce then
            if activeCall then
                NetworkController.Send("CALL_END", activeCall.id)
                activeCall = nil
            end
            token = `ct_void{HttpService:GenerateGUID()}`
            setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
            populateNumbers()
        end
    end))

    PhoneTrove:Add(BtnsFrame.CloseBtn.Activated:Connect(function()
        PhoneGUI:Close()
    end))

    PhoneTrove:Add(BtnsFrame.AcceptBtn.Activated:Connect(function()
        if activeCall then
            goToMessageList()
            NetworkController.Send("call_accept", activeCall.id)
            insertMessage(`Answered call from {activeCall.caller.Name}`)
            InventoryGUI.FlashPhone(false);
        else
            setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
            populateNumbers()
        end
    end))

    PhoneTrove:Add(BtnsFrame.DeclineBtn.Activated:Connect(function()
        if activeCall then
            NetworkController.Send("call_decline", activeCall.id)
            activeCall = nil
            InventoryGUI.FlashPhone(false);
        end
        setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
        populateNumbers()
        PhoneGUI:Close()
    end))

    PhoneTrove:Add(TextChatService.SendingMessage:Connect(function(textChatMessage)
        local text = textChatMessage.Text:gsub("&amp;", "&"):gsub("&lt;", "<"):gsub("&gt;", ">"):gsub('&quot;', '"'):gsub("&apos;", "'")
        if activeCall then
            NetworkController.Send("CALL_MESSAGE", activeCall.id, text)
        end
    end))

    phoneGUI.Enabled = true
end

function PhoneGUI:Disable()
    phoneGUI.Enabled = false

    selectedNumber = nil
    if frames.Emergency.Visible == false then
        frames.Emergency.DetailsImage.DetailsBox.Text = ""
        frames.Emergency.LocationImage.LocationBox.Text = ""
    end

    if PhoneTrove then PhoneTrove:Clean() end
    pruneFrame(frames.NumbersList.NumbersListScrollingFrame)
end

function PhoneGUI:Start()
    setFrame(frames.NumbersList)

    NetworkController.Connect("call_failed", function(t)
        if token == t then
            insertMessage("Call failed.")
            callDebounce = false
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("call_busy", function(t)
        if token == t then
            insertMessage("The line is busy.")
            callDebounce = false
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("call_dialing", function(t, p)
        if token == t then
            callDebounce = false
            activeCall = p
            insertMessage(`Ringing...`)
        else
            NetworkController.Send("CALL_END", p.id)
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("CALL_INCOMING", function(callData: CallData)
        activeCall = callData;
        Notification('Incoming Call', 'You have an incoming call', nil, 'PhoneOrange')
        InventoryGUI.FlashPhone(true)

        setFrame(frames.CallerSplash)
        local caller = callData.caller;

        local succ, res = pcall(Players.GetUserThumbnailAsync, Players, caller.UserId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420);
        if succ then
            frames.CallerSplash.AvatarImage.Image = res;
        end;

        frames.CallerSplash.CallerName.Text = caller.Name;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('BUSINESS_CALL', function(callData: CallData)
        activeCall = callData;

        setFrame(frames.MessageList);
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("CALL_CONNECT", function(id)
        if activeCall and activeCall.id == id then
            insertMessage("Call is connected.")
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("CALL_REFUSED", function(id)
        if activeCall and activeCall.id == id then
            insertMessage("Call declined.")
            callDebounce = false
            activeCall = nil
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("CALL_MESSAGE", function(id, message, isLocalPlayer)
        if activeCall and id == activeCall.id then
            insertMessage(message, isLocalPlayer)
            -- TODO: Flash inventory if tool unequipped
        else
            NetworkController.Send("CALL_END", id)
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect("CALL_END", function(id, skipMessage)
        if activeCall and id == activeCall.id then
            InventoryGUI.FlashPhone(false);

            if frames.CallerSplash.Visible == true then
                callDebounce = false
                activeCall = nil
                setFrame(frames.NumbersList)
                populateNumbers()
                return
            end

            if skipMessage ~= false then
                insertMessage("Call ended.")
            end
            callDebounce = false
            activeCall = nil
        end
    end)

    self.Modules.UI.Draggable.new(phoneGUI, MainFrame.TopBarFrame, MainFrame)
end

function PhoneGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController
    Error = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI.Error
    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new
    InventoryGUI = self.Controllers.UI.InventoryGUI;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove
end

return PhoneGUI



================================================================================

--[[
    PlayerLookupGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56

-- Player LookupGUI
-- Khizzer
-- July 11, 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local ACTIVE_WITH_DETAILS_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.4, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local RecordService;

local PlayerLookupGUI = {}

local WhitelistedTeams;
local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local LocalPlayers = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer;
local playerGUI = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerGui');
local playerDatabaseGUI = playerGUI:WaitForChild('PlayerDatabaseGUI');
local mainFrame = playerDatabaseGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local boloReasonBox = btnsFrame.ReasonBoxImage.ReasonBox;
local setBoloBtn = btnsFrame.SetBoloBtn;
local removeBoloBtn = btnsFrame.RemoveBoloBtn;

local OpenTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION})
local CloseTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION})

local searchBtn = bodyFrame.SearchBtn;

local detailsFrame = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local arrestsListFrame: ScrollingFrame = detailsFrame.ArrestsListImage.ArrestsListScrollingFrame;
local citationsListFrame: ScrollingFrame = detailsFrame.CitationsListImage.CitationsListScrollingFrame;
local nameLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.NameLabel;
local boloLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.BoloLabel;
local warrantLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.WarrantLabel;
local arrestCountLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.ArrestCountLabel;
local citationCountLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.CitationCountLabel;
local speedingFineLabel: TextLabel = detailsFrame.SpeedingFineLabel;
local avatarImage: ImageLabel = detailsFrame.AvatarImage;

local extraDetailsFrame = bodyFrame.ExtraDetailsFrame;
local officerLabel = extraDetailsFrame.OfficerLabel;
local officerTeamLabel = extraDetailsFrame.TeamLabel;
local chargesLabel = extraDetailsFrame.ChargesLabel;
local sentenceLengthLabel = extraDetailsFrame.LengthLabel;
local descriptionLabel = extraDetailsFrame.DescriptionLabel;
local exitExtraDetailsBtn = extraDetailsFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local usernameBox = bodyFrame.UsernameBoxImage.UsernameBox;

local components = playerDatabaseGUI.Components;
local recordBtnPrefab = components.RecordBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local extraDetailsTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_WITH_DETAILS_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local selectedBtn;
local isLEO;

local extraDetailsExitConnection;

local searchedPlayer;

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize(frame)
    frame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#frame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
end;

local function updateChargesLabel(charges)
    if #charges == 0 then
        chargesLabel.Text = 'No charges inputted'
    -- elseif #charges <= 3 then
    --     chargesLabel.Text = 'Charges: \n'..table.concat(charges, '\n')
    else
        chargesLabel.Text = `Charges ({#charges}): `..table.concat(charges, '; ')
    end
end;

local connections = {};

function PlayerLookupGUI:IsEnabled()
    return playerDatabaseGUI.Enabled == true
end

function PlayerLookupGUI:Toggle()
	if playerDatabaseGUI.Enabled == false then
		playerDatabaseGUI.Enabled = true
        mainFrame.Visible = true;
        OpenTween:Play();
        if isLEO and LocalPlayers:GetAttribute("Division") ~= 'GCPS' then
            table.insert(connections, setBoloBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                if #boloReasonBox.Text < 3 then
                    _G.AeroError('Bolo reason must be at least 3 characters long.');
                    return;
                end;

                NetworkController.Send('SetBolo', searchedPlayer, boloReasonBox.Text);
                removeBoloBtn.Visible = true;
                setBoloBtn.Visible = false;
                boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = false;
            end));
        end
	else
		playerDatabaseGUI.Enabled = false
        CloseTween:Play();
        CloseTween.Completed:Wait();
        mainFrame.Visible = false;
        for _,v in next, connections do
            v:Disconnect();
            v = nil;
        end;
        connections = {};
        selectedBtn = nil;
        extraDetailsFrame.Visible = false;
        nameLabel.Text = 'Username: ';
        arrestCountLabel.Text = 'Arrest Count: ';
        citationCountLabel.Text = 'Citation Count: ';
        boloLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Bolo: ' else '';
        warrantLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Warrant: ' else '';
        avatarImage.Image = '';
        removeBoloBtn.Visible = false;
        setBoloBtn.Visible = false;
        boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = false;
        for _,v in next, arrestsListFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
        end;
        for _,v in next, citationsListFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
        end;
    end
end

function PlayerLookupGUI:Render(data, username: string)
    if data == 'Not found' then return; end;
    searchedPlayer = username;

    for _,v in next, arrestsListFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
    end

    for _,v in next, citationsListFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
    end;


    local function getSortedIndexes(dataIndex: string): {}
        local sortedIndexes = {};

        for index,record in next, data[dataIndex] or {} do
            sortedIndexes[#sortedIndexes + 1] = index;
        end;

        table.sort(sortedIndexes, function(a, b)
            local firstDate = data[dataIndex][a]['Date'];
            local secondDate = data[dataIndex][b]['Date'];

            local firstDateSplit = string.split(firstDate, '/');
            local secondDateSplit = string.split(secondDate, '/');

            local firstDateTime = DateTime.fromUniversalTime(tonumber(firstDateSplit[3]), tonumber(firstDateSplit[1]), tonumber(firstDateSplit[2]));
            local secondDateTime = DateTime.fromUniversalTime(tonumber(secondDateSplit[3]), tonumber(secondDateSplit[1]), tonumber(secondDateSplit[2]));

            return firstDateTime.UnixTimestamp > secondDateTime.UnixTimestamp;
        end);

        return sortedIndexes;
    end;


    for _,v in next, getSortedIndexes('ArrestRecord') do
        local record = data['ArrestRecord'][v];
        local recordBtn = recordBtnPrefab:Clone()
        recordBtn.Parent = arrestsListFrame;
        recordBtn.RecordText.Text = tostring(record['Length'])..'s/'..record['Date'];

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        recordBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        recordBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);

        recordBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play()
                selectedBtn = nil;
            end

            selectedBtn = recordBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
            extraDetailsTween:Play();

            extraDetailsFrame.Visible = true;

            officerLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Officer: '..record['Officer'] else '';
            officerTeamLabel.Text = 'Officer Team: '..record['OfficerTeam'];
            updateChargesLabel(record['Offences']);
            sentenceLengthLabel.Text = 'Sentence Length (s): '..tostring(record['Length']);
            descriptionLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Desc. of Incident: \n'..record['Details'] else ''
        end)

        if not extraDetailsExitConnection then
            extraDetailsExitConnection = exitExtraDetailsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                openTween:Play();
                extraDetailsFrame.Visible = false;
            end);
        end;
    end;

    nameLabel.Text = 'Username: ' .. username;
    arrestCountLabel.Text = 'Arrest Count: '.. tostring(#getSortedIndexes('ArrestRecord'));
    citationCountLabel.Text = 'Citation Count: '.. tostring(#getSortedIndexes('CitationRecord'));

    for _,v in next, getSortedIndexes('CitationRecord') do
        local record = data['CitationRecord'][v];
        local recordBtn = recordBtnPrefab:Clone()
        recordBtn.Parent = citationsListFrame;
        recordBtn.RecordText.Text = '$' .. tostring(record['Price'])..'/'..record['Date'];

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(recordBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        recordBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        recordBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);

        recordBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            if selectedBtn == recordBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play()
                selectedBtn = nil;
            end

            selectedBtn = recordBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
            extraDetailsTween:Play();

            extraDetailsFrame.Visible = true;

            officerLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Officer: '..record['Officer'] else '';
            officerTeamLabel.Text = 'Officer Team: '..record['OfficerTeam'];
            updateChargesLabel(record['Offences']);
            sentenceLengthLabel.Text = 'Cited amount (CA$): '..tostring(record['Price']);
            descriptionLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Desc. of Incident: \n'..record['Details'] else '';
        end)

        if not extraDetailsExitConnection then
            extraDetailsExitConnection = exitExtraDetailsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                openTween:Play();
                extraDetailsFrame.Visible = false;
            end);
        end;
    end;

    local boloData = data['Bolo'];

    if isLEO and boloData.SetBy then
        boloLabel.Text = 'Bolo: '.. boloData.SetBy ..'/'.. boloData.Details;
        removeBoloBtn.Visible = true;
        setBoloBtn.Visible = false;
        boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = false;
        table.insert(connections, removeBoloBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
            NetworkController.Send('RemoveBolo', searchedPlayer);
            removeBoloBtn.Visible = false;
            setBoloBtn.Visible = true;
            boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = true;
        end))
    elseif isLEO then
        removeBoloBtn.Visible = false;
        setBoloBtn.Visible = true;
        boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = true;
        boloLabel.Text = 'Bolo: NONE';
    end;

    if isLEO and data['Warrant'] == 'No' then
        warrantLabel.Text = 'Warrant: NONE';
    elseif isLEO then
        warrantLabel.Text = 'Warrant: '..data['Warrant'];
    end

    speedingFineLabel.Text = `Speeding Fine: ${data['SpeedingFine']}`;

    local suc, _err = pcall(function()
        local userId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(usernameBox.Text);
        if userId then
            avatarImage.Image = Players:GetUserThumbnailAsync(userId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size420x420);
        end
    end)

    if not suc then avatarImage.Image = ''; end;
end

function PlayerLookupGUI:Start()

    local function update()
        if isLEO ~= WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(LocalPlayers) or LocalPlayers:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' then
            playerDatabaseGUI.Enabled = false;
            isLEO = WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(LocalPlayers) or LocalPlayers:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS';
            CloseTween:Play();
            mainFrame.Visible = false;
            for _,v in next, connections do
                v:Disconnect();
                v = nil;
            end;
            connections = {};
            selectedBtn = nil;
            extraDetailsFrame.Visible = false;
            nameLabel.Text = 'Username: ';
            arrestCountLabel.Text = 'Arrest Count: ';
            citationCountLabel.Text = 'Citation Count: ';
            boloLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Bolo: ' else '';
            warrantLabel.Text = if isLEO then 'Warrant: ' else '';
            avatarImage.Image = '';
            bodyFrame.UsernameBoxImage.Visible = isLEO
            bodyFrame.PlayerLabel.Visible = isLEO
            bodyFrame.SearchBtn.Visible = isLEO
            removeBoloBtn.Visible = false;
            setBoloBtn.Visible = false;
            boloReasonBox.Parent.Visible = false;
            for _,v in next, arrestsListFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
            end;
            for _,v in next, citationsListFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then v:Destroy(); end;
            end;
        end
    end

    LocalPlayers:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(update)
    LocalPlayers:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Division'):Connect(update)
    update()

    searchBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        if usernameBox.Text == '' then return; end;
        if not isLEO then return; end;
        local data = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('DatabaseLookup', usernameBox.Text); --This yields
        self:Render(data, game.Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(game.Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(usernameBox.Text)))
    end)

	exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(self.Toggle)

end;



function PlayerLookupGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
end


return PlayerLookupGUI
