--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/ProtestSignGUI.lua ---

--[[
    ProtestSignGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Protest SignGUI
-- Khizzer
-- January 20, 2022



local ProtestSignGUI = {}
local ListenerList;
local MainListeners;
local SidebarListeners;
local NetworkController;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local protestSignGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('ProtestSignGUI');

local mainFrame = protestSignGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local colourFrame = bodyFrame.ColourFrame;
local colourWheel = colourFrame.ColourWheel;
local colourPreview = colourFrame.ColourPreview;
local darknessSlider = colourFrame.DarknessSlider;
local slider = darknessSlider.Slider;

local textFrame = bodyFrame.TextFrame;
local fontsBtn = textFrame.FontBtn;
local fontsImage = fontsBtn.FontsImage;
local fontsScrollingFrame = fontsImage.FontsScrollingFrame;
local textBoxImage = textFrame.TextBoxImage;
local textBox = textBoxImage.TextBox;

local sidebarImage = bodyFrame.SidebarImage;
local sidebarBtnList = sidebarImage.SidebarScrollingFrame;
local textBtn = sidebarBtnList.TextBtn;
local backgroundBtn =  sidebarBtnList.BackgroundBtn;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local submitBtn = btnsFrame.SubmitBtn;

local components = protestSignGUI.Components;
local fontBtnPreFab = components.FontBtn;

local selectedCategory;

local function toPolar(v)
	return math.atan2(v.y, v.x), v.magnitude;
end;

local function radToDeg(x)
	return ((x + math.pi) / (2 * math.pi)) * 360;
end;

local hue, saturation, value = 0, 0, 1;

local function UpdateSelector(mouseX, mouseY)
    local radius = colourWheel.AbsoluteSize.x/2;
    local d = Vector2.new(mouseX, mouseY) - colourWheel.AbsolutePosition - colourWheel.AbsoluteSize/2;

    if (d:Dot(d) > radius*radius) then
		d = d.unit * radius;
	end
	
	colourWheel.Selector.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, d.x, 0.5, d.y);
	
	local phi, len = toPolar(d * Vector2.new(1, -1));
	hue, saturation = radToDeg(phi)/360, len / radius;
	darknessSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, 1);
	
	colourPreview.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, value);
end;

local function UpdateSlider(mouseX, mouseY)
    local rY = mouseY - darknessSlider.AbsolutePosition.y;
	local cY = math.clamp(rY, 0, darknessSlider.AbsoluteSize.y - slider.AbsoluteSize.y);
	slider.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0, cY);

	value = 1 - (cY / (darknessSlider.AbsoluteSize.y - slider.AbsoluteSize.y));

    colourPreview.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(hue, saturation, value);
end

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    fontsScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#fontsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
end;

local selectedFont;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local submitConnection;
local exitConnection;

function ProtestSignGUI:Enable()
    openTween:Play();

    if not SidebarListeners then
        SidebarListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;
    if not MainListeners then
        MainListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end

    if not submitConnection then 
        submitConnection = submitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
            NetworkController.Send('PROTEST_SIGN_CUSTOMISATION', colourPreview.ImageColor3, ((selectedFont and selectedFont.FontLabel.Text) or ('PermanentMarker')), textBox.Text);
        end);
    end;

    if not exitConnection then
        exitConnection = exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(ProtestSignGUI.Disable);
    end

    local textHoverTween = TweenService:Create(textBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local textHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(textBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local textSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(textBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
    
    SidebarListeners:Connect(textBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedCategory == textBtn then return; end;
        textHoverTween:Play();
    end);
    
    SidebarListeners:Connect(textBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedCategory == textBtn then return; end;
        textHoverEndTween:Play();
    end);

    SidebarListeners:Connect(textBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedCategory then
            TweenService:Create(selectedCategory, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end
            
        selectedCategory = textBtn;
        textSelectedTween:Play();

        MainListeners:DisconnectAll();

        colourFrame.Visible = false;
        textFrame.Visible = true;

        local fonts = Enum.Font:GetEnumItems();

        for i,v in next, fonts do
            local font = tostring(v);
            font = (font):split('.')[3];
            fonts[i] = font;
        end;

        for _,v in next, fontsScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        MainListeners:Connect(fontsBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
            fontsImage.Visible = not fontsImage.Visible;
        end)

        for _,v in next, fonts do
            local fontBtn = fontBtnPreFab:Clone();
            fontBtn.Parent = fontsScrollingFrame;
            fontBtn.FontLabel.Text = v;
            fontBtn.FontLabel.Font = Enum.Font[v];

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(fontBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(fontBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(fontBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            MainListeners:Connect(fontBtn.MouseEnter, function()
            if selectedFont == fontBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            MainListeners:Connect(fontBtn.MouseLeave, function()
            if selectedFont == fontBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            MainListeners:Connect(fontBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
            if selectedFont then
                TweenService:Create(selectedFont, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedFont = fontBtn;

            textBox.Font = Enum.Font[v];

            selectedTween:Play();
            end);
        end

        UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    end)

    local backgroundHoverTween = TweenService:Create(backgroundBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local backgroundHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(backgroundBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local backgroundSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(backgroundBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
    
    SidebarListeners:Connect(backgroundBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedCategory == backgroundBtn then return; end;
        backgroundHoverTween:Play();
    end);
    
    SidebarListeners:Connect(backgroundBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedCategory == backgroundBtn then return; end;
        backgroundHoverEndTween:Play();
    end);

    SidebarListeners:Connect(backgroundBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedCategory then
            TweenService:Create(selectedCategory, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end
            
        selectedCategory = backgroundBtn;
        backgroundSelectedTween:Play();

        colourFrame.Visible = true;
        textFrame.Visible = false;

        local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService");
        local Mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse();

        MainListeners:DisconnectAll();

        local WheelDown = false;
        local SliderDown = false;

        MainListeners:Connect(UserInputService.InputEnded, function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                WheelDown = false;
                SliderDown = false;
            end;
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(colourWheel.MouseButton1Down, function()
            WheelDown = true;
            UpdateSelector(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(colourWheel.MouseMoved, function()
            if WheelDown then
                UpdateSelector(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
            end;
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(darknessSlider.MouseButton1Down, function()
            SliderDown = true;
            UpdateSlider(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
        end);

        MainListeners:Connect(darknessSlider.MouseMoved, function()
            if SliderDown then
                UpdateSlider(Mouse.X, Mouse.Y);
            end;
        end);
    end)
end;

function ProtestSignGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    MainListeners:DisconnectAll();
    SidebarListeners:DisconnectAll();

    if exitConnection then exitConnection:Disconnect(); exitConnection = nil; end;
    if submitConnection then submitConnection:Disconnect(); submitConnection = nil; end;
end;

function ProtestSignGUI:Start()
end;

function ProtestSignGUI:Init()
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return ProtestSignGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/RadioGUI.lua ---

--[[
    RadioGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TextService = game:GetService('TextService');

local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local ABSOLUTE_SIZE_X = 360;
local PADDING = 15;

local newUDim2 = UDim2.new;
local newVector2 = Vector2.new;
local transmissionKey = Enum.KeyCode.Semicolon;
local channelCycleKey = Enum.KeyCode.RightBracket;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local radioGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('RadioGUI');
local UIScale = radioGUI.UIScale;

local mainFrame = radioGUI.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;
local settingsBtn = topBarFrame.SettingsBtn;
local channelBtn = topBarFrame.ChannelBtn;
local panicBtn = topBarFrame.PanicBtn;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local messagesFrame = bodyFrame.MessagesFrame;
local UIListLayout = messagesFrame.UIListLayout;
local inputBox: TextBox = bodyFrame.InputBoxImage.InputBox;
local components = radioGUI.Components;
local messageLabelImagePrefab = components.MessageLabelImage;

local settingsFrame = radioGUI.SettingsFrame;
local settingsBodyFrame = settingsFrame.BodyFrame;
local transmissionKeyBtn = settingsBodyFrame.TransmissionKeyBtn;
local transmissionKeyLabel = transmissionKeyBtn.TransmissionKeyLabel;
local channelCycleKeyBtn = settingsBodyFrame.ChannelCycleKeyBtn;
local channelCycleKeyLabel = channelCycleKeyBtn.ChannelCycleKeyLabel;

local toggle = components.Toggle;
local transmission = components.Transmission;
local panicSound = components.Panic;

local radioAnimation;

local radioSendConnection;
local panicConnection;

local currentChannel = 1;
local currentChannelName = 'UNIVERSAL';

local channels = {
	'UNIVERSAL',
	'TAC 1',
	'TAC 2',
	'DISPATCH',
	'FIRE/EMS',
	'CORRECTIONS'
};

local listeners;
local settingsListeners;
local RadioChannels;

local inputEnded = game:GetService('UserInputService').InputEnded;

local function CreateLabel(msg, playTransmissionSound, specialMsgType)
	local messageLabelImage = messageLabelImagePrefab:Clone();
	local messageLabel = messageLabelImage.MessageLabel;
	messageLabel.Text = msg;
	local ySize = TextService:GetTextSize(msg, messageLabel.TextSize, messageLabel.Font, newVector2(ABSOLUTE_SIZE_X, 1000)).Y;
	messageLabelImage.Size = newUDim2(1, 0, 0, ySize + PADDING);
	local children = messagesFrame:GetChildren();
	if #children - 1 > 4 then
		children[2]:Destroy();
	end;

	if string.find(msg, 'BOLO: ') or string.find(msg, 'ALERT: ') or string.find(msg, 'ATTN: ') then
		messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(63, 126, 194)
	elseif string.find(msg, 'PANIC BUTTON ACTIVATED. LOCATION: ') then
		messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(194, 63, 63)
	elseif string.find(msg, 'ALARM ACTIVATED AT VANCOUVER ISLAND REGIONAL CORRECTIONAL CENTRE. SWITCH TO CORRECTIONS CHANNEL FOR UPDATE.') then
		messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(32, 58, 86)
	end;

	if specialMsgType then
		if specialMsgType == 'System' then
			messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(63, 126, 194)
		elseif specialMsgType == 'Panic' then
			messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(194, 63, 63)
			panicSound:Play();
		elseif specialMsgType == 'Prison' then
			messageLabelImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(32, 58, 86)
			panicSound:Play();
		end;
	end;

	messageLabelImage.Parent = messagesFrame;
	if playTransmissionSound then
		transmission:Play();
	end;
end;

local function CharacterAdded(char)
	if not char then return; end;
	radioAnimation = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid'):WaitForChild('Animator'):LoadAnimation(components.RadioAnimation);
end;

local RadioGUI = {};

function RadioGUI:LoadPastMessages(channelName)
	local messages = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetRadioMessages', channelName);
	for i, v in next, messages do
		if string.sub(v, 1, 7):lower() == 'lookup ' then
			CreateLabel(v, false, 'System');
		else
			CreateLabel(v, false);
		end;
	end;
end;

function RadioGUI:CycleChannel()
	for i, v in next, messagesFrame:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('ImageLabel') then
			v:Destroy();
		end;
	end;
	currentChannel = currentChannel + 1;
	if currentChannel > #channels then
		currentChannel = 1;
	end;
	currentChannelName = channels[currentChannel];
	channelBtn.Text = currentChannelName;
	self:LoadPastMessages(currentChannelName);
	if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'GCPS' then
		bodyFrame.InputBoxImage.Visible = currentChannelName == "I-OPS" or currentChannelName == "T-OPS"
		panicBtn.Visible = currentChannelName == "I-OPS" or currentChannelName == "T-OPS"
	end
end;

function RadioGUI.IsEnabled()
	return radioGUI.Enabled;
end;

function RadioGUI:Enable()
	CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);

	channels = {};

	currentChannelName = 'UNIVERSAL'
	channelBtn.Text = currentChannelName
	currentChannel = 1;
	bodyFrame.InputBoxImage.Visible = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS'
	panicBtn.Visible = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS'

	local unorderedDictionary, orderedChannels = RadioChannels.Get();

	for _,v in ipairs(orderedChannels) do
		local accessFunc = unorderedDictionary[v];
		if accessFunc(localPlayer) then
			table.insert(channels, v);
		end;
	end;

	local ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
	if listeners == nil and settingsListeners == nil then
		listeners = ListenerList.new();
		settingsListeners = ListenerList.new();

		listeners:Connect(UIListLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal('AbsoluteContentSize'), function()
			bodyFrame.Size = newUDim2(1, -10, 0, (UIListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y / UIScale.Scale) + 6);
		end);
		radioSendConnection = NetworkController.Connect('RadioSend', function(msg, channel, specialMsgType)
			if channel == currentChannelName then
				CreateLabel(msg, true, specialMsgType);
			end;
		end);
		panicConnection = NetworkController.Connect('PanicButton', function(msg, channel)
			if channel == currentChannelName then
				CreateLabel(msg, false, 'Panic');
			end;
		end);
		prisonConnection = NetworkController.Connect('RadioPrisonAlarm', function(msg)
			if currentChannelName == 'UNIVERSAL' then
				CreateLabel(msg, false, 'Prison');
			end;
		end)
		listeners:Connect(inputEnded, function(input, onGUI)
			if onGUI then return; end;
			local keyCode = input.KeyCode;
			if keyCode == transmissionKey and bodyFrame.InputBoxImage.Visible then
				inputBox:CaptureFocus();

			elseif keyCode == channelCycleKey then
				self:CycleChannel();
			end;
		end);
		listeners:Connect(inputBox.Focused, function()
			toggle:Play();
			if localPlayer.Character and localPlayer.Character:GetAttribute("Earpiece") ~= true and localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then
				radioAnimation:Play();
			end
		end)
		listeners:Connect(inputBox.FocusLost, function(enterPressed)
			radioAnimation:Stop();
			if not enterPressed then return; end;
			local text = inputBox.Text;
			if not text:find('%S') then return; end;
			NetworkController.Send('RadioSend', text, currentChannelName);
			inputBox.Text = '';
		end);
		listeners:Connect(channelBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			self:CycleChannel();
		end);
		listeners:Connect(settingsBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			self:EnableSettings();
		end);
		listeners:Connect(localPlayer.CharacterAdded, CharacterAdded);

		listeners:Connect(panicBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			NetworkController.Send('RadioPanic', self.Controllers.Area.AreaController.Location or 'Area not detected', currentChannelName)
		end);

		self:LoadPastMessages(currentChannelName);
		radioGUI.Enabled = true;
	end
end;

function RadioGUI:EnableSettings()
	if settingsFrame.Position == UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1.5, 0) then
		local listeningTransmissionKey;
		local listeningChannelCycleKey;
		settingsListeners:Connect(transmissionKeyBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			if listeningTransmissionKey then return; end;
			transmissionKeyLabel.Text = '...';
			listeningTransmissionKey = inputEnded:Connect(function(input, onGUI)
				if onGUI then return; end;
				local keyCode = input.KeyCode;
				local keyCodeName = keyCode.Name;
				if keyCodeName ~= 'Unknown' and keyCode ~= channelCycleKey then
					listeningTransmissionKey:Disconnect();
					transmissionKey = keyCode;
					NetworkController.Send('SetKey', 'TransmissionKey', keyCodeName);
					keyCodeName = keyCodeName:upper();
					transmissionKeyLabel.Text = keyCodeName;
					inputBox.PlaceholderText = "Click here or press '" .. keyCodeName .. "' to transmit";
					listeningTransmissionKey = nil;
				end;
			end);
		end);
		settingsListeners:Connect(channelCycleKeyBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			if listeningChannelCycleKey then return; end;
			channelCycleKeyLabel.Text = '...';
			listeningChannelCycleKey = inputEnded:Connect(function(input, onGUI)
				if onGUI then return; end;
				local keyCode = input.KeyCode;
				local keyCodeName = keyCode.Name;
				if keyCodeName ~= 'Unknown' and keyCode ~= transmissionKey then
					listeningChannelCycleKey:Disconnect();
					channelCycleKey = keyCode;
					NetworkController.Send('SetKey', 'ChannelCycleKey', keyCodeName);
					keyCodeName = keyCodeName:upper();
					channelCycleKeyLabel.Text = keyCodeName;
					listeningChannelCycleKey = nil;
				end;
			end);
		end);
		settingsListeners:Connect(settingsBodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
			self:DisableSettings();
		end);
		settingsFrame.Visible = true;
		settingsFrame:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0), Enum.EasingDirection.Out, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, 0.23, true);
	elseif settingsFrame.Position == UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0) then
		self:DisableSettings();
	end;
end;

function RadioGUI:Disable()
	if listeners ~= nil and settingsListeners ~= nil then
		pcall(function()
			listeners:DisconnectAll();
			if radioSendConnection then
				radioSendConnection.Disconnect();
				radioSendConnection = nil;
			end;
			if panicConnection then
				panicConnection.Disconnect();
				panicConnection = nil;
			end;
			settingsListeners:DisconnectAll();
			settingsFrame.Visible = false;
			radioGUI.Enabled = false;
			settingsListeners = nil;
			listeners = nil;
		end)
	end
end;

function RadioGUI:DisableSettings()
	if settingsListeners ~= nil then
		pcall(function()
			settingsListeners:DisconnectAll();
			settingsFrame:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 1.5, 0), Enum.EasingDirection.Out, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, 0.23, true, function()
				settingsFrame.Visible = false;
			end);
		end)
	end
end;

function RadioGUI:Start()

	pcall(function()
		transmissionKey = Enum.KeyCode[localPlayer:WaitForChild('TransmissionKey').Value];
	end);
	inputBox.PlaceholderText = "Click here or press '" .. transmissionKey.Name:upper() .. "' to transmit";
	transmissionKeyLabel.Text = transmissionKey.Name:upper();

	pcall(function()
		channelCycleKey = Enum.KeyCode[localPlayer:WaitForChild('ChannelCycleKey').Value];
	end);
	channelCycleKeyLabel.Text = channelCycleKey.Name:upper();

	self.Modules.UI.Draggable.new(radioGUI, topBarFrame, mainFrame);
end;

function RadioGUI:Init()
	RadioChannels = self.Shared.RadioChannels;
	NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return RadioGUI;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/RepairToolGUI.lua ---

--[[
    RepairToolGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Repair ToolGUI
-- Khizzer
-- September 10, 2021

local DEFAULT_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.9);

local repairToolGUI = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('RepairToolGUI');
local mainFrame = repairToolGUI.MainFrame;
local statusLabel = mainFrame.BodyFrame.StatusLabel;

local RepairToolGUI = {}

function RepairToolGUI.Enable()
    repairToolGUI.Enabled = true;
    mainFrame:TweenPosition(ACTIVE_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true);
end;

function RepairToolGUI.SetStatus(status)
    statusLabel.Text = 'Repairing Vehicle [' .. status .. ']';
end;

function RepairToolGUI.Disable()
    mainFrame:TweenPosition(DEFAULT_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true, function()
        repairToolGUI.Enabled = false;
    end);
end;

function RepairToolGUI:Start()
    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('RepairCar', function(status)
        if not repairToolGUI.Enabled then
            self.Enable();
        end;
        self.SetStatus(status);
        if status == 0 or status == 'Cancelled' then
            wait(1);
            self.Disable();
        end;
    end);
end;



return RepairToolGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/RobBankGUI.lua ---

--[[
    RobBankGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Rob BankGUI
-- Khizzer
-- July 21, 2021



local RobBankGUI = {}

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local BankRobberyGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('BankRobberyGUI');

local Constants;
local DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.7);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local UserInput;
local ErrorGUI;
local TableUtil;
local Network;

local mainFrame = BankRobberyGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local gameFrame = bodyFrame.GameFrame;
local whiteSquare = gameFrame.Controlled;
local finishSquare = gameFrame.Finish;
local redLines = gameFrame.RedLines;

local WHeld = false;
local AHeld = false;
local SHeld = false;
local DHeld = false;

local MOVEMENT_SPEED = 3;

local START_POSITION = UDim2.fromOffset(387, 121);

local Robbing = false;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local function collidesWith(gui1, gui2)
    local gui1_topLeft = gui1.AbsolutePosition;
    local gui1_bottomRight = gui1_topLeft + gui1.AbsoluteSize;

    local gui2_topLeft = gui2.AbsolutePosition;
    local gui2_bottomRight = gui2_topLeft + gui2.AbsoluteSize;

    return ((gui1_topLeft.x < gui2_bottomRight.x and gui1_bottomRight.x > gui2_topLeft.x) and (gui1_topLeft.y < gui2_bottomRight.y and gui1_bottomRight.y > gui2_topLeft.y)) 
end;

local function CopyChildrenToParent(children, parent)
    parent:ClearAllChildren();
    for i,v in next, children:GetChildren() do
        local clone = v:Clone();
        clone.Parent = parent;
    end;
end;

function RobBankGUI:EndRobbery(result)
    BankRobberyGUI.Enabled = false;
    Robbing, WHeld, AHeld, SHeld, DHeld = false, false, false, false, false;
    local PlayerControl = require(localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerScripts'):WaitForChild('PlayerModule'):WaitForChild('ControlModule'));
    PlayerControl:Enable();
--    localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false;
    Network.Send('BankRobbery', result);
    if result == 'Failure' then
        ErrorGUI.Error('You failed! Try again next time...');
    end;
end;

function RobBankGUI:StartRobbery()
    BankRobberyGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    local Patterns = game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('BankPatterns'):GetChildren();

    TableUtil.Shuffle(Patterns);

    local counter = 1;

    local PlayerControl = require(localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerScripts'):WaitForChild('PlayerModule'):WaitForChild('ControlModule'));
    PlayerControl:Disable();
    
    CopyChildrenToParent(Patterns[1], gameFrame.RedLines);

    local Keyboard = UserInput:Get('Keyboard');
    Robbing = true;

    Keyboard.KeyDown:Connect(function(keyCode)
        if not Robbing then return; end;
        if keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W then
            WHeld = true;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then
            AHeld = true;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then
            SHeld = true;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then
            DHeld = true;
        end;
    end);

    Keyboard.KeyUp:Connect(function(keyCode)
        if not Robbing then return; end;
        if keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W then
            WHeld = false;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then
            AHeld = false;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then
            SHeld = false;
        elseif keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then
            DHeld = false;
        end;
    end);

    while Robbing do
        wait();
        if WHeld == true then
            whiteSquare.Position -= UDim2.fromOffset(0, MOVEMENT_SPEED);
        end;

        if AHeld == true then
            whiteSquare.Position -= UDim2.fromOffset(MOVEMENT_SPEED, 0);
        end;

        if SHeld == true then
            whiteSquare.Position += UDim2.fromOffset(0, MOVEMENT_SPEED);
        end;

        if DHeld == true then
            whiteSquare.Position += UDim2.fromOffset(MOVEMENT_SPEED, 0);
        end;

        for i,v in next, redLines:GetChildren() do
            if collidesWith(v, whiteSquare) == true then
                whiteSquare.Position = START_POSITION;
                self:EndRobbery('Failure');
                closeTween:Play();
            end;
        end;

        if collidesWith(whiteSquare, finishSquare) then
            whiteSquare.Position = START_POSITION;
            if counter + 1 == 4 then
                self:EndRobbery('Success');
                closeTween:Play();
            else
                counter += 1;
                CopyChildrenToParent(Patterns[counter], gameFrame.RedLines);
            end
        end;
    end;
end;

function RobBankGUI:Start()
    Network.Connect(DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT, function()
        self:StartRobbery();
    end);
end;

function RobBankGUI:Init()
    UserInput = self.Controllers.UserInput;
    ErrorGUI = self.Controllers.UI.ErrorGUI;
    TableUtil = self.Shared.TableUtil;
    Network = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Constants = self.Shared.Constants.Robbery;
    DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT = Constants['DISPLAY_BANK_ROBBERY_EVENT']
end;

return RobBankGUI;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/SettingsGUI.lua ---

--[[
    SettingsGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- SettingsGUI
-- Khizzer
-- April 16, 2022

local SettingsGUI = {}
local Lighting = game:GetService('Lighting');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');


local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local settingsFolder = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Settings')

local settingsGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('SettingsGUI');
local mainFrame = settingsGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local settingsListImage = bodyFrame.SettingsListImage;
local settingsListScrollingFrame = settingsListImage.SettingsListScrollingFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local components = settingsGUI.Components;
local settingPrefab = components.SettingPrefab;


local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local DEFAULT_SLIDER_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(103, 103, 103);
local ENABLED_SLIDER_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local NetworkController;
local ListenerList;

--slider positions
local enabledPosition = UDim2.new(0, 35, 0.5, 0);
local disabledPosition = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0.5, 0);

local settingInfo = {
    ['WaypointSetting'] = {
        Title = 'Waypoints';
        Description = 'Enable or disable waypoints on buildings';
    };
    ['KeybindsVisibility'] = {
        Title = 'Keybind Visibility';
        Description = 'Show or hide keybinds GUI';
    };
    ['Shadows'] = {
        Title = 'Shadows';
        Description = 'Enable or disable shadows for performance';
    }
}

local GuiListeners;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function SettingsGUI:Enable()
    if not GuiListeners then GuiListeners = ListenerList.new(); end;
    settingsGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    for settingName: string, settingValue: any in settingsFolder:GetAttributes() do
        local description = settingInfo[settingName].Description or 'No description available';
        local title = settingInfo[settingName].Title or 'No title available';

        local settingFrame = settingPrefab:Clone();
        settingFrame.Name = settingName;
        settingFrame.Parent = settingsListScrollingFrame;
        settingFrame.DescriptionLabel.Text = description;
        settingFrame.TitleLabel.Text = title;

        if typeof(settingValue) == 'boolean' then
            local sliderLabel: ImageLabel = settingFrame.SliderLabel;
            local sliderBtn: ImageButton = sliderLabel.SliderBtn;

            sliderLabel.Visible = true;
            sliderBtn.Position = settingValue and enabledPosition or disabledPosition;
            sliderBtn.ImageColor3 = settingValue and ENABLED_SLIDER_COLOR or DEFAULT_SLIDER_COLOR;

            GuiListeners:Connect(sliderBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
                if sliderBtn:GetAttribute('isTweening') then return end;

                local newSetting = not settingsFolder:GetAttribute(settingName);

                NetworkController.Send('UpdateSetting', settingName, newSetting);

                local newPosition = sliderBtn.Position == enabledPosition and disabledPosition or enabledPosition;
                local newColor = sliderBtn.ImageColor3 == ENABLED_SLIDER_COLOR and DEFAULT_SLIDER_COLOR or ENABLED_SLIDER_COLOR;

                local tween = TweenService:Create(sliderBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {
                    Position = newPosition;
                    ImageColor3 = newColor;
                })

                sliderBtn:SetAttribute('isTweening', true);

                tween:Play();

                tween.Completed:Once(function()
                    sliderBtn:SetAttribute('isTweening', nil);
                    tween:Destroy();
                end);

                settingsFolder:SetAttribute(settingName, not settingValue);
            end);
        end;
    end;

    GuiListeners:Connect(exitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        SettingsGUI:Disable();
    end)
end;

function SettingsGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        settingsGUI.Enabled = false;
        for _,v in next, settingsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ImageLabel') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;
    end)
end;

function SettingsGUI.Toggle()
    if GuiListeners then GuiListeners:Destroy(); GuiListeners = nil; end;
    if settingsGUI.Enabled then
        SettingsGUI:Disable();
    else
        SettingsGUI:Enable();
    end;
end;

function SettingsGUI:Start()
    Lighting.GlobalShadows = settingsFolder:GetAttribute('Shadows');
    settingsFolder:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Shadows'):Connect(function()
        Lighting.GlobalShadows = settingsFolder:GetAttribute('Shadows');
    end);
end;

function SettingsGUI:Init()
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return SettingsGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/ShopGUI.lua ---

--[[
    ShopGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local dummyTools = ReplicatedStorage.dummyTools

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local CAMERA_OFFSET = CFrame.new(1, 1.5, 0);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local shopGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('ShopGUI');
local mainFrame = shopGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local buyBtn = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local refillBtn = btnsFrame.RefillBtn;

local weaponsListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.WeaponsListImage.WeaponsListScrollingFrame;

local detailsFrame = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local weaponViewportFrame = detailsFrame.WeaponViewportFrame;
local statsFrame = detailsFrame.StatsFrame;

local priceLabel = statsFrame.PriceLabel;
local ammoLabel = statsFrame.AmmoLabel;
local damageLabel = statsFrame.DmgLabel;
local refillPriceLabel = statsFrame.RefillPriceLabel;

local components = shopGUI.Components;
local weaponBtnPrefab = components.WeaponBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local selectedBtn;

local viewportCamera;
local viewportWeaponModel;

local buyConnection;
local refillBtnConnection;

local NetworkController;
local Notification;

local function CreateCamera()
    local camera = Instance.new('Camera');
    return camera;
end;

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    local uiListLayout = weaponsListScrollingFrame.UIGridLayout;
    local absoluteContentSize = uiListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize;
    -- weaponsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#weaponsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
    weaponsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, absoluteContentSize.Y);
end;

local function SetupCameraAndGetViewportWeapon(camera, name)
    local weapon: Model = game.ReplicatedStorage.dummyTools[name]:Clone();

    local cframe, size = weapon:GetBoundingBox();

    local rot = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0), math.rad(90), 0);

    size = rot:VectorToObjectSpace(size);

    local frameSize = 128;

    local sizeX, sizeY, sizeZ = math.abs(size.X), math.abs(size.Y), math.abs(size.Z);

    local h = (sizeY / math.tan(math.rad(camera.FieldOfView / 2)) * 2) + (sizeZ / 2);

    local frameX = (sizeX > sizeY and frameSize or (frameSize * (sizeX / sizeY)));
    local frameY = (sizeY > sizeX and frameSize or (frameSize * (sizeY / sizeX)));

    weaponViewportFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, frameX, 0, frameY);
    camera.CFrame = cframe * rot * CFrame.new(0, 0, h);

--    camera.CFrame = CFrame.new((weapon.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CAMERA_OFFSET).Position, weapon.PrimaryPart.Position);

    return weapon;
end;

local ShopGUI = {}

function ShopGUI.IsEnabled()
    return shopGUI.Enabled;
end;

function ShopGUI.Enable(dealerLegal)
    viewportCamera = CreateCamera();
    weaponViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = viewportCamera;

    refillBtnConnection = refillBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('shop->refill');
    end);

    local function setupItem(tool)
        local itemName = tool.Name;
        local damage = tool:GetAttribute('Damage') or tool:GetAttribute('BaseDamage')
        local clipSize = tool:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo');
        local maxReserveAmmo = tool:GetAttribute('MaxReserveAmmo');
        local price = tool:GetAttribute('Price'); -- XXX:

        local itemType;

        if damage and clipSize then
            itemType = 'GUN';
        elseif damage and not clipSize then
            itemType = 'MELEE';
            damage = ('%d-%d'):format(v:GetAttribute('BaseDamage'), v:GetAttribute('CritDamage'));
        else
            itemType = 'MISC';
        end;

        local itemBtn = weaponBtnPrefab:Clone();
        itemBtn.WeaponLabel.Text = itemName;
        itemBtn.Parent = weaponsListScrollingFrame;

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        local function ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn()
            local hasBoughtGun = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(itemName) or localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(itemName)
            if hasBoughtGun and itemType == 'GUN' then
                refillBtn.Visible = true;
                buyBtn.Visible = false;
            else
                buyBtn.Visible = true;
                refillBtn.Visible = false;
            end;
        end;


        itemBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        itemBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);

        itemBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedBtn = itemBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();

            priceLabel.Text = 'Price: $'..price;
            --buyBtn.Visible = true;

            if itemType == 'GUN' then
                damageLabel.Text = 'Damage: '..damage;
                ammoLabel.Text = 'Clip Size: '..clipSize;
                refillPriceLabel.Text = 'Refill Price: '..maxReserveAmmo;
            elseif itemType == 'MELEE' then
                damageLabel.Text = 'Damage: '..damage;
                ammoLabel.Text = '';
                refillPriceLabel.Text = '';
            else
                damageLabel.Text = '';
                ammoLabel.Text = '';
                refillPriceLabel.Text = '';
            end;

            if viewportWeaponModel then
                viewportWeaponModel:Destroy();
            end;

            viewportWeaponModel = SetupCameraAndGetViewportWeapon(viewportCamera, itemName);
            viewportWeaponModel.Parent = weaponViewportFrame;

            ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn();

            if buyConnection then
                buyConnection:Disconnect();
            end;

            buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if itemType == 'GUN' and dealerLegal and not hasPAL() then
                    Notification(
                        "Purchase Refused",
                        `You must have a PAL to buy from an authorized dealer.`,
                        nil,
                        'Red'
                    )
                    return
                end

                NetworkController.Send('DEALER_PURCHASE', itemName);
                ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn()
                ShopGUI.Disable()
            end);
        end);
    end

    for i, v in next, dummyTools:GetChildren() do
        if (dealerLegal == true and v:GetAttribute('Legal') == true) or (dealerLegal == false) then
            if not dealerLegal and v.Name == "PAL" then continue end
        end;
    end;

    UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize();

    shopGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play()
end;

function ShopGUI.Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    shopGUI.Enabled = false;


    buyBtn.Visible = false;
    refillBtn.Visible = false;

    priceLabel.Text = '';
    damageLabel.Text = '';
    ammoLabel.Text = '';
    refillPriceLabel.Text = '';

    weaponViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = nil;
    if viewportCamera then
        viewportCamera:Destroy();
    end;
    if viewportWeaponModel then
        viewportWeaponModel:Destroy();
    end;
    if buyConnection then
        buyConnection:Disconnect();
        buyConnection = nil;
    end;

    if refillBtnConnection then
        refillBtnConnection:Disconnect();
        refillBtnConnection = nil;
    end;

    for i, v in next, weaponsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
end;

function ShopGUI:Start()
    exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(self.Disable)
end;

function ShopGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController
    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new
end

return ShopGUI

--[[

-- Snow PlowGUI
-- Khizzer
-- November 20, 2022



local SnowPlowGUI = {}

local Draggable;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local snowPlowGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('SnowPlowGUI');
local mainFrame = snowPlowGUI.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local verticalFrame = bodyFrame.VerticalFrame;
local upBtn = verticalFrame.UpBtn;
local downBtn = verticalFrame.DownBtn;
local horizontalFrame = bodyFrame.HorizontalFrame;
local leftBtn = horizontalFrame.LeftBtn;
local centreBtn = horizontalFrame.CentreBtn;
local rightBtn = horizontalFrame.RightBtn;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local NetworkController;

local ListenerList;
local GuiListeners;

local TRANSLINK_TEAM = game:GetService('Teams').Translink;

local selectedVerticalBtn;
local selectedHorizontalBtn;


function SnowPlowGUI:Enable()
    local carValue = localPlayer.Car;

    if not localPlayer.Team == TRANSLINK_TEAM then return; end;
    local snowPlowState = carValue.Value.Config.State:FindFirstChild('SnowPlow');
    if not snowPlowState then return; end;

    if not GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;

    snowPlowGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    GuiListeners:Connect(upBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedVerticalBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end;

        selectedVerticalBtn = upBtn;
        TweenService:Create(upBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        NetworkController.Send('SetSnowPlow', 'Up');
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(downBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedVerticalBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end;

        selectedVerticalBtn = downBtn;
        TweenService:Create(downBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        NetworkController.Send('SetSnowPlow', 'Down');
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(leftBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedHorizontalBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end;

        selectedHorizontalBtn = leftBtn;
        TweenService:Create(leftBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        NetworkController.Send('SetSnowPlow', 'Left');
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(centreBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedHorizontalBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end;

        selectedHorizontalBtn = centreBtn;
        TweenService:Create(centreBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        NetworkController.Send('SetSnowPlow', 'Centre');
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(rightBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedHorizontalBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        selectedHorizontalBtn = rightBtn;
        TweenService:Create(rightBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        NetworkController.Send('SetSnowPlow', 'Right');
    end);

    local verticalState = snowPlowState:GetAttribute('Vertical');
    local horizontalState = snowPlowState:GetAttribute('Horizontal');

    if verticalState == 'Up' then
        selectedVerticalBtn = upBtn;
        downBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    elseif verticalState == 'Down' then
        selectedVerticalBtn = downBtn;
        upBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    end;

    if horizontalState == 'Left' then
        selectedHorizontalBtn = leftBtn;
        centreBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        rightBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    elseif horizontalState == 'Centre' then
        selectedHorizontalBtn = centreBtn;
        leftBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        rightBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    elseif horizontalState == 'Right' then
        selectedHorizontalBtn = rightBtn;
        leftBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        centreBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    end;

    selectedVerticalBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
    selectedHorizontalBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;

    GuiListeners:Connect(upBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn ~= upBtn then
            upBtn.ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(upBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn ~= upBtn then
            upBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(downBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn ~= downBtn then
            downBtn.ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(downBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedVerticalBtn ~= downBtn then
            downBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(leftBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= leftBtn then
            leftBtn.ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(leftBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= leftBtn then
            leftBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(centreBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= centreBtn then
            centreBtn.ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(centreBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= centreBtn then
            centreBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(rightBtn.MouseEnter, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= rightBtn then
            rightBtn.ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(rightBtn.MouseLeave, function()
        if selectedHorizontalBtn ~= rightBtn then
            rightBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        end;
    end);
end;

function SnowPlowGUI:Disable()
    GuiListeners:DisconnectAll();
    GuiListeners = nil;
    
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        snowPlowGUI.Enabled = false;
    end);
end;

function SnowPlowGUI:Start()
    Draggable.new(snowPlowGUI, topBarFrame, mainFrame);
    NetworkController.Connect('SnowPlowGuiVisibility', function(enable)
        if enable then
            self:Enable();
        else
            self:Disable();
        end;
    end)
end;

function SnowPlowGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;

    snowPlowGUI.Enabled = false;
    mainFrame.Position = DEFAULT_POSITION;
    Draggable = self.Modules.UI.Draggable;
end;


return SnowPlowGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/TeamChangeGUI.lua ---

--[[
    TeamChangeGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Team ChangeGUI
-- Khizzer
-- December 7, 2021
local GroupService = game:GetService("GroupService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')
local Teams = game:GetService('Teams');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TeamChangeGUI = {};

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local DIVISIONS_FOLDER = ReplicatedStorage.Divisions;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local teamChangeGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('TeamChangeGUI');
local mainFrame = teamChangeGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local teamsListImage = bodyFrame.TeamsListImage;
local scrollingFrame = teamsListImage.ScrollingFrame;

local categoryImage = bodyFrame.CategoryImage;
local categoryFrame = categoryImage.CategoryFrame;
local teamsBtn = categoryFrame.TeamsBtn;
local divisionsBtn = categoryFrame.DivisionsBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local components = teamChangeGUI.Components;
local teamBtnPreFab = components.TeamBtn;

local selectedCategoryBtn = teamsBtn;

local NetworkController;
local DeveloperCheck;

local groups = {}
local populateTask: thread?

local function PopulateScrollingFrame(contentType: string)
    for _,v in next, scrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
    if contentType == 'Teams' then
        for i, v in next, Teams:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Team') and v:GetAttribute("GroupID") and v:GetAttribute("MinimumRank") then
                if not DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) then
                    local groupId = v:GetAttribute("GroupID")
                    local minRank = v:GetAttribute("MinimumRank")
                    if
                        localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupId) >= minRank
                        or (groups[groupId] ~= nil and groups[groupId] >= minRank)
                    then
                        if v:FindFirstChild('Condition') then
                            if not require(v.Condition)(localPlayer) then continue end;
                        end
                    else
                        continue
                    end
                end

                local teamBtn = teamBtnPreFab:Clone();
				teamBtn.Parent = scrollingFrame;
                teamBtn.TeamLabel.Text = v.Name;
                teamBtn.Name = if v.Name == 'Civilian' then 'AAAAA_Civilian' else v.Name;

                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(teamBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = v.TeamColor.Color});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(teamBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

                teamBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end)

                teamBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end)

                teamBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                    NetworkController.Send('ChangeTeam', v);
                    TeamChangeGUI:Disable();
                end)
            end
        end
    elseif contentType == 'Divisions' then
        if not DIVISIONS_FOLDER:FindFirstChild(localPlayer.Team.Name) then
            return
        end
        for _,v in next, DIVISIONS_FOLDER[localPlayer.Team.Name]:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Folder') then
                if v.Name == "GCPS" or not DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) then
                    if localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(v:GetAttribute("GroupID")) < v:GetAttribute("MinimumRank") then continue end
                    if v:FindFirstChild('Condition') then
                        if not require(v.Condition)(localPlayer) then continue end;
                    end
                end

                local teamBtn = teamBtnPreFab:Clone();
                teamBtn.Parent = scrollingFrame;
                teamBtn.TeamLabel.Text = v.Name;
                teamBtn.Name = v.Name;

                local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(teamBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(teamBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

                teamBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    hoverTween:Play();
                end);

                teamBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                    hoverEndTween:Play();
                end);

                teamBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    NetworkController.Send('DIVISION_CHANGE', v.Name);
                    TeamChangeGUI:Disable();
                end);
            end
        end
    end
end

function TeamChangeGUI:Toggle()
    if teamChangeGUI.Enabled == false then
        teamChangeGUI.Enabled = true;
        openTween:Play();

        if populateTask then
            task.cancel(populateTask)
        end
        populateTask = task.spawn(PopulateScrollingFrame, 'Teams')

        divisionsBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
        teamsBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;

        selectedCategoryBtn = teamsBtn;
    else
        self:Disable();
    end;
end;

function TeamChangeGUI:Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait()
    teamChangeGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function TeamChangeGUI:Start()
    localPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(function()
        if teamChangeGUI.Enabled then
            self:Disable();
        end;
    end);

    bodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(self.Disable)

    local teamHoverTween = TweenService:Create(teamsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local teamHoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(teamsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local teamSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(teamsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

    teamsBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn == teamsBtn then return; end;
        teamHoverTween:Play();
    end);

    teamsBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn == teamsBtn then return; end;
        teamHoverEndTween:Play();
    end);

    teamsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedCategoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        selectedCategoryBtn = teamsBtn;
        teamSelectedTween:Play();

        if populateTask then
            task.cancel(populateTask)
        end
        populateTask = task.spawn(PopulateScrollingFrame, 'Teams')
    end);

    local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(divisionsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
    local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(divisionsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
    local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(divisionsBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

    divisionsBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn == divisionsBtn then return; end;
        hoverTween:Play();
    end);

    divisionsBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn == divisionsBtn then return; end;
        hoverEndTween:Play();
    end);

    divisionsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if selectedCategoryBtn then
            TweenService:Create(selectedCategoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
        end

        selectedCategoryBtn = divisionsBtn;
        selectedTween:Play();

        if populateTask then
            task.cancel(populateTask)
        end
        populateTask = task.spawn(PopulateScrollingFrame, 'Divisions')
    end);

    task.defer(function()
        while true do
            local ok, res
            repeat
                ok, res = pcall(GroupService.GetGroupsAsync, GroupService, localPlayer.UserId)
                if not ok then
                    warn(`Could not get groups for team changer: {res}`)
                    task.wait(5)
                else
                    for _, group in res do
                        groups[group.Id] = group.Rank
                    end
                end
            until ok
            task.wait(120)
        end
    end)

    for _, v in Teams:GetChildren() do
        if v:FindFirstChild('Condition') then
            require(v.Condition)
        end
    end
    for _, x in DIVISIONS_FOLDER:GetDescendants() do
        if x:IsA("ModuleScript") and x.Name == "Condition" and x.Parent.Parent.Parent == DIVISIONS_FOLDER then
            require(x)
        end
    end
end;

function TeamChangeGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end;


return TeamChangeGUI;

--[[
    TimeGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local TimeGUI = {};

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local timeGUI = Instance.new('ScreenGui');
timeGUI.IgnoreGuiInset = true;
timeGUI.ResetOnSpawn = false;

local timeLabel = Instance.new('TextLabel');
timeLabel.Parent = timeGUI

function TimeGUI:Start()
    timeLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0, 2);
    timeLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
    timeLabel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0);
    timeLabel.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(150, 20);
    timeLabel.TextSize = 12
    timeLabel.FontFace = Font.fromName("Arial", Enum.FontWeight.Bold, Enum.FontStyle.Normal)
    timeLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
    timeLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
    timeGUI.Parent = localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerGui')

    RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        local dt = DateTime.now();
        timeLabel.Text = dt:FormatUniversalTime('ddd D MMM YYYY HH:mm:ss', 'en-us');
    end)
end

return TimeGUI

--[[

    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local DEFAULT_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.9);

local tirePumpGUI = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('TirePumpGUI');
local mainFrame = tirePumpGUI.MainFrame;
local statusLabel = mainFrame.BodyFrame.StatusLabel;

local TirePumpGUI = {};

function TirePumpGUI.Enable()
    tirePumpGUI.Enabled = true;
    mainFrame:TweenPosition(ACTIVE_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true);
end;

function TirePumpGUI.SetStatus(status)
    statusLabel.Text = 'Pumping Tire [' .. status .. ']';
end;

function TirePumpGUI.Disable()
    mainFrame:TweenPosition(DEFAULT_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true, function()
        tirePumpGUI.Enabled = false;
    end);
end;

function TirePumpGUI:Start()
    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('TirePump', function(status)
        if not tirePumpGUI.Enabled then
            self.Enable();
        end;
        self.SetStatus(status);
        if status == 0 or status == 'Cancelled' then
            wait(1);
            self.Disable();
        end;
    end);
end;

function TirePumpGUI:Init()

end;

return TirePumpGUI;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/ToolContainerGUI.lua ---

--[[
    ToolContainerGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local NetworkFunctionController;
local NetworkController;
local TrunkService;

local DEFAULT_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POS = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local wait;
local fromOffset = UDim2.fromOffset;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local tweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local trunkGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('TrunkGUI');
local mainFrame = trunkGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local otherContainerScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.TrunkFrame.TrunkScrollingFrame;
local inventoryScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.InventoryFrame.InventoryScrollingFrame;
local toolBtnPrefab = trunkGUI.Components.ToolBtn;

local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local onHover = {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)};
local onHoverEnd = {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)};

local ToolContainerGUI = {};

function ToolContainerGUI.Enabled()
    return trunkGUI.Enabled;
end;

type ToolContainer = {
    Type: "Player" | "Bin" | "Car";
    Instance: Instance;
}

type TrunkResponse = {
    CanOpen: boolean;
    ConsentNeeded: boolean;
}

local PLAYER_TOOL_CONTAINER = {
    Type = "Player";
    Instance = localPlayer;
};

function ToolContainerGUI:Toggle(containerData: ToolContainer)
    local function LoadTool(tool, inventorySide)
        local toolBtn = toolBtnPrefab:Clone();
        local toolName = tool.Name;
        local parentFrame = inventorySide and inventoryScrollingFrame or otherContainerScrollingFrame;
        local onHoverTween = tweenService:Create(toolBtn, tweenInfo, onHover);
        local onHoverEndTween = tweenService:Create(toolBtn, tweenInfo, onHoverEnd);
        toolBtn.ToolLabel.Text = toolName;
        toolBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            onHoverTween:Play();
        end);
        toolBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            onHoverEndTween:Play();
        end);
        toolBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local newParentFrame = (toolBtn.Parent == otherContainerScrollingFrame) and inventoryScrollingFrame or otherContainerScrollingFrame;
            local sourceContainer = (newParentFrame == otherContainerScrollingFrame) and PLAYER_TOOL_CONTAINER or containerData;
            local destinationContainer = (newParentFrame == otherContainerScrollingFrame) and containerData or PLAYER_TOOL_CONTAINER;

            NetworkController.Send('SwapFromToolContainer', toolName, sourceContainer, destinationContainer);
            toolBtn.Parent = newParentFrame;
            newParentFrame.CanvasSize = fromOffset(0, (#newParentFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 35);
        end);
        toolBtn.Parent = parentFrame;
        parentFrame.CanvasSize = fromOffset(0, (#parentFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 35);
    end;

    local backpack = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Backpack');
    if containerData then
        if containerData.Type == "Car" then
            local canOpen: TrunkResponse = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('CanOpenTrunk', containerData);
            if not canOpen.CanOpen and not canOpen.ConsentNeeded then return; end;
            if canOpen.ConsentNeeded then
                local permissionGiven = self.ConsentSignal:Wait();
                self.Controllers.UI.YesNoPromptGUI:ForceClose();
                if not permissionGiven then return; end;
            end;
        end;
        for i, v in next, backpack:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Tool') then
                LoadTool(v, true);
            end;
        end;
        local _tools = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetToolContainer', containerData);
        for i, v in next, _tools do
            LoadTool(v);
        end;

        trunkGUI.Enabled = true;
        mainFrame.Visible = true;
        mainFrame:TweenPosition(ACTIVE_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true);

        local rootPart = localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
        if containerData.Type == "Car" then
            while (rootPart.Position - containerData.Instance.Body.Trunk.Position).Magnitude < 7 do wait(); end;
        elseif containerData.Type == "Bin" then
            while (rootPart.Position - containerData.Instance.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude < 7 do wait(); end;
        elseif containerData.Type == "Player" then
            while (rootPart.Position - containerData.Instance.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 7 do wait(); end;
        end;
        self:Toggle();
    else
        mainFrame:TweenPosition(DEFAULT_POS, nil, nil, 0.23, true, function()
            mainFrame.Visible = false;
            trunkGUI.Enabled = false;
            for i, v in next, otherContainerScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v:Destroy();
                end;
            end;
            for i, v in next, inventoryScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
                    v:Destroy();
                end;
            end;
        end);
    end;
end;

function ToolContainerGUI:Start()
    self.ConsentSignal = self.Shared.Signal.new();
    bodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        self:Toggle();
    end);

    NetworkController.Connect('ConsentTrunkSearch', function()
        self.ConsentSignal:Fire(true);
    end)
end;

function ToolContainerGUI:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
end;

return ToolContainerGUI;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/TowTruckGUI.lua ---

--[[
    TowTruckGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Tow TruckGUI
-- Khizzer
-- August 15, 2021



local TowTruckGUI = {}
local NetworkController;

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');


local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local playerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui;
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.9);

local towTruckGUI = playerGUI:WaitForChild('TowTruckGUI');
local mainFrame = towTruckGUI.MainFrame;
local towBtnsFrame = mainFrame.TowBtnsFrame;
local attachBtn = towBtnsFrame.AttachBtn;
local winchInBtn = towBtnsFrame.WinchInBtn;
local bedBtn = towBtnsFrame.BedBtn;
local bedLabel = bedBtn.BedLabel;
local weldBtn = towBtnsFrame.WeldBtn;

local exitBtn = mainFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn;

local userInput;



local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService");

local clickConnection;

local TOW_TRUCK_ATTACH_EVENT
local TOW_TRUCK_DETACH_EVENT
local TOW_TRUCK_WINCH_IN_EVENT
local TOW_TRUCK_STOP_WINCH_EVENT
local FLATBED_LOWER_BED_EVENT
local FLATBED_RAISE_BED_EVENT
local FLATBED_WELD_EVENT
local FLATBED_RELEASE_EVENT
local FLATBED_WINCH_IN_EVENT
local FLATBED_STOP_WINCH_EVENT
local FLATBED_ATTACH_EVENT
local FLATBED_DETACH_EVENT
local Functions

function TowTruckGUI.Enabled()
    return towTruckGUI.Enabled;
end

function TowTruckGUI:Toggle(enabled)
    if enabled then
        towTruckGUI.Enabled = true;
        TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION}):Play();
    else
        TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION}):Play()
        towTruckGUI.Enabled = false;
    end
end

function TowTruckGUI:Start()
    local preferred = userInput:GetPreferred()

    local inputType;
    if (preferred == userInput.Preferred.Touch) then
        inputType = 'Mobile';
    elseif (preferred == userInput.Preferred.Mouse or preferred == userInput.Preferred.Keyboard) then
        inputType = 'Desktop'
    end;

    local function getTowTruckType()
        local car = localPlayer.Car;
        if (not car) or (not car.Value) or (not string.find(car.Value.Name, 'TowTruck')) then return; end;

        if (string.lower(car.Value.Name)):find('tow truck') then return 'Regular' end;
        if (string.lower(car.Value.Name)):find('flatbed') then return 'Flatbed' end;
    end;

    attachBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local car = localPlayer.Car;
        if (not car) or (not car.Value) or (not string.find(car.Value.Name, 'TowTruck')) then return; end;

        if car.Value:FindFirstChild('Attached') then
            if getTowTruckType() == 'Regular' then
                print('regular, sending');
                NetworkController.Send(TOW_TRUCK_DETACH_EVENT);
            elseif getTowTruckType() == 'Flatbed' then
                NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_DETACH_EVENT);
            end;
            TweenService:Create(attachBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            if clickConnection then
                clickConnection:Disconnect();
                clickConnection = nil;
                for _,part in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('TowPart') do
                    part.Transparency = 1
                end
            end;
            return;
        end;

        if clickConnection then --If not winch attached but button activated
            TweenService:Create(attachBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            clickConnection:Disconnect();
            clickConnection = nil;
            for _,part in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('TowPart') do
                part.Transparency = 1
            end
        else --If not winch attached but button is not already activated
            TweenService:Create(attachBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            if inputType == 'Mobile' then
                
            else --Desktop
                for _,part in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('TowPart') do
                    part.Transparency = 0.5
                end
                local mouse = userInput:Get('Mouse');
                clickConnection = mouse.LeftDown:Connect(function()
                    local mouseTarget, pos = mouse:CastWithWhitelist(CollectionService:GetTagged('TowPart'))
                    if mouseTarget then
                        local targetParent = mouseTarget.Parent;
                        local targetParentName = targetParent.Name;

                        if (targetParentName == 'Body') or (targetParentName == 'Chassis') then
                            if getTowTruckType() == 'Regular' then
                                NetworkController.Send(TOW_TRUCK_ATTACH_EVENT, targetParent.Parent, pos)
                            elseif getTowTruckType() == 'Flatbed' then 
                                NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_ATTACH_EVENT, targetParent.Parent, pos);
                            end;
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end;
    end)

    winchInBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if winchInBtn.ImageColor3 == DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR then
            if getTowTruckType() == 'Regular' then
                NetworkController.Send(TOW_TRUCK_WINCH_IN_EVENT);
            elseif getTowTruckType() == 'Flatbed' then
                NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_WINCH_IN_EVENT);
            end
        else
            if getTowTruckType() == 'Regular' then
                NetworkController.Send(TOW_TRUCK_STOP_WINCH_EVENT);
            elseif getTowTruckType() == 'Flatbed' then 
                NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_STOP_WINCH_EVENT);
            end;
        end;
    end)

    bedBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if bedLabel.Text == 'LOWER BED' then
            NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_LOWER_BED_EVENT);
        else
            NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_RAISE_BED_EVENT);
        end;
    end)

    weldBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if weldBtn.ImageColor3 == DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR then
            NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_WELD_EVENT);
        else
            NetworkController.Send(FLATBED_RELEASE_EVENT);
        end
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('WinchingIn', function()
        winchInBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
    end);

    NetworkController.Connect('WinchStopped', function()
        winchInBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('WeldedToBed', function()
        weldBtn.ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('ReleasedFromBed', function()
        weldBtn.ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('BedLowerable', function()
        bedLabel.Text = 'LOWER BED';
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('BedRaisable', function()
        bedLabel.Text = 'RAISE BED';
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('DisableCarGUI', function()
        localPlayer.PlayerGui.CarGUI.Enabled = false;
    end)

    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        TowTruckGUI:Toggle(false);
    end);

end;

function TowTruckGUI:Init()
    userInput = self.Controllers.UserInput;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    local Constants = self.Shared.Constants.TowTruck;
    TOW_TRUCK_ATTACH_EVENT = Constants['TOW_TRUCK_ATTACH_EVENT']
    TOW_TRUCK_DETACH_EVENT = Constants['TOW_TRUCK_DETACH_EVENT']
    TOW_TRUCK_WINCH_IN_EVENT = Constants['TOW_TRUCK_WINCH_IN_EVENT']
    TOW_TRUCK_STOP_WINCH_EVENT = Constants['TOW_TRUCK_STOP_WINCH_EVENT']
    FLATBED_LOWER_BED_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_LOWER_BED_EVENT'] 
    FLATBED_RAISE_BED_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_RAISE_BED_EVENT'] 
    FLATBED_WELD_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_WELD_EVENT']
    FLATBED_RELEASE_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_RELEASE_EVENT']
    FLATBED_WINCH_IN_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_WINCH_IN_EVENT']
    FLATBED_STOP_WINCH_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_STOP_WINCH_EVENT']
    FLATBED_ATTACH_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_ATTACH_EVENT'];
    FLATBED_DETACH_EVENT = Constants['FLATBED_DETACH_EVENT']
    Functions = self.Shared.Functions;
end;

return TowTruckGUI
