--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/TrailerSignGUI.lua ---

--[[
    TrailerSignGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Trailer SignGUI
-- Khizzer
-- January 31, 2023

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");

local TrailerSignGUI = {}

local Trove = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.Trove);
local NetworkController;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local trailerSignGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('TrailerSignGUI');
local mainFrame = trailerSignGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local setBtn = btnsFrame.SetBtn;
local signFrame = bodyFrame.SignFrame;
local signTextBox = signFrame.SignBox;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function TrailerSignGUI:Enable(interactionPart)
    if not interactionPart then return; end;

    --Sanity checks if gui is still open and they press it again
    if self._enabled and self._currentTrailer == interactionPart then return; end;
    if self._enabled then 
        self._currentTrailer = interactionPart; return;
    end;

    trailerSignGUI.Enabled = true;
    self._enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    self._currentTrailer = interactionPart;

    self._trove = Trove.new();

    self._trove:Connect(signTextBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'), function()
        local text = signTextBox.Text;

        text = text:upper();
        text = text:gsub('[^A-Z ]', '');

        signTextBox.Text = text;
    end)

    self._trove:Connect(exitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        self:Disable();
    end);

    self._trove:Connect(setBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        local text = signTextBox.Text;

        NetworkController.Send('SetTrailerSign', self._currentTrailer, text);
    end)
end;

function TrailerSignGUI:Disable()
    if not self._enabled then return; end;

    self._trove:Clean();
    self._trove = nil;

    self._currentTrailer = nil;
    
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        trailerSignGUI.Enabled = false;
        self._enabled = false;
    end);
end;

function TrailerSignGUI:Init()
    self._enabled = trailerSignGUI.Enabled;
    self._currentTrailer = nil;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return TrailerSignGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/TutorialGUI.lua ---

--[[
    TutorialGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- TutorialGUI
-- Rikona
-- January 16, 2023

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService");

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local playerGui = localPlayer.PlayerGui;

local tutorialGUI = playerGui:WaitForChild("TutorialGUI");

local TutorialSystemFolder = ReplicatedStorage.Tutorial;

local TGMainFrame = tutorialGUI.MainFrame;
local nextBtn = TGMainFrame.NextBtn;

local currentFrame = tutorialGUI:GetAttribute("CurrentFrame")

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5)
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5)
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23)

local openTween = TweenService:Create(TGMainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION})
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(TGMainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION})

local COOLDOWN_TIME = 0.3
local Cooldown = false

local Functions;
local ListenerList;

local CurrentFrame = 'Vehicles';

local Blur

local TutorialGUI = {}

function TutorialGUI:Enable()
    self:PromptTutorial();
end

function TutorialGUI:PromptTutorial()
	tutorialGUI.Enabled = true
	Blur = Functions:Create'BlurEffect' {
		Enabled = true;
		Size = 0;
		Parent = game.Lighting;
	}
	TweenService:Create(Blur, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = 12}):Play()
	openTween:Play()
end

function TutorialGUI:Start()
	nextBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if Cooldown == true then return; end;

		Cooldown = true
		task.delay(COOLDOWN_TIME, function()
			Cooldown = false
		end)

		if CurrentFrame == "Vehicles" then
			CurrentFrame = "Cash"
			TGMainFrame.VehiclesFrame.Visible = false
			TGMainFrame.CashFrame.Visible = true
		elseif CurrentFrame == "Cash" then
			CurrentFrame = "Firearms"
			TGMainFrame.CashFrame.Visible = false
			TGMainFrame.FirearmsFrame.Visible = true
		elseif CurrentFrame == "Firearms" then
			CurrentFrame = "Teams"
			TGMainFrame.FirearmsFrame.Visible = false
			TGMainFrame.TeamsFrame.Visible = true
		elseif CurrentFrame == "Teams" then
			CurrentFrame = "Final"
			TGMainFrame.TeamsFrame.Visible = false
			TGMainFrame.FinalFrame.Visible = true
			nextBtn.Label.Text = "Finish"
		elseif CurrentFrame == "Final" then
			closeTween:Play()
			closeTween.Completed:Wait()
			TweenService:Create(Blur, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = 0}):Play()
			Blur:Destroy()
			tutorialGUI:Destroy()
			local FolderClone = TutorialSystemFolder:Clone()
			FolderClone.Parent = workspace
			FolderClone.BankTouch.Touched:Connect(function(Hit)
				if Hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
					for _, Object in FolderClone:GetChildren() do
						if Object.Name:match("Bank") then
							Object:Destroy()
						end
					end
				end
			end)
			FolderClone.GunTouch.Touched:Connect(function(Hit)
				if Hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
					for _, Object in FolderClone:GetChildren() do
						if Object.Name:match("Gun") then
							Object:Destroy()
						end
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	end)
end

function TutorialGUI:Init()
	Functions = self.Shared.Functions;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
end

return TutorialGUI

--[[
    TutorialPromptGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Tutorial PromptGUI
-- Khizzer
-- January 22, 2023

local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService");

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local playerGui = localPlayer.PlayerGui;

local tutorialPromptGui = playerGui:WaitForChild("TutorialPromptGUI");
local mainFrame = tutorialPromptGui.MainFrame;
local confirmBtn = mainFrame.MainFrame.ConfirmBtn;
local denyBtn = mainFrame.MainFrame.DenyBtn;

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local ListenerList;
local NetworkController;

local GuiListeners;

local TutorialGUI;

local TutorialPromptGUI = {}

function TutorialPromptGUI:Enable()
    print('Enable');
    if self._enabled then return end;

    if not GuiListeners then
        GuiListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;

    self._enabled = true;
    tutorialPromptGui.Enabled = true;

    openTween:Play();

    GuiListeners:Connect(denyBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
        self:Disable();
    end);

    GuiListeners:Connect(confirmBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
        self:Disable();
        TutorialGUI:Enable();
    end);
end

function TutorialPromptGUI:Disable()
    if not self._enabled then return; end;

    GuiListeners:DisconnectAll();
    GuiListeners = nil;

    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Once(function()
        self._enabled = false;
        tutorialPromptGui.Enabled = false;
    end);

    NetworkController.Send('TutorialAcknowledged');
end;

function TutorialPromptGUI:Start()
    --it seems networkcontroller isnt fast enough to get the tutorial prompt event sometimes
    localPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal('TutorialPrompt'):Once(function()
        if localPlayer:GetAttribute('TutorialPrompt') then
            self:Enable();
        end
    end);

    if localPlayer:GetAttribute('TutorialPrompt') then
        self:Enable();
    end
end;

function TutorialPromptGUI:Init()
    TutorialGUI = self.Controllers.UI.TutorialGUI;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    self._enabled = tutorialPromptGui.Enabled;
end;


return TutorialPromptGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UI/UniformLockerGUI.lua ---

--[[
    UniformLockerGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Uniform LockerGUI
-- Khizzer
-- July 31, 2021



local UniformLockerGUI = {}

local UniformLockerService;

local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local playerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui;
local UniformGUI = playerGUI:WaitForChild('UniformGUI');

local LeftFrame = UniformGUI.LeftFrame;
local LeftBodyFrame = LeftFrame.BodyFrame;
local LeftCategoryBtnsList = LeftBodyFrame.CategoryList;
local LeftCategoryBtnsListGridLayout = LeftCategoryBtnsList.UIGridLayout
local ExitBtn = LeftBodyFrame.BtnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local ExitBtnConnection;

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local RightFrame = UniformGUI.RightFrame;
local RightBodyFrame = RightFrame.BodyFrame;
local RightOuterFrame = RightBodyFrame.OuterFrame;
local RightButtonFrame = RightOuterFrame.ButtonFrame;

local Components = UniformGUI.Components;
local ItemBtnPrefab = Components.ItemBtn;

local Functions;
local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local connections = {};

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local Uniforms = {
	['Hats'] = { };
	['Vests'] = { };
	['Holsters'] = { };
	['Shirts'] = { };
	['Pants'] = { };
	['Extras'] = { };
};

local selectedBtn;
local selectedCategory;

local previewAvatar;

function AddItem(type, item, name)
	Uniforms[type][name] = item;
end;

local hid = {}

function HideOtherUIs(val)
	if val == true then
		for i,v in pairs(playerGUI:GetChildren()) do
			if v:IsA("ScreenGui") then
				if v ~= UniformGUI then
					if v.Enabled == true then
						table.insert(hid, (#hid + 1), v)
						v.Enabled = false
					end
				end
			end
		end
	else
		for i,v in pairs(hid) do
			if v:IsA("ScreenGui") then
				v.Enabled = true
				hid[i] = nil
			end
		end
	end
end

function ShowCategory(category)
	RightButtonFrame:ClearAllChildren();
	local UIGridLayout = Instance.new('UIGridLayout');
	UIGridLayout.CellSize = UDim2.fromOffset(57, 57);
	UIGridLayout.CellPadding = UDim2.fromOffset(10, 5);
	UIGridLayout.Parent = RightButtonFrame;


	for name,item in next, Uniforms[category] do
		local itemBtn = ItemBtnPrefab:Clone();
		itemBtn.Parent = RightButtonFrame;
		itemBtn.Name = name;
		itemBtn.ItemLabel.Text = name;

		local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
		local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
		local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

		itemBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
			if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
			hoverTween:Play();
		end);

		itemBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
			if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
			hoverEndTween:Play();
		end);

		itemBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if category == "Extras" and selectedBtn == itemBtn then
				TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
				selectedBtn = nil;
				NetworkController.Send('UniformLocker', category, item);
				return
			end

			if selectedBtn then
				TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
			end;

			selectedBtn = itemBtn;
			selectedTween:Play();

			NetworkController.Send('UniformLocker', category, item);
		end)
	end;
end;

function UniformLockerGUI:Enable()
	HideOtherUIs(true)
	UniformGUI.Enabled = true;

	camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable;

	local character = localPlayer.Character;
	local torso = character.Torso;

	camera.CFrame = torso.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -5) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0);

	for _,v in next, RightButtonFrame:GetChildren() do
		if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
			v:Destroy();
		end;
	end;

	local data = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetUniforms');

	local uniforms = data.Uniforms;
	local vests = data.Vests;
	local hats = data.Hats;
	local holsters = data.Holsters;
	local extras = data.Extras;

	for _,array in next, uniforms do
		AddItem(array[2] ,array[3], array[1]) --Shirt/Pants, asset id, name
	end;

	for _,vest in next, vests do
		AddItem('Vests', vest, vest.Name);
	end;

	for _,v in next, hats do
		AddItem('Hats', v, v.Name);
	end;

	for _,v in next, holsters do
		AddItem('Holsters', v, v.Name);
	end;

	for _,v in next, extras do
		AddItem('Extras', v, v);
	end;

	for _,button in next, LeftCategoryBtnsList:GetChildren() do

		if button:IsA('ImageButton') then
			local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(button, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
			local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(button, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
			local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(button, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

			button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				if selectedCategory then
					TweenService:Create(selectedCategory, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
				end;

				selectedCategory = button;
				selectedTween:Play();

				local btnName = button.Name;
				local btnPos = btnName:find('Btn');
				local category = btnName:sub(1, btnPos - 1);
				ShowCategory(category);
			end)

			button.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
				if selectedCategory == button then return; end;
				hoverTween:Play();
			end);

			button.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
				if selectedCategory == button then return; end;
				hoverEndTween:Play();
			end);
		end;
	end;

	if not ExitBtnConnection then
		ExitBtnConnection = ExitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(self.Disable)
	end

end;

function UniformLockerGUI.Disable()
	Uniforms = {
		['Hats'] = { };
		['Vests'] = { };
		['Holsters'] = { };
		['Shirts'] = { };
		['Pants'] = { };
		['Extras'] = { };
	}
	HideOtherUIs(false)
	camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom;

	UniformGUI.Enabled = false;

	if ExitBtnConnection then
		ExitBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		ExitBtnConnection = nil;
	end;
end;

function UniformLockerGUI:Start()
end;

function UniformLockerGUI:Init()
	NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
	UniformLockerService = self.Services.UniformLockerService;
	Functions = self.Shared.Functions;
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return UniformLockerGUI

--[[
    WarehouseGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UI
    Parent: UI
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- WarehouseGUI
-- Khizzer
-- June 15, 2022



local WarehouseGUI = {}

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local PlayerGui = Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui;

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local warehouseGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('WarehouseGUI');
local mainFrame = warehouseGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local categoryFrame = bodyFrame.CategoryFrame;
local infoBtn = categoryFrame.InfoBtn;
local manageBtn = categoryFrame.ManageBtn;

local infoFrame = bodyFrame.InfoFrame;
local locationLabel = infoFrame.LocationLabel;
local ownerLabel = infoFrame.OwnerLabel;
local capacityLabel = infoFrame.CapacityLabel;

local manageRFrame = bodyFrame.ManageRFrame;
local moneyLabel = manageRFrame.MoneyLabel;
local dealerCutLabel = manageRFrame.DealerCutLabel;
local sellBtn = manageRFrame.SellBtn;

local manageLFrame = bodyFrame.ManageLFrame;
local suppliesFrame = manageLFrame.SuppliesFrame;
local suppliesBarImage = suppliesFrame.SuppliesBarImage;
local moneyFrame = manageLFrame.MoneyFrame;
local moneyBarImage = moneyFrame.MoneyBarImage;

local warehouseListImage = bodyFrame.WarehouseListImage;
local warehouseListScrollingFrame = warehouseListImage.WarehouseListScrollingFrame;
local buyBtn = warehouseListScrollingFrame.BuyBtn;

local components = warehouseGUI.Components;
local templateBtn = components.TemplateBtn;


--BtnsFrame with exitbtn
local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local visitBtn = btnsFrame.VisitBtn;

local selectedCategoryBtn = infoBtn;

local warehouseListeners;

local ListenerList;

local NetworkFunctionController;
local NetworkController;

local selectedPropertyBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

function WarehouseGUI.IsEnabled()
    return warehouseGUI.Enabled;
end;

type _warehouseInfo = {
    Owner: string;
    Location: string;
    Capacity: number;
}

type managementData = {
    Supplies: number;
    Money: number;
    RawMoney: number;
}

local manageSelectedTween = TweenService:Create(manageBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});


function WarehouseGUI:EnableInterior(warehouse: Model)
    if not warehouseListeners then
        warehouseListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;
    warehouseListeners:DisconnectAll();
    warehouseGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    warehouseListImage.Visible = false;
    infoFrame.Visible = true;
    manageRFrame.Visible = false;
    manageLFrame.Visible = false;
    categoryFrame.Visible = true;

    local warehouseInfo: _warehouseInfo = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetWarehouseInfo', warehouse);

    if not warehouseInfo then return; end;

    ownerLabel.Text = 'Owner: '.. (warehouseInfo.Owner or '[VACANT]');
    locationLabel.Text = 'Location: '..(warehouseInfo.Location or '');
    capacityLabel.Text = 'Capacity: '..warehouseInfo.Capacity;

    local owner = false;

    if warehouseInfo.Owner == localPlayer.Name then
        owner = true;
    end


    warehouseListeners:Connect(manageBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if owner then
            local managementData: managementData = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetManagementData', warehouse);

            if selectedCategoryBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedCategoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedCategoryBtn = manageBtn;
            manageSelectedTween:Play();


            if not managementData then
                return;
            end;

            manageLFrame.Visible = true;
            manageRFrame.Visible = true;
            infoFrame.Visible = false;

            moneyBarImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(managementData.Money, 1);
            suppliesBarImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(managementData.Supplies, 1);

            moneyLabel.Text = 'Money: CA$'..managementData.RawMoney;
            dealerCutLabel.Text = 'Dealer Cut: '..tostring(ReplicatedStorage.DealerCut.Value)..'%';
        else
            _G.AeroError('You are not the owner of this warehouse.');
        end;
    end)

    warehouseListeners:Connect(sellBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if owner then
            local managementData: managementData = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetManagementData', warehouse);

            if managementData.RawMoney < 30000 then
                _G.AeroError('You need a minimum of 30,000 to sell your goods.');
                return;
            end;

            NetworkController.Send('InitiateWarehouseGoodsSell', warehouse);

            self:Disable()
        else
            _G.AeroError('You are not the owner of this warehouse.');
        end;
    end)
end;

function WarehouseGUI:Enable(warehouse: Model)
    if not warehouseListeners then
        warehouseListeners = ListenerList.new();
    end;
    warehouseListeners:DisconnectAll();

    warehouseListImage.Visible = true;
    infoFrame.Visible = false;
    manageRFrame.Visible = false;
    manageLFrame.Visible = false;
    categoryFrame.Visible = false;

    local propertiesHere = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetWarehousePropertiesHere', warehouse);

    warehouseGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();

    --[[
        propertiesHere looks like this
        {
            Owner

        }
    ]]

    for _,v in warehouseListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') and v ~= buyBtn then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for _,v in propertiesHere do
        local propertyBtn = templateBtn:Clone();
        propertyBtn.Parent = warehouseListScrollingFrame;
        propertyBtn.TemplateLabel.Text = string.format("%s's warehouse", v)

        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(propertyBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(propertyBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(propertyBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        propertyBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedPropertyBtn == propertyBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        propertyBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedPropertyBtn == propertyBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);

        propertyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedPropertyBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedPropertyBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedPropertyBtn = propertyBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();
        end);
    end;

    warehouseListeners:Connect(visitBtn.MouseButton1Down, function()
        if not selectedPropertyBtn then
            _G.AeroError('You must select a property to visit.');
            return;
        end

        local propertyName = selectedPropertyBtn.TemplateLabel.Text;
        local index = string.find(propertyName, "'");
        local propertyOwner = string.sub(propertyName, 1, index - 1);

        NetworkController.Send('VisitWarehouse', warehouse, propertyOwner);
    end)

    warehouseListeners:Connect(buyBtn.MouseButton1Click, function()
        NetworkController.Send('BuyWarehouse', warehouse);
    end)
end;

function WarehouseGUI:Disable()
    if not self.IsEnabled() then return; end;
    warehouseListeners:DisconnectAll();
    closeTween:Play()
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    warehouseGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

function WarehouseGUI:Start()
    warehouseListeners = ListenerList.new();

    do
        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(infoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(infoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
        local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(infoBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

        infoBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedCategoryBtn == infoBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        infoBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedCategoryBtn == infoBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);

        infoBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if selectedCategoryBtn then
                TweenService:Create(selectedCategoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
            end

            selectedCategoryBtn = infoBtn;
            selectedTween:Play();

            manageLFrame.Visible = false;
            manageRFrame.Visible = false;
            infoFrame.Visible = true;
        end)
    end;

    do
        local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(manageBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
        local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(manageBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

        manageBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            if selectedCategoryBtn == manageBtn then return; end;
            hoverTween:Play();
        end);

        manageBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            if selectedCategoryBtn == manageBtn then return; end;
            hoverEndTween:Play();
        end);
    end;

    exitBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        self:Disable();
    end);

    local function CreateObjectValueAndMoveParent(object: Instance, parent: Instance, objectValueStorage: Instance)
        local pointer = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        pointer.Value = object;
        pointer.Parent = objectValueStorage;
        object.Parent = parent;
        return object;
    end

    NetworkController.Connect('WarehouseWaypoint', function(dealerPos, dealerTorso)
        local folders = Instance.new('Folder');
        folders.Name = 'WarehouseWaypoint';
        folders.Parent = localPlayer.Character;

        local Attachment0 = Instance.new('Attachment');
        Attachment0.Name = 'WarehouseDealerPos';
        CreateObjectValueAndMoveParent(Attachment0, dealerTorso, folders);
        Attachment0.WorldPosition = dealerPos;

        local Attachment1 = Instance.new('Attachment');
        Attachment1.Name = 'PlayerPos';
        CreateObjectValueAndMoveParent(Attachment1, localPlayer.Character.Torso, folders);

        local beam = Instance.new('Beam');
		beam.Texture = 'rbxassetid://3192533593';
		beam.TextureMode = Enum.TextureMode.Wrap;
		beam.LightInfluence = 0.5;
		beam.Attachment0 = Attachment0;
        beam.Attachment1 = Attachment1;
		beam.Parent = localPlayer.Character.Torso;
        beam.Name = 'WarehouseBeam';
        beam.Brightness = 100
        beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0));
        beam.FaceCamera = true;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('DestroyWarehouseWaypoint', function(dealerTorso)
        local folders = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('WarehouseWaypoint');
        if not folders then return; end;
        for _,v in folders:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('ObjectValue') then
                v.Value:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        folders:Destroy();

        localPlayer.Character.Torso['WarehouseBeam']:Destroy();
    end)
end;

function WarehouseGUI:Init()
    ListenerList = self.Shared.ListenerList;
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return WarehouseGUI

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local function UpdateAmmoLabel()
    ammoLabel.Text = ammo .. ' / ' .. reserveAmmo;
end;

local fireMode;

local function UpdateStateLabel(wep)
	titleLabel.Text = wep .. " [" .. string.upper(fireMode) .. "]"
end

local WeaponGUI = {};

WeaponGUI.MobileCrosshair = mobileCrosshair;

function WeaponGUI:Enable(gunName, ammo, reserveAmmo, prefix, fireMode)
    titleLabel.Text = gunName .. " [" .. string.upper(fireMode) .. "]";
    prefixLabel.Text = prefix;
    ammoLabel.Position = UDim2.fromOffset((prefixLabel.TextBounds.X + 3) / UIScale.Scale, ammoLabel.Position.Y.Offset);
    self.SetAmmo(ammo);
	self.SetReserveAmmo(reserveAmmo);
	self.SetFireMode(fireMode, gunName)
    weaponGUI.Enabled = true;
end;

function WeaponGUI.SetAmmo(ammo_)
    ammo = ammo_;
    UpdateAmmoLabel();
end;

function WeaponGUI.SetFireMode(fireMode_, wep)
	fireMode = fireMode_;
	UpdateStateLabel(wep);
end;

function WeaponGUI.SetReserveAmmo(reserveAmmo_)
    reserveAmmo = reserveAmmo_;
    UpdateAmmoLabel();
end;

    weaponGUI.Enabled = false;
end;

end;

end;

return WeaponGUI;

-- Yes No PromptGUI
-- Khizzer
-- November 20, 2021

--[[ How to use:

YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt('Title', 'Description', yesCallback, noCallback)

]]

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local playerGui = localPlayer.PlayerGui;
local YesNoPromptGui = playerGui:WaitForChild('YesNoPromptGUI');
local mainFrame = YesNoPromptGui.MainFrame;
local topBarFrame = mainFrame.TopBarFrame;
local titleLabel = topBarFrame.TitleLabel;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local textFrame = bodyFrame.TextFrame;
local descriptionLabel = textFrame.DescriptionLabel;
local BtnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local yesBtn = BtnsFrame.YesBtn;
local NetworkController;
local noBtn = BtnsFrame.NoBtn;


local ALPHA_TESTER_MESSAGE = "Welcome to Vancouver V2. By pressing yes, you agree to follow all rules in the desciption and regulations set forth by the moderation team."

local Functions

local CarSpawnerController

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);

local yesBtnConnection;
local noBtnConnection;

local DeveloperCheck;


local YesNoPromptGUI = {}

function YesNoPromptGUI:CreatePrompt(title: string, description: string, yesCallback, noCallback)
	assert(typeof(yesCallback) == "function", 'Prompt with title '..title.. ' has no "yes" callback')
	assert(typeof(noCallback) == "function", 'Prompt with title '..title.. ' has no "no" callback')

--[[ 	local Blur = Functions:Create'BlurEffect' {
		Enabled = true;
		Size = 0;
		Parent = game.Lighting;
	} ]]

	local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
	local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

	openTween:Play();
	--TweenService:Create(Blur, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = 12}):Play()
	openTween.Completed:Wait();


	titleLabel.Text = title;
	descriptionLabel.Text = description;

	yesBtnConnection = yesBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		yesCallback();
		closeTween:Play();
--[[ 		local closeBlurTween = TweenService:Create(Blur, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = 12})
		closeBlurTween:Play();
		closeBlurTween.Completed:Wait();
		Blur:Destroy(); ]]
		yesBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		yesBtnConnection = nil;
		noBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		noBtnConnection = nil;
	end)

	noBtnConnection = noBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		noCallback();
		closeTween:Play();
--[[ 		local closeBlurTween = TweenService:Create(Blur, TWEEN_INFO, {Size = 12})
		closeBlurTween:Play();
		closeBlurTween.Completed:Wait();
		Blur:Destroy(); ]]
		yesBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		yesBtnConnection = nil;
		noBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		noBtnConnection = nil;
	end)
end;

function YesNoPromptGUI:ForceClose()
	if yesBtnConnection then
		yesBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		yesBtnConnection = nil;
	end;
	if noBtnConnection then
		noBtnConnection:Disconnect();
		noBtnConnection = nil;
	end;
	local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});
	closeTween:Play();
	closeTween.Completed:Wait();
	closeTween:Destroy();
end;

function YesNoPromptGUI:Start()
--[[ 	if not DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) then
		task.wait(3)
		self:CreatePrompt('Alpha Testing', ALPHA_TESTER_MESSAGE,
			function()

			end,
			function()

			end
		)
	end; ]]
end;

function YesNoPromptGUI:Init()
	DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
	Functions = self.Shared.Functions;
	CarSpawnerController = self.Controllers.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerController;
	local GangGUI = self.Controllers.UI.GangGUI;

	NetworkController.Connect('OfficerTrunkSearch', function(suspect)
		self:CreatePrompt('Override Trunk Search', `You are attempting to get permission to search {suspect.Name}'s car. Click yes to override their permission or no to cancel the search.`,
		function()
			self.Controllers.UI.ToolContainerGUI.ConsentSignal:Fire(true);
		end,
		function()

		end)

	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('SuspectTrunkSearch', function(officer)
		self:CreatePrompt('Trunk Search', `{officer.Name} is trying to search your car. Do you wish to give them permission?`,
		function()
			NetworkController.Send('ConsentTrunkSearch', officer , true);
		end,
		function()

		end)
	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('PromptYesNo', function(...)
		local Args = {...}
		if Args[1] and Args[2] then
			self:CreatePrompt(Args[1], Args[2], Args[3] or function() end, Args[4] or function() end)
		end
	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('PromptCitationPayOff', function(...)
		local Args = {...}
		if Args[1] and Args[2] then
			self:CreatePrompt(Args[1], Args[2], function() NetworkController.Send('CitationPay', true) end, function() NetworkController.Send('CitationPay', false) end)
		end
	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('PromptCarPayOff', function(...)
		local Args = {...}
		if Args[1] and Args[2] and Args[3] then
			self:CreatePrompt(Args[1], Args[2], function() CarSpawnerController.PayOffCar(Args[3]) end, function() end)
		end
	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('InviteToGang', function(leader, gangName)
		self:CreatePrompt('Invite to Gang',
		leader..' has invited you to join the '..gangName..' gang.',
		function()
			NetworkController.Send('AcceptGangInvite', gangName);
			GangGUI.CreateBtn.Visible = false;
		end,
		function()
			NetworkController.Send('DeclineGangInvite', gangName);
		end)
	end)
end;


return YesNoPromptGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UserInput.lua ---

--[[
    UserInput (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- User Input
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- January 2, 2018

--[[
	
	UserInput simply encapsulates all user input modules.
	
	UserInput.Preferred
		- Keyboard
		- Mouse
		- Gamepad
		- Touch
	
	UserInput:Get(inputModuleName)
	UserInput:GetPreferred()

	UserInput.PreferredChanged(preferred)
	
	
	Example:
	
	local keyboard = userInput:Get("Keyboard")
	keyboard.KeyDown:Connect(function(key) end)
	
--]]



local UserInput = {}

UserInput.HideMouse = false

UserInput.Preferred = {
	Keyboard = 0;
	Mouse = 1;
	Gamepad = 2;
	Touch = 3;
}
UserInput._preferred = nil

local modules = {}
local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")


function UserInput:Get(moduleName)
	return modules[moduleName]
end


function UserInput:Init()

	for _,obj in ipairs(script:GetChildren()) do
		if (obj:IsA("ModuleScript")) then
			local module = require(obj)
			self:WrapModule(module)
			modules[obj.Name] = module
		end
	end
	
	local function SetMouseIconEnabled(enabled)
		if (self.HideMouse) then
			userInput.MouseIconEnabled = enabled
		end
	end

	local function ChangePreferred(newPreferred)
		if (self._preferred ~= newPreferred) then
			self._preferred = newPreferred
			self.PreferredChanged:Fire(newPreferred)
			if (newPreferred == self.Preferred.Mouse or newPreferred == self.Preferred.Keyboard) then
				SetMouseIconEnabled(true)
			else
				SetMouseIconEnabled(false)
			end
		end
	end

	local function LastInputTypeChanged(lastInputType)
		if (lastInputType.Name:match("^Mouse")) then
			ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Mouse)
		elseif (lastInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard or lastInputType == Enum.UserInputType.TextInput) then
			ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Keyboard)
		elseif (lastInputType.Name:match("^Gamepad")) then
			ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Gamepad)
		elseif (lastInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
			ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Touch)
		end
	end
	userInput.LastInputTypeChanged:Connect(LastInputTypeChanged)
	self.PreferredChanged = self.Shared.Signal.new()

	if (game:GetService("GuiService"):IsTenFootInterface()) then
		ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Gamepad)
	elseif (userInput.TouchEnabled) then
		ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Touch)
	else
		ChangePreferred(self.Preferred.Keyboard)
	end

end


function UserInput:GetPreferred()
	return self._preferred
end


return UserInput

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UserInput_contents/Gamepad.lua ---

--[[
    Gamepad (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UserInput
    Parent: UserInput
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Gamepad
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- December 28, 2017

--[[
	
	gamepad = Gamepad.new(gamepadUserInputType)
	
	Boolean      gamepad:IsDown(keyCode)
	Boolean      gamepad:IsConnected()
	InputObject  gamepad:GetState(keyCode)
	Void         gamepad:SetMotor(motor, value)
	Void         gamepad:StopMotor(motor)
	Void         gamepad:StopAllMotors()
	Boolean      gamepad:IsMotorSupported(motor)
	Boolean      gamepad:IsVibrationSupported()
	Float        gamepad:GetMotorValue(motor)
	Float        gamepad:ApplyDeadzone(value, deadzoneThreshold)
	
	gamepad.ButtonDown(keyCode)
	gamepad.ButtonUp(keyCode)
	gamepad.Changed(keyCode, input)
	gamepad.Connected()
	gamepad.Disconnected()
	
--]]



local Gamepad = {}
Gamepad.__index = Gamepad

local gamepadsByInputType = {}

local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local hapticService = game:GetService("HapticService")
local abs = math.abs

local InverseLerp


function Gamepad.new(gamepad)
	
	if (gamepadsByInputType[gamepad]) then
		return gamepadsByInputType[gamepad]
	end
	
	local self = setmetatable({
		_gamepadInput = gamepad;
		_state = {};
		_isConnected = false;
	}, Gamepad)
	
	self.ButtonDown   = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.ButtonUp     = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.Changed      = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.Connected    = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.Disconnected = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	
	self._listeners = self.Shared.ListenerList.new()
	
	if (userInput:GetGamepadConnected(gamepad)) then
		self._isConnected = true
		self:ConnectAll()
	end
	
	-- Connected:
	userInput.GamepadConnected:Connect(function(gamepadNum)
		if (gamepadNum == gamepad) then
			self._isConnected = true
			self:ConnectAll()
			self.Connected:Fire()
		end
	end)
	
	-- Disconnected:
	userInput.GamepadDisconnected:Connect(function(gamepadNum)
		if (gamepadNum == gamepad) then
			self._isConnected = false
			self:DisconnectAll()
			self.Disconnected:Fire()
		end
	end)
	
	-- Map InputObject states to corresponding KeyCodes:
	for _,input in ipairs(userInput:GetGamepadState(gamepad)) do
		self._state[input.KeyCode] = input
	end
	
	gamepadsByInputType[gamepad] = self
	
	return self
	
end


function Gamepad:ConnectAll()
	
	-- Input Began:
	self._listeners:Connect(userInput.InputBegan, function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		if (input.UserInputType == self._gamepadInput) then
			self.ButtonDown:Fire(input.KeyCode)
		end
	end)
	
	-- Input Ended:
	self._listeners:Connect(userInput.InputEnded, function(input, _processed)
		if (input.UserInputType == self._gamepadInput) then
			self.ButtonUp:Fire(input.KeyCode)
		end
	end)
	
	-- Input Changed:
	self._listeners:Connect(userInput.InputChanged, function(input, _processed)
		if (input.UserInputType == self._gamepadInput) then
			self.Changed:Fire(input.KeyCode, input)
		end
	end)
	
end


function Gamepad:DisconnectAll()
	self._listeners:DisconnectAll()
end


function Gamepad:IsDown(keyCode)
	return userInput:IsGamepadButtonDown(self._gamepadInput, keyCode)
end


function Gamepad:IsConnected()
	return self._isConnected
end


function Gamepad:GetState(keyCode)
	return self._state[keyCode]
end


function Gamepad:SetMotor(motor, value)
	hapticService:SetMotor(self._gamepadInput, motor, value)
end


function Gamepad:IsMotorSupported(motor)
	return hapticService:IsMotorSupported(self._gamepadInput, motor)
end


function Gamepad:IsVibrationSupported()
	return hapticService:IsVibrationSupported(self._gamepadInput)
end


function Gamepad:StopMotor(motor)
	self:SetMotor(motor, 0)
end


function Gamepad:GetMotorValue(motor)
	return hapticService:GetMotor(self._gamepadInput, motor)
end


function Gamepad:StopAllMotors()
	for _,motor in ipairs(Enum.VibrationMotor:GetEnumItems()) do
		self:StopMotor(motor)
	end
end


function Gamepad:ApplyDeadzone(value, deadzoneThreshold)
	if (abs(value) < deadzoneThreshold) then
		return 0
	else
		return InverseLerp(deadzoneThreshold, 1, abs(value)) * (value > 0 and 1 or -1)
	end
end


function Gamepad:Start()
	
end


function Gamepad:Init()
	InverseLerp = self.Shared.NumberUtil.InverseLerp
end


return Gamepad

--[[
    Keyboard (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UserInput
    Parent: UserInput
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56

-- Keyboard
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- December 28, 2017

--[[
	
	Boolean   Keyboard:IsDown(keyCode)
	Boolean   Keyboard:AreAllDown(keyCodes...)
	Boolean   Keyboard:AreAnyDown(keyCodes...)
	
	Keyboard.KeyDown(keyCode)
	Keyboard.KeyUp(keyCode)
	
--]]



local Keyboard = {}

local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")


function Keyboard:IsDown(keyCode)
	return userInput:IsKeyDown(keyCode)
end


function Keyboard:AreAllDown(...)
	for _,keyCode in pairs{...} do
		if (not userInput:IsKeyDown(keyCode)) then
			return false
		end
	end
	return true
end


function Keyboard:AreAnyDown(...)
	for _,keyCode in pairs{...} do
		if (userInput:IsKeyDown(keyCode)) then
			return true
		end
	end
	return false
end


function Keyboard:Start()
	
end


function Keyboard:Init()
	
	self.KeyDown = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.KeyUp = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	
	userInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
			self.KeyDown:Fire(input.KeyCode)
		end
	end)
	
	userInput.InputEnded:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
			self.KeyUp:Fire(input.KeyCode)
		end
	end)
	
end


return Keyboard

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UserInput_contents/Mobile.lua ---

--[[
    Mobile (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UserInput
    Parent: UserInput
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Mobile
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- December 28, 2017

--[[

	Mobile:GetDeviceAcceleration()
	Mobile:GetDeviceGravity()
	Mobile:GetDeviceRotation()
	
	Mobile.TouchStarted(position)
	Mobile.TouchEnded(position)
	Mobile.TouchMoved(position, delta)
	Mobile.TouchTapInWorld(position)
	Mobile.TouchPinch(touchPositions, scale, velocity, state)
	Mobile.TouchLongPress(touchPositions, state)
	Mobile.TouchPan(touchPositions, totalTranslation, velocity, state)
	Mobile.TouchRotate(touchPositions, rotation, velocity, state)
	Mobile.TouchSwipe(swipeDirection, numberOfTouches)
	Mobile.TouchTap(touchPositions)
	Mobile.DeviceAccelerationChanged(acceleration)
	Mobile.DeviceGravityChanged(gravity)
	Mobile.DeviceRotationChanged(rotation, cframe)
	
--]]



local Mobile = {}

local RAY_DISTANCE = 1000

local workspace = workspace

local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera


function Mobile:GetRay(position)
	local viewportMouseRay = cam:ViewportPointToRay(position.X, position.Y)
	return Ray.new(viewportMouseRay.Origin, viewportMouseRay.Direction * RAY_DISTANCE)
end


function Mobile:Cast(position, ignoreDescendantsInstance, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mobile:Cast() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRay(self:GetRay(position), ignoreDescendantsInstance, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
end


function Mobile:CastWithIgnoreList(position, ignoreDescendantsTable, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mobile:CastWithIgnoreList() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(self:GetRay(position), ignoreDescendantsTable, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
end


function Mobile:CastWithWhitelist(position, whitelistDescendantsTable, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mobile:CastWithWhitelist() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRayWithWhitelist(self:GetRay(position), whitelistDescendantsTable, ignoreWater)
end


function Mobile:Raycast(raycastParams, distance)
	local mousePos = userInput:GetMouseLocation()
	local viewportMouseRay = cam:ViewportPointToRay(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y)
	return workspace:Raycast(viewportMouseRay.Origin, viewportMouseRay.Direction * (distance or RAY_DISTANCE), raycastParams)
end


function Mobile:Init()
	
	self.TouchStarted = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchEnded = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchMoved = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchTapInWorld = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchPinch = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchLongPress = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchPan = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchRotate = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchSwipe = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.TouchTap = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	
	userInput.TouchStarted:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchStarted:Fire(input.Position)
	end)
	
	userInput.TouchEnded:Connect(function(input, _processed)
		self.TouchEnded:Fire(input.Position)
	end)
	
	userInput.TouchMoved:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchMoved:Fire(input.Position, input.Delta)
	end)
	
	userInput.TouchTapInWorld:Connect(function(position, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchTapInWorld:Fire(position)
	end)
	
	userInput.TouchPinch:Connect(function(touchPositions, scale, velocity, state, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchPinch:Fire(touchPositions, scale, velocity, state)
	end)

	userInput.TouchLongPress:Connect(function(touchPositions, state, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchLongPress:Fire(touchPositions, state)
	end)

	userInput.TouchPan:Connect(function(touchPositions, totalTranslation, velocity, state, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchPan:Fire(touchPositions, totalTranslation, velocity, state)
	end)

	userInput.TouchRotate:Connect(function(touchPositions, rotation, velocity, state, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchRotate:Fire(touchPositions, rotation, velocity, state)
	end)

	userInput.TouchSwipe:Connect(function(swipeDirection, numberOfTouches, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchSwipe:Fire(swipeDirection, numberOfTouches)
	end)

	userInput.TouchTap:Connect(function(touchPositions, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		self.TouchTap:Fire(touchPositions)
	end)

	self.GetDeviceAcceleration = userInput.GetDeviceAcceleration
	self.GetDeviceGravity = userInput.GetDeviceGravity
	self.GetDeviceRotation = userInput.GetDeviceRotation
	self.DeviceAccelerationChanged = userInput.DeviceAccelerationChanged
	self.DeviceGravityChanged = userInput.DeviceGravityChanged
	self.DeviceRotationChanged = userInput.DeviceRotationChanged
	
end


return Mobile

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/UserInput_contents/Mouse.lua ---

--[[
    Mouse (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → UserInput
    Parent: UserInput
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Mouse
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- December 28, 2017

--[[
	
	Vector2        Mouse:GetPosition()
	Vector2        Mouse:GetDelta()
	Void           Mouse:Lock()
	Void           Mouse:LockCenter()
	Void           Mouse:Unlock()
	Ray            Mouse:GetRay(distance)
	Ray            Mouse:GetRayFromXY(x, y)
	Void           Mouse:SetMouseIcon(iconId)
	Void           Mouse:SetMouseIconEnabled(isEnabled)
	Boolean        Mouse:IsMouseIconEnabled()
	Boolean        Mouse:IsButtonPressed(mouseButton)
	RaycastResult  Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams [, distance = 1000])
	
	Mouse.LeftDown()
	Mouse.LeftUp()
	Mouse.RightDown()
	Mouse.RightUp()
	Mouse.MiddleDown()
	Mouse.MiddleUp()
	Mouse.Moved()
	Mouse.Scrolled(amount)
	
--]]



local Mouse = {}

local RAY_DISTANCE = 1000

local playerMouse = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera

local workspace = workspace


function Mouse:GetPosition()
	return userInput:GetMouseLocation()
end


function Mouse:GetDelta()
	return userInput:GetMouseDelta()
end


function Mouse:Lock()
	userInput.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCurrentPosition
end


function Mouse:LockCenter()
	userInput.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter
end


function Mouse:Unlock()
	userInput.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default
end


function Mouse:SetMouseIcon(iconId)
	playerMouse.Icon = (iconId and ("rbxassetid://" .. iconId) or "")
end


function Mouse:SetMouseIconEnabled(enabled)
	userInput.MouseIconEnabled = enabled
end


function Mouse:IsMouseIconEnabled()
	return userInput.MouseIconEnabled
end


function Mouse:IsButtonPressed(mouseButton)
	return userInput:IsMouseButtonPressed(mouseButton)
end


function Mouse:GetRay(distance)
	local mousePos = userInput:GetMouseLocation()
	local viewportMouseRay = cam:ViewportPointToRay(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y)
	return Ray.new(viewportMouseRay.Origin, viewportMouseRay.Direction * distance)
end


function Mouse:GetRayFromXY(x, y)
	local viewportMouseRay = cam:ViewportPointToRay(x, y)
	return Ray.new(viewportMouseRay.Origin, viewportMouseRay.Direction)
end


function Mouse:Cast(ignoreDescendantsInstance, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mouse:Cast() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRay(self:GetRay(RAY_DISTANCE), ignoreDescendantsInstance, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
end


function Mouse:CastWithIgnoreList(ignoreDescendantsTable, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mouse:CastWithIgnoreList() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(self:GetRay(RAY_DISTANCE), ignoreDescendantsTable, terrainCellsAreCubes, ignoreWater)
end


function Mouse:CastWithWhitelist(whitelistDescendantsTable, ignoreWater)
	warn("Mouse:CastWithWhitelist() is deprecated; please use Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams) instead")
	return workspace:FindPartOnRayWithWhitelist(self:GetRay(RAY_DISTANCE), whitelistDescendantsTable, ignoreWater)
end


function Mouse:Raycast(raycastParams, distance)
	local mousePos = userInput:GetMouseLocation()
	local viewportMouseRay = cam:ViewportPointToRay(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y)
	return workspace:Raycast(viewportMouseRay.Origin, viewportMouseRay.Direction * (distance or RAY_DISTANCE), raycastParams)
end


function Mouse:Init()
	
	self.LeftDown   = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.LeftUp     = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.RightDown  = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.RightUp    = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.MiddleDown = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.MiddleUp   = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.Moved      = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self.Scrolled   = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	
	userInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (processed) then return end
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1) then
			self.LeftDown:Fire()
		elseif (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then
			self.RightDown:Fire()
		elseif (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton3) then
			self.MiddleDown:Fire()
		end
	end)
	
	userInput.InputEnded:Connect(function(input, _processed)
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1) then
			self.LeftUp:Fire()
		elseif (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then
			self.RightUp:Fire()
		elseif (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton3) then
			self.MiddleUp:Fire()
		end
	end)
	
	userInput.InputChanged:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement) then
			self.Moved:Fire()
		elseif (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseWheel) then
			if (not processed) then
				self.Scrolled:Fire(input.Position.Z)
			end
		end
	end)
	
end


return Mouse

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/WeaponDealer/WeaponDealerController.lua ---

--[[
    WeaponDealerController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → WeaponDealer
    Parent: WeaponDealer
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local WeaponDealerGUI;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local rootPart;

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local currentInteractedDealer;

local WeaponDealerController = {};

function WeaponDealerController:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

function WeaponDealerController.CheckDistanceFromDealer(interactionPart)
    local dealerPosition = interactionPart.Position;
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        while true do
            if (dealerPosition - rootPart.Position).Magnitude > 6 then break; end;
            if not WeaponDealerGUI.IsEnabled() then
                break;
            end;
            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
        if WeaponDealerGUI.IsEnabled() then
            WeaponDealerGUI.Disable();
        end;
    end)();
end;

function WeaponDealerController:ToggleDealerGUI(weaponDealer)
    currentInteractedDealer = weaponDealer;
    local legal = weaponDealer:GetAttribute('Legal');
    if WeaponDealerGUI.IsEnabled() then
        WeaponDealerGUI.Disable();
    else
        WeaponDealerGUI.Enable(legal);
    end;
    self.CheckDistanceFromDealer(weaponDealer);
end;

function WeaponDealerController:Start()
end;

function WeaponDealerController:Init()
    WeaponDealerGUI = self.Controllers.WeaponDealer.WeaponDealerGUI;
end;

return WeaponDealerController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/WeaponDealer/WeaponDealerGUI.lua ---

--[[
    WeaponDealerGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → WeaponDealer
    Parent: WeaponDealer
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Gun DealerGUI
-- Khizzer
-- June 23, 2021


local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local dummyTools = ReplicatedStorage.dummyTools

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);

local CAMERA_OFFSET = CFrame.new(1, 1.5, 0);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local gunDealerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('WeaponDealerGUI');
local mainFrame = gunDealerGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local buyBtn = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local refillBtn = btnsFrame.RefillBtn;

local weaponsListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.WeaponsListImage.WeaponsListScrollingFrame;

local detailsFrame = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local weaponViewportFrame = detailsFrame.WeaponViewportFrame;
local statsFrame = detailsFrame.StatsFrame;

local priceLabel = statsFrame.PriceLabel;
local ammoLabel = statsFrame.AmmoLabel;
local damageLabel = statsFrame.DmgLabel;
local refillPriceLabel = statsFrame.RefillPriceLabel;

local components = gunDealerGUI.Components;
local weaponBtnPrefab = components.WeaponBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local selectedBtn;

local viewportCamera;
local viewportWeaponModel;

local buyConnection;
local refillBtnConnection;

local NetworkController;
local Notification;

local function CreateCamera()
    local camera = Instance.new('Camera');
    return camera;
end;

local function hasPAL()
    return localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("PAL")
        or localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("PS | PAL")
        or localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("PAL")
        or localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("PS | PAL")
end

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    local uiListLayout = weaponsListScrollingFrame.UIGridLayout;
    local absoluteContentSize = uiListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize;
    -- weaponsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#weaponsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
    weaponsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, absoluteContentSize.Y);
end;

local function SetupCameraAndGetViewportWeapon(camera, name)
    local weapon: Model = game.ReplicatedStorage.dummyTools[name]:Clone();

    local cframe, size = weapon:GetBoundingBox();

    local rot = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0), math.rad(90), 0);

    size = rot:VectorToObjectSpace(size);

    local frameSize = 128;

    local sizeX, sizeY, sizeZ = math.abs(size.X), math.abs(size.Y), math.abs(size.Z);

    local h = (sizeY / math.tan(math.rad(camera.FieldOfView / 2)) * 2) + (sizeZ / 2);

    local frameX = (sizeX > sizeY and frameSize or (frameSize * (sizeX / sizeY)));
    local frameY = (sizeY > sizeX and frameSize or (frameSize * (sizeY / sizeX)));

    weaponViewportFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, frameX, 0, frameY);
    camera.CFrame = cframe * rot * CFrame.new(0, 0, h);

--    camera.CFrame = CFrame.new((weapon.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CAMERA_OFFSET).Position, weapon.PrimaryPart.Position);

    return weapon;
end;

local WeaponDealerGUI = {}

function WeaponDealerGUI.IsEnabled()
    return gunDealerGUI.Enabled;
end;

function WeaponDealerGUI.Enable(dealerLegal)
    viewportCamera = CreateCamera();
    weaponViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = viewportCamera;

    refillBtnConnection = refillBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        NetworkController.Send('REFILL_DEALER');
    end);

    for i, v in next, dummyTools:GetChildren() do
        if (dealerLegal == true and v:GetAttribute('Legal') == true) or (dealerLegal == false) then
            if not dealerLegal and v.Name == "PAL" then continue end

            local itemName = v.Name;
            local damage = v:GetAttribute('Damage') or v:GetAttribute('BaseDamage')
            local clipSize = v:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo');
            local maxReserveAmmo = v:GetAttribute('MaxReserveAmmo');
            local price = v:GetAttribute('Price');

            local itemType;

            if damage and clipSize then
                itemType = 'GUN';
            elseif damage and not clipSize then
                itemType = 'MELEE';
                damage = ('%d-%d'):format(v:GetAttribute('BaseDamage'), v:GetAttribute('CritDamage'));
            else
                itemType = 'MISC';
            end;

            local itemBtn = weaponBtnPrefab:Clone();
            itemBtn.WeaponLabel.Text = itemName;
            itemBtn.Parent = weaponsListScrollingFrame;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(itemBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            local function ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn()
                local hasBoughtGun = localPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(itemName) or localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(itemName)
                if hasBoughtGun and itemType == 'GUN' then
                    refillBtn.Visible = true;
                    buyBtn.Visible = false;
                else
                    buyBtn.Visible = true;
                    refillBtn.Visible = false;
                end;
            end;


            itemBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            itemBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn == itemBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            itemBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn then
                    TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                end

                selectedBtn = itemBtn;
                selectedTween:Play();

                priceLabel.Text = 'Price: $'..price;
                --buyBtn.Visible = true;

                if itemType == 'GUN' then
                    damageLabel.Text = 'Damage: '..damage;
                    ammoLabel.Text = 'Clip Size: '..clipSize;
                    refillPriceLabel.Text = 'Refill Price: '..maxReserveAmmo;
                elseif itemType == 'MELEE' then
                    damageLabel.Text = 'Damage: '..damage;
                    ammoLabel.Text = '';
                    refillPriceLabel.Text = '';
                else
                    damageLabel.Text = '';
                    ammoLabel.Text = '';
                    refillPriceLabel.Text = '';
                end;

                if viewportWeaponModel then
                    viewportWeaponModel:Destroy();
                end;

                viewportWeaponModel = SetupCameraAndGetViewportWeapon(viewportCamera, itemName);
                viewportWeaponModel.Parent = weaponViewportFrame;

                ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn();

                if buyConnection then
                    buyConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if itemType == 'GUN' and dealerLegal and not hasPAL() then
                        Notification(
                            "Purchase Refused",
                            `You must have a PAL to buy from an authorized dealer.`,
                            nil,
                            'Red'
                        )
                        return
                    end

                    NetworkController.Send('DEALER_PURCHASE', itemName);
                    ReloadBuyAndRefillBtn()
                    WeaponDealerGUI.Disable()
                end);
            end);
        end;
    end;

    UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize();

    gunDealerGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play()
end;

function WeaponDealerGUI.Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    gunDealerGUI.Enabled = false;


    buyBtn.Visible = false;
    refillBtn.Visible = false;

    priceLabel.Text = '';
    damageLabel.Text = '';
    ammoLabel.Text = '';
    refillPriceLabel.Text = '';

    weaponViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = nil;
    if viewportCamera then
        viewportCamera:Destroy();
    end;
    if viewportWeaponModel then
        viewportWeaponModel:Destroy();
    end;
    if buyConnection then
        buyConnection:Disconnect();
        buyConnection = nil;
    end;

    if refillBtnConnection then
        refillBtnConnection:Disconnect();
        refillBtnConnection = nil;
    end;

    for i, v in next, weaponsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
end;

function WeaponDealerGUI:Start()
    exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(self.Disable)
end;

function WeaponDealerGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController
    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new
end


return WeaponDealerGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/WindController.lua ---

--[[
    WindController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local WindController = {};

local gustCycleDelay = 30  -- Max duration between gust cycles in seconds
local gustCycleDuration = 10  -- Duration of each gust cycle in seconds

function WindController:Start()

    -- During each gust cycle, a portion of "gust" will be added to "baseWind" in a ramped fashion
    local baseWind = Vector3.new(5, 0, 2)  -- Base wind speed and direction
    local gust = Vector3.new(25, 0, 10)  -- Gust speed and direction
    local gustIntervals = 100  -- Number of iterations used to calculate each gust interval
    local dg = gustCycleDuration / gustIntervals
    local dgf = dg / gustCycleDuration

    -- Set global wind to base wind initially
    workspace.GlobalWind = baseWind

    -- Wait delay amount before starting gusts
    task.wait(gustCycleDelay)

    while true do
        for i = 1, gustIntervals do
            local f = math.sin(math.pi * dgf * i)  -- Use sin() function to ramp gust
            workspace.GlobalWind = baseWind + f * gust  -- Set global wind to base wind + gust
            task.wait(dg)
        end
        workspace.GlobalWind = baseWind  -- Reset global wind to base wind at end of gust cycle
        task.wait(math.random() * gustCycleDelay)  -- Wait a random fraction of delay before next gust cycle
    end
end;

return WindController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Fusion/Core.lua ---

--[[
    Core (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Fusion
    Parent: Fusion
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
--!strict

--[[
	The entry point for the Fusion library.
]]

local PubTypes = require(script.PubTypes)
local restrictRead = require(script.Utility.restrictRead)

local Fusion = restrictRead("Fusion", {
	version = {major = 0, minor = 3, isRelease = false},

	New = require(script.Instances.New),
	Hydrate = require(script.Instances.Hydrate),
	Ref = require(script.Instances.Ref),
	Out = require(script.Instances.Out),
	Cleanup = require(script.Instances.Cleanup),
	Children = require(script.Instances.Children),
	OnEvent = require(script.Instances.OnEvent),
	OnChange = require(script.Instances.OnChange),
	Attribute = require(script.Instances.Attribute),
	AttributeChange = require(script.Instances.AttributeChange),
	AttributeOut = require(script.Instances.AttributeOut),

	Value = require(script.State.Value),
	Computed = require(script.State.Computed),
	ForPairs = require(script.State.ForPairs),
	ForKeys = require(script.State.ForKeys),
	ForValues = require(script.State.ForValues),
	Observer = require(script.State.Observer),

	Tween = require(script.Animation.Tween),
	Spring = require(script.Animation.Spring),

	cleanup = require(script.Utility.cleanup),
	doNothing = require(script.Utility.doNothing),
	peek = require(script.State.peek)
}) :: Fusion

export type StateObject<T> = PubTypes.StateObject<T>
export type CanBeState<T> = PubTypes.CanBeState<T>
export type Symbol = PubTypes.Symbol
export type Value<T> = PubTypes.Value<T>
export type Computed<T> = PubTypes.Computed<T>
export type ForPairs<KO, VO> = PubTypes.ForPairs<KO, VO>
export type ForKeys<KI, KO> = PubTypes.ForKeys<KI, KO>
export type ForValues<VI, VO> = PubTypes.ForKeys<VI, VO>
export type Observer = PubTypes.Observer
export type Tween<T> = PubTypes.Tween<T>
export type Spring<T> = PubTypes.Spring<T>
export type Use = PubTypes.Use

type Fusion = {
	version: PubTypes.Version,

	New: (className: string) -> ((propertyTable: PubTypes.PropertyTable) -> Instance),
	Hydrate: (target: Instance) -> ((propertyTable: PubTypes.PropertyTable) -> Instance),
	Ref: PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	Cleanup: PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	Children: PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	Out: (propertyName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	OnEvent: (eventName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	OnChange: (propertyName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	Attribute: (attributeName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	AttributeChange: (attributeName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,
	AttributeOut: (attributeName: string) -> PubTypes.SpecialKey,

	Value: <T>(initialValue: T) -> Value<T>,
	Computed: <T>(callback: (Use) -> T, destructor: (T) -> ()?) -> Computed<T>,
	ForPairs: <KI, VI, KO, VO, M>(inputTable: CanBeState<{[KI]: VI}>, processor: (Use, KI, VI) -> (KO, VO, M?), destructor: (KO, VO, M?) -> ()?) -> ForPairs<KO, VO>,
	ForKeys: <KI, KO, M>(inputTable: CanBeState<{[KI]: any}>, processor: (Use, KI) -> (KO, M?), destructor: (KO, M?) -> ()?) -> ForKeys<KO, any>,
	ForValues: <VI, VO, M>(inputTable: CanBeState<{[any]: VI}>, processor: (Use, VI) -> (VO, M?), destructor: (VO, M?) -> ()?) -> ForValues<any, VO>,
	Observer: (watchedState: StateObject<any>) -> Observer,

	Tween: <T>(goalState: StateObject<T>, tweenInfo: TweenInfo?) -> Tween<T>,
	Spring: <T>(goalState: StateObject<T>, speed: CanBeState<number>?, damping: CanBeState<number>?) -> Spring<T>,

	cleanup: (...any) -> (),
	doNothing: (...any) -> (),
	peek: Use
}

return Fusion
